# physics.optics [[Back]](#toc)

### [1] [Light-propelled microparticles based on symmetry-broken refractive index profiles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14917)
*Julian Jeggle,Matthias Rüschenbaum,Adrian Paskert,Ivan Kalthoff,Elena Vinnemeier,Jesco Schönfelder,Jörg Imbrock,Cornelia Denz,Marcel Rey,Raphael Wittkowski*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种通过非对称光折射实现推进的3D可打印胶体微粒（SBRIP粒子），其内部折射率梯度提供光学对称破缺，实现基于透明度的动量传递机制，为体积极性物质和自适应非线性光学材料开辟了新途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 活性胶体微粒需要可靠的驱动机制来维持定向运动。基于光的推进特别有吸引力，因为它提供持续的能量供应并实现直接的时空控制。然而，传统系统依赖吸收或反射会产生加热和阴影效应。

Method: 本文介绍了具有对称破缺折射率分布（symmetry-broken refractive index profiles, SBRIP）的3D可打印粒子，通过非对称光折射实现直接动量传递。建立了折射推进的理论框架，并使用光线追踪和有限体积法进行数值模拟，并通过几何对称破缺粒子的实验验证了动量传递机制。

Result: SBRIP粒子实现了基于透明度的推进机制，最小化加热并减轻体相悬浮液中的阴影效应。粒子的高透明度确保了深光穿透，实现了体积极性物质（volumetric active matter）的构建。该机制在几何对称破缺的均匀折射率粒子中也得到验证。

Conclusion: 这种基于折射的推进机制为自适应非线性光学材料开辟了新途径，其中光驱动粒子重组可调制局部折射率，在光场和材料结构之间建立动态反馈回路。该方法从根本上将推进与粒子几何形状解耦，实现了独立于外部形状的光学对称破缺。

Abstract: Active colloidal microparticles require reliable actuation to sustain directed motion. Light-based propulsion is particularly attractive as it provides persistent energy supply and enables direct spatiotemporal control. Here, we introduce 3D-printable particles with symmetry-broken refractive index profiles (SBRIP particles) that achieve propulsion through direct momentum transfer from asymmetric light refraction. Internal refractive-index gradients provide optical symmetry breaking independent of external shape, fundamentally decoupling propulsion from particle geometry. Geometrically symmetry-broken particles with a homogeneous refractive index are another special case, where propulsion originates from refractive contrast at the boundary instead of within the particle. Unlike conventional systems relying on absorption or reflection, this transparency-based mechanism minimizes heating and mitigates shadowing in bulk suspensions. We present a theoretical framework for refractive propulsion as well as numerical simulations of the SBRIP particles using raytracing and the finite volume method. This is complemented by experiments, validating the momentum transfer mechanism using particles with geometric symmetry breaking. The high transparency of our particles ensures deep light penetration, enabling the realization of volumetric active matter. This opens pathways toward adaptive nonlinear optical materials where light-driven particle reorganization modulates the local refractive index, establishing a dynamic feedback loop between the optical field and the material structure.

</details>


### [2] [Toroidal Plasmonic Nanodimers for Enhanced Near-Infrared Emission in Heterostructured InP Quantum Dots](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14992)
*Arda Gulucu,Emre Ozan Polat*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 该研究通过有限时域差分模拟，探索了银环形等离子体纳米天线二聚体（Ag TPNDs）作为几何可调平台，用于增强异质结构InP量子点在近红外区域的发射性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近红外发射器在650-900 nm范围内对浑浊介质成像和传感具有重要价值，但无镉InP量子点常因非辐射途径和低效光子耦合而亮度受限。异质结构InP量子点的能带排列可能导致载流子空间分离，降低电子-空穴波函数重叠，从而影响其发射性能。

Method: 采用有限时域差分模拟方法研究银环形等离子体纳米天线二聚体，该几何结构支持强局域束缚模式并产生高强度纳米间隙热点。通过调节环形纵横比，可系统调谐天线共振频率，使其与量子点发射波段（675-845 nm）光谱匹配。

Result: 光谱匹配后实现了大的珀塞尔增强和高量子效率，表明增强的衰减速率能有效转化为辐射发射。研究还发现发射体-天线间距的纳米级变化会强烈调制辐射速率和光谱响应。

Conclusion: 环形等离子体纳米二聚体被确立为拓扑驱动平台，可用于控制近红外量子发射器的发射特性，并推动近红外纳米光子学应用的发展。

Abstract: Near-infrared (NIR) emitters operating in the 650-900 nm range are highly attractive for imaging and sensing in turbid media; however, cadmium-free InP-based quantum dots (QDs) often suffer from limited brightness due to nonradiative pathways and inefficient photon outcoupling. In particular, heterostructured InP QDs can exhibit band alignments that induce partial spatial separation of charge carriers, leading to reduced electron-hole wavefunction overlap. This modifies intrinsic recombination dynamics and enhances the sensitivity of their emission to the surrounding photonic environment. Here, we investigate silver toroidal plasmonic nanoantenna dimers (Ag TPNDs) through finite-difference-time-domain (FDTD) simulations as a geometry-tunable platform for enhancing NIR emission of heterostructured InP-based QDs. The coupled toroidal geometry supports strongly confined bonding modes that generate intense nanogap hotspots, while its resonance can be systematically tuned through the toroid aspect ratio. By spectrally aligning the antenna response with QD emission bands (675-845 nm), we achieve large Purcell enhancements together with high quantum efficiencies, demonstrating efficient conversion of enhanced decay rates into radiative emission. We further show that nanometer-scale variations in emitter-antenna separation strongly modulate the radiative rates and spectral response. These results establish toroidal plasmonic nanodimers as a topology-driven platform for controlling emission in NIR quantum emitters and for advancing NIR nanophotonic applications.

</details>


### [3] [Optical Modulation Due to Energy Exchange Between Photonic and Exciton Modes in the Intermediate Coupling Regime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15066)
*Evripidis Michail,Sander A. Mann,Kamyar Rashidi,Christoph Lambert,Vinod M. Menon,Andrea Alu,Matthew Y. Sfeir*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本研究开发了一种基于方酸染料（squaraine-dye）近红外吸收光子结构的光学调制方案，利用中间激子-光子耦合（intermediate exciton-photon coupling）实现了对光诱导响应的动态控制，为宽带近红外光信号调制提供了新途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 有机光电器件作为光学调制器（optical modulators）的应用受到近红外（NIR）区域低吸收、响应时间慢和非线性效应弱的限制。本研究旨在解决这些限制，开发适用于下一代光电子学（optoelectronics）的主动可调光子器件。

Method: 研究采用基于近红外吸收方酸染料的光子结构，利用中间激子-光子耦合方案。通过能量-动量分辨泵浦-探测光谱（energy-momentum resolved pump-probe spectroscopy）测量光学响应，并使用时间耦合模式理论（temporal coupled-mode theory）分析数据。

Result: 研究发现系统光学响应的符号和大小强烈依赖于激子模式与光子模式之间的能量失谐（energy detuning）。在接近共振时，强耦合与弱耦合之间的交叉区域出现了明显的能量交换过程（energy exchange process）。

Conclusion: 该方案实现了对光诱导响应的动态控制，为扩展到近红外光谱区域的宽带光信号调制（broadband optical signal modulation）提供了可行途径，克服了传统有机光电器件在光学调制应用中的局限性。

Abstract: Actively tunable photonic devices are vital for next-generation optoelectronics requiring rapid switching and high bandwidth. Although organic optoelectronic devices have found wide application, their use as optical modulators has been limited by low absorption in the critical near-infrared (NIR) region, slow response time, and weak nonlinearities. To address these limitations, we developed a scheme based on intermediate exciton-photon coupling in a NIR absorbing squaraine-dye based photonic structure. Using energy-momentum resolved pump-probe spectroscopy, we show that the sign and magnitude of the optical response of our system depends strongly on the energy detuning between the excitonic and photonic modes. These data are analyzed using temporal coupled-mode theory to show that near resonance, a distinct energy exchange process emerges in the cross-over regime between strong and weak light-matter coupling. This effect enables dynamical control over the photoinduced response, providing a pathway for broadband optical signal modulation extending into the NIR spectral region.

</details>

# physics.gen-ph [[Back]](#toc)

### [4] [On Computational CUDA Studies of Black Hole Shadows](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14213)
*S. E. Baddis,A. Belhaj,H. Belmahi,S. E. Ennadifi,M. Jemri*

Main category: physics.gen-ph

TL;DR: 该研究结合CUDA高性能数值计算与Hamilton-Jacobi形式理论，分析了含全局单极子的旋转带电Euler-Heisenberg黑洞的阴影特性及其能量发射率，并利用事件视界望远镜观测数据对黑洞参数设定了严格约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探索在全局单极子（global monopole）存在情况下，旋转带电Euler-Heisenberg黑洞的阴影特性及其能量发射率，并将理论预测与事件视界望远镜（Event Horizon Telescope）的实际观测数据进行对比验证。

Method: 采用结合高性能CUDA数值代码与Hamilton-Jacobi形式理论（Hamilton-Jacobi formalism）的计算方法，通过变化黑洞参数来研究阴影结构和能量发射率，并利用CUDA计算框架建立参数约束。

Result: 研究发现阴影结构和能量发射率均依赖于全局单极子参数（global monopole parameter）、电荷（electric charge）和旋转参数（rotation parameter），但Euler-Heisenberg非线性参数（Euler-Heisenberg nonlinear parameter）对两者均无显著影响。

Conclusion: 通过CUDA计算框架将理论预测与事件视界望远镜观测数据相协调，为全局单极子参数、电荷和旋转参数建立了严格的约束界限，验证了理论模型与观测结果的一致性。

Abstract: Combining high-performance CUDA numerical codes with the Hamilton--Jacobi formalism, we investigate the shadows properties of rotating charged Euler--Heisenberg black holes in the presence of global monopoles. Then, we discuss the associated energy emission rate by varying the involved black hole parameters. As a result, we show that both the shadow structure and the energy emission rate depend on the global monopole parameter, the electric charge, and the rotation parameter. However, we observe that the Euler--Heisenberg nonlinear parameter does not significantly affect either the shadow or the energy emission rate. In order to reconcile the present theoretical predictions with the shadow observations reported by the Event Horizon Telescope collaboration, we employ a CUDA-based computational approach to establish strict bounds on the GM parameter, the electric charge, and the rotation parameter.

</details>

# cond-mat.supr-con [[Back]](#toc)

### [5] [$μ$SR study of time-reversal symmetry constraints and bulk superfluid response in Li$_{0.95}$FeAs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14376)
*Rustem Khasanov,Hubertus Luetkens,Nikolai D. Zhigadlo*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该研究通过零场和横向场μ子自旋旋转/弛豫（μSR）测量，证实Li₀.₉₅FeAs为体相多能隙超导体，未检测到时间反演对称性破缺，并确定了其超流密度主要由中等和小能隙的费米面贡献。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在通过μSR技术探究Li₀.₉₅FeAs超导体的基本性质，特别是验证其是否为体相超导体、是否存在时间反演对称性破缺（time-reversal-symmetry breaking），并确定其超导能隙结构。

Method: 采用高压自熔剂法生长Li₀.₉₅FeAs单晶样品，通过零场（ZF）和横向场（TF）μ子自旋旋转/弛豫（μSR）测量技术，分析超导转变温度附近的电子弛豫率变化和涡旋响应。

Result: ZF-μSR未检测到超导态中时间反演对称性破缺的证据；TF-μSR确认了样品的体相超导性，测得面内磁穿透深度λ_ab=245(15) nm，超流密度温度依赖符合有效双能隙模型，其中Δ₁=2.0(2) meV，Δ₂=0.7(2) meV。

Conclusion: Li₀.₉₅FeAs被确认为无时间反演对称性破缺的体相多能隙超导体，μSR测量显示其超流密度主要由携带中等和小能隙的费米面贡献，最大能隙的能带仅贡献约3%，解释了体相与表面敏感探针报告能隙尺度的差异。

Abstract: We report zero-field (ZF) and transverse-field (TF) muon-spin rotation/relaxation ($μ$SR) measurements on superconducting Li$_{0.95}$FeAs ($T_{\rm c}\simeq16.0$ K) grown by a high-pressure self-flux method. The ZF-$μ$SR data show no detectable change of the electronic relaxation rate on cooling through $T_{\rm c}$, providing no evidence for time-reversal-symmetry breaking in the superconducting state. TF-$μ$SR measurements reveal a well-developed vortex response with strong flux pinning and a negligible nonsuperconducting contribution, confirming that superconductivity is a bulk property of the sample. From the second moment of the internal field distribution we determine a low-temperature in-plane magnetic penetration depth $λ_{ab}= 245(15)$ nm. The temperature dependence of the normalized superfluid density is well described by an effective two-gap model with $Δ_1 = 2.0(2)$ meV and $Δ_2 = 0.7(2)$ meV. A quantitative comparison with ARPES-based band weights shows that the $μ$SR response is dominated by the Fermi-surface sheets carrying the intermediate and small superconducting gaps, whereas the band hosting the largest gap contributes only about 3\% to the total superfluid density and is therefore not resolved in the present analysis. Taken together, these results establish Li$_{0.95}$FeAs as a bulk multigap superconductor without detectable time-reversal symmetry breaking and show how $μ$SR reconciles the gap scales reported by bulk and surface-sensitive probes in this multiband system.

</details>


### [6] [Revisiting apparent ideal diamagnetism at ambient conditions in graphene-n-heptane-permalloy systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14395)
*Rajendra Dulal,Serafim Teknowijoyo,Sara Chahid,Vahan Nikoghosyan,Armen Gulian*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 先前报道的石墨烯-正庚烷-坡莫合金系统在常温下表现出的理想抗磁性（ideal diamagnetism）并非由石墨烯引起，而是由坡莫合金箔片不均匀性和实验几何结构导致的磁场重新分布所模拟的假象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在澄清先前实验中观察到的矛盾现象：石墨烯-正庚烷-坡莫合金系统在常温下表现出理想抗磁性，但同时也存在信号冻结（signal freezing）和偶尔顺磁响应（paramagnetic responses）等不一致行为。

Method: 通过对比实验方法，在不使用石墨烯的情况下进行相同测量，以确定观察到的效应是否真正源于石墨烯。实验采用亚毫高斯（sub-milligauss）级别的超低场磁测量技术。

Result: 无石墨烯的对照实验产生了类似信号，证明石墨烯并非观察效应的原因。结果表明，坡莫合金箔片（permalloy foil）的不均匀性和实验几何结构导致的磁场重新分布（magnetic field redistribution）可以模拟出理想抗磁性的表现。

Conclusion: 这些发现修正了对先前结果的解释，强调在解释超低场磁测量（ultra-low-field magnetic measurements）时需要格外谨慎，避免将系统伪影误认为材料本征特性。

Abstract: We previously reported apparent ideal diamagnetism at ambient conditions in a graphene-n-heptane-permalloy system. At the same time, the experiments revealed inconsistent behavior, including signal freezing and occasional paramagnetic responses. Further measurements performed without graphene produced similar signals, indicating that graphene is not responsible for the observed effects. The results suggest that magnetic field redistribution caused by inhomogeneities in the permalloy foil and experimental geometry can mimic ideal diamagnetism in sub-milligauss measurements. These findings revise the interpretation of our earlier results and emphasize caution in interpreting ultra-low-field magnetic measurements.

</details>


### [7] [Direct laser micromachining of superconducting terahertz Josephson plasma emitters](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14485)
*Reo Yamaguchi,Takuma Sakurai,Kazuhiro Yamaki,Akinobu Irie,Junichiro Kato,Taichiro Nishio,Shigeyuki Ishida,Hiroshi Eisaki,Manabu Tsujimoto*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于紫外激光微加工Bi-2212单晶的超导太赫兹约瑟夫森等离子体发射器快速无掩模制造方法，该方法保留了晶体内部均匀的本征约瑟夫森结堆叠，实现了稳定的太赫兹辐射。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统制造方法通常复杂且耗时，需要开发一种快速、无掩模的制造技术来制备超导太赫兹约瑟夫森等离子体发射器（JPEs），以简化制造流程并降低成本。

Method: 采用直接紫外激光微加工（direct ultraviolet laser micromachining）技术对Bi₂Sr₂CaCu₂O₈₊δ（Bi-2212）单晶进行处理，使用Ag、Cu和Cr三种电极材料进行器件制备。

Result: 所有电极器件均能产生太赫兹辐射，其中Cu电极性能与Ag相当但成本更低；光谱和偏振分析显示辐射为椭圆偏振且以几何腔共振模式为主；结构表征表明加工宽度和深度受Bi-2212各向异性热导率控制。

Conclusion: 这种直接激光微加工方法为JPEs提供了一种快速、通用的制造技术，并且广泛适用于超导电子学和太赫兹器件领域。

Abstract: We demonstrate a rapid, maskless fabrication method for superconducting terahertz Josephson plasma emitters (JPEs) based on direct ultraviolet laser micromachining of Bi$_2$Sr$_2$CaCu$_2$O$_{8+δ}$ (Bi-2212) single crystals. Although machining debris is formed near the processed regions, uniform stacks of intrinsic Josephson junctions are preserved inside the crystal, enabling stable terahertz emission. Devices fabricated with Ag, Cu, and Cr electrodes all exhibited terahertz radiation, with Cu electrodes showing performance comparable to Ag while offering a low-cost alternative. Spectroscopic and polarization analyses indicate that the emitted radiation is elliptically polarized and dominated by the geometrical cavity resonance mode. Structural and electrical characterizations reveal that the machining width and depth are not limited by the optical spot size but are governed by the anisotropic thermal conductivity of Bi-2212, consistent with a thermally dominated laser ablation process. This direct laser micromachining approach provides a fast and versatile fabrication technique for JPEs and is broadly applicable to superconducting electronics and terahertz devices.

</details>


### [8] [Wide-field magnetic imaging of shielding-current-driven vortex rearrangement under local heating using diamond quantum sensors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14578)
*Ryoei Ota,Shunsuke Nishimura,Koki Honda,Takeyuki Tsuji,Taro Yamashita,Takayuki Iwasaki,Mutsuko Hatano,Kento Sasaki,Kensuke Kobayashi*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该研究利用金刚石氮空位（NV）色心系综的宽场磁成像技术，定量测量了NbN薄膜中涡旋的杂散磁场分布，并通过局部激光加热和逐步改变外加磁场，实时捕捉了超过100分钟的涡旋构型重排过程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解和控制超导体中的涡旋运动对于抑制超导器件中的耗散以及开发基于涡旋的器件应用都具有重要意义。研究涡旋动力学有助于优化超导设备的性能并探索新的应用可能性。

Method: 采用完美对准的金刚石氮空位（NV）色心系综进行宽场磁成像，定量测量了NbN薄膜中涡旋的杂散磁场分布。在局部激光加热条件下，逐步改变外加磁场并连续测量，实现了对涡旋构型重排的实时空间观测。

Result: 观测到的涡旋重排与局部激光加热导致的钉扎力（pinning force）减弱以及由磁场变化感生的屏蔽电流所产生的洛伦兹力（Lorentz force）作用一致。实验成功捕获了超过100分钟的实时涡旋构型变化过程。

Conclusion: 该研究为理解涡旋动力学提供了新见解，并提出了潜在应用方向，包括将涡旋排除在超导器件的敏感区域之外，以及在基于涡旋的器件中实现涡旋的精确定位。

Abstract: Understanding and controlling vortex motion in superconductors are important both for suppressing dissipation in superconducting devices and for device applications that exploit vortices. In this work, we quantitatively imaged the stray magnetic field distribution of vortices in an NbN thin film by wide-field magnetic imaging using a perfectly aligned diamond NV ensemble. By continuously measuring while stepwise varying the applied magnetic field under local laser heating, we captured a rearrangement of the vortex configuration in real space and in real time over more than 100 min. The observed vortex rearrangement is consistent with a reduction of the pinning force due to local laser heating and with the Lorentz force exerted by shielding currents induced by the field variation. These results provide insight into vortex dynamics and suggest potential applications, including vortex exclusion from sensitive regions of superconducting devices and vortex positioning in vortex-based devices.

</details>


### [9] [Quantum Landscape of Superconducting Diodes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14623)
*Muhammad Nadeem,Xiaolin Wang*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该研究将超导二极管（superconducting diodes）的量子特性映射到量子技术架构中，旨在解决现有量子硬件在控制和可扩展性方面的挑战，通过集成非线性、非互易性电路元件实现温度匹配的经典-量子混合工作流。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有非集成量子技术硬件面临两个主要挑战：非线性非互易电路元件（nonlinear and nonreciprocal circuit elements）通常复杂、笨重且耗散；经典控制电子学（classical control electronics）与量子处理器之间的温度梯度（temperature gradient）使可扩展性更加困难。

Method: 研究将超导二极管（superconducting diodes）的内置非线性、非互易性和量子功能映射到片上集成电路量子电动力学（on-chip integrated circuit quantum electrodynamics, c-QED）架构中，利用热力学约束（thermodynamic constraints）和场效应（field effects）构建量子增强平台。

Result: 超导二极管的特性能够实现噪声弹性量子比特（noise-resilient qubit）和量子比特接口的可扩展集成，支持高效功率传输、相干控制和存储、高保真度读取以及量子极限放大（quantum-limited amplification）。

Conclusion: 该视角有望在超导电路量子硬件发展中发挥关键作用，实现温度匹配的经典、量子和混合工作流（temperature-matched classical, quantum, and hybrid workflows），促进热兼容性和片上可扩展性。

Abstract: This study maps the quantum landscape of superconducting diodes (SDs) \cite{nadeem23} onto the quantum technology architecture, which is currently constrained by fundamental challenges in control and scalability. In the existing non-integrated quantum technology hardware, control and scalability related issues emerge at two fronts: First, nonlinear and nonreciprocal circuit elements, which are essential building blocks for quantum processors, are often complex, bulky, and dissipative. Second, the temperature gradient between classical control electronics ($T_C\gtrsim$ K), which is also dissipative, and the quantum processor at cryogenic temperatures ($T_Q\sim$ mK) makes scalability even more challenging. The main focus is to reveal how the built-in nonlinearity, nonreciprocity, and quantum functionalities of SDs are significant for on-chip integrated circuit quantum electrodynamics (c-QED), enabling scalable integration of noise-resilient qubit and qubit-interfaces for efficient power delivery, coherent control and memory, high-fidelity readout, and quantum-limited amplification. To this end, this study will also shed light on how thermodynamic constraints and field effects can be harnessed within a quantum-enhanced SD platform, thereby enabling thermal compatibility between classical and quantum workflows, isothermal all-electrical control, and on-chip scalability. This perspective is expected to play a pivotal role in the advancement of superconducting circuit-based quantum hardware with temperature-matched classical, quantum, and hybrid workflows.

</details>


### [10] [Interlayer hybridization enables superconductivity in bilayer nickelates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14701)
*Shilong Zhang,Meng Zhang,Qilin Luo,Zihao Tao,Hsiao-Yu Huang,Kunhao Li,Jie Li,Junchi Fu,Di-Jing Huang,Yanwu Xie,Yi Lu,Yingying Peng*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本研究通过稳定超导(La,Pr)₃Ni₂O₇薄膜并利用X射线光谱技术，揭示了双层镍酸盐中实现超导所需的微观电子重组机制，特别是层间d_z²-p_z-d_z²杂化通道的关键作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Ruddlesden-Popper镍酸盐为超越铜酸盐和铁基超导体的高温超导提供了新途径，但双层镍酸盐中实现超导的电子重组机制尚未解决，主要由于难以直接探测超导相。

Method: 通过保护性覆盖层稳定超导(La,Pr)₃Ni₂O₇薄膜，利用X射线吸收谱（X-ray absorption）和共振非弹性X射线散射（resonant inelastic X-ray scattering）直接进行光谱探测，结合理论分析研究电子态演化。

Result: 研究发现面内d_x²-y²态形成巡游骨架，而超导性仅在相干d_z²-p_z-d_z²层间杂化发展时出现，伴随静态自旋序抑制和强烈阻尼的自旋激发。氧化学计量和外延应变均作用于该层间通道。

Conclusion: 超导性存在于层间相干性和关联强度的狭窄窗口内，这些发现确定了双层镍酸盐中实现超导所需的微观要素，并提供了其出现的多轨道图像。

Abstract: Ruddlesden-Popper nickelates offer a new route to high-temperature superconductivity beyond the cuprates and iron-pnictides. However, the electronic reorganization that enables superconductivity in bilayer nickelates remain unresolved, largely due to the difficulty of directly probing the superconducting phase. Here, we overcome this limitation by stabilizing superconducting (La,Pr)$_3$Ni$_2$O$_7$ thin films with a protective capping layer, thereby enabling direct spectroscopic access via X-ray absorption and resonant inelastic X-ray scattering. We resolve the evolution of in-plane and out-of-plane electronic states, spin and orbital excitations, and spin-density-waves across insulating, superconducting, and metallic regimes. Combining experimental results with theoretical analysis, we show that the in-plane $d_{x^2-y^2}$ states form an itinerant backbone, while superconductivity emerges only when coherent $d_{z^2}$-$p_z$-$d_{z^2}$ interlayer hybridization develops, accompanied by suppressed static spin order and strongly damped spin excitations. Oxygen stoichiometry and epitaxial strain both act on this interlayer channel, placing superconductivity within a narrow window of interlayer coherence and correlation strength. These findings identify the microscopic ingredients required for superconductivity in bilayer nickelates and provide a multiorbital picture of its emergence.

### [11] [Fermi-liquid versus non-Fermi-liquid/'strange-metal' fits to the electrical resistivity in the quantum critical magnetic regime of an unconventional superconductor](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14952)
*W. Knafo,T. Thebault,K. Somesh,G. Lapertot,G. Knebel,D. Braithwaite,D. Aoki*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 在重费米子顺磁体UTe₂中，非常规超导性在磁场诱导的变磁性量子相变附近出现。通过对比不同质量样品的电阻率数据，研究发现非费米液体行为可能掩盖了低温下的"隐藏"费米液体T²区域，强调了高质量样品对确认量子临界行为的重要性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解非常规超导性的核心问题是探究超导相内部是否存在量子临界点（quantum critical point）。在多种非常规超导体中，非费米液体/奇异金属的Tⁿ电阻率变化（n<2）被认为是磁量子临界性的特征，但实验上难以证明这种高温行为确实源于本征的零温量子临界区域。

Method: 对两个不同质量的UTe₂样品进行了电阻率数据的比较分析，磁场方向相对于b轴倾斜角度θ≃35-40°。数据拟合采用费米液体函数ρ=ρ₀+AT²或非费米液体/奇异金属函数ρ=ρ₀+AₙTⁿ。

Result: 在40T以上诱导的超导相附近，从Tⁿ拟合中提取出非物理的剩余电阻率ρ₀<0，这表明在低温下可能最终恢复"隐藏"的费米液体T²区域。高质量样品的低剩余电阻率对于确认量子临界行为至关重要。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明，需要调查具有低剩余电阻率的高质量样品来确认或否定被超导性掩盖的"隐藏"量子临界行为的存在。这一发现强调了样品质量在揭示量子临界现象中的关键作用。

Abstract: The question of a possible quantum critical point lying inside of a superconducting phase is central for understanding unconventional superconductivity. In various unconventional superconductors, non-Fermi-liquid/'strange-metal' $T^{n}$ variations, with $n<2$, of the electrical resistivity have been identified as the signature of magnetic quantum criticality. However, a difficulty is to prove experimentally that a non-Fermi-liquid/'strange-metal' law identified at temperatures above the superconducting temperature is the signature of an intrinsic zero-temperature quantum critical regime. In the heavy-fermion paramagnet UTe$_2$, unconventional superconductivity develops in the vicinity of a metamagnetic quantum phase transition induced by a magnetic field, and the quantum critical magnetic properties are suspected to play a role for the superconducting mechanism. In this work, we present a comparative analysis of electrical resistivity data collected on two UTe$_2$ samples of different qualities, in magnetic fields tilted by angles $θ\simeq35-40$~$^\circ$ from $\mathbf{b}$ to $\mathbf{c}$. Fits to the data have been performed either with a Fermi-liquid function $ρ=ρ_0+AT^{2}$ or with a non-Fermi-liquid/'strange-metal' function $ρ=ρ_0+A_nT^n$. Near to a superconducting phase induced beyond 40~T, non-physical residual resistivities $ρ_0<0$ are extracted from the $T^n$ fits, revealing that a 'hidden' Fermi-liquid $T^2$ regime may be ultimately recovered at low temperature. The results obtained here highlight the importance to investigate high-quality samples with low residual resistivity to confirm - or not - the presence of a suspected 'hidden' quantum critical behavior masked by superconductivity.

</details>


### [12] [Type II Lifshitz invariant and optically active Higgs mode in time-reversal symmetry broken superconductors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15054)
*Raigo Nagashima,Chihiro Mamiya,Naoto Tsuji*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该论文引入了"第二类Lifshitz不变量"的概念，这是一种在超导体中出现的特殊对称性允许项，它改变符号于粒子-空穴变换下，并导致希格斯模式在光学电导谱中可见。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Lifshitz不变量是序相Ginzburg-Landau自由能中的对称性允许项，涉及序参数和单空间导数，作为异常光学响应的来源。然而，传统的第一类Lifshitz不变量在粒子-空穴变换下保持符号不变，需要探索更丰富的对称性结构。

Method: 作者引入了"第二类Lifshitz不变量"的概念，它在粒子-空穴变换下改变符号。通过群论分析，对所有允许第二类Lifshitz不变量的磁点群中不可约核心表示对进行了分类。同时，对多种破坏时间反演对称性的多带超导体模型进行了光学电导的数值计算。

Result: 研究表明，第二类Lifshitz不变量仅出现在破坏时间反演对称性的超导体中，并使得希格斯模式（Higgs mode）在光学电导谱中可见。数值计算结果与群论分析一致，确认了理论预测的有效性。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了一类普遍存在的破坏时间反演对称性的超导体，它们承载着光学活性的希格斯模式。第二类Lifshitz不变量的识别为理解超导体中的异常光学响应提供了新的理论框架。

Abstract: Lifshitz invariant is a symmetry-allowed term in the Ginzburg-Landau free energy of an ordered phase, involving the order parameters and a single spatial derivative, which serves as a source of unusual optical responses. Here we introduce a ``type II" Lifshitz invariant for superconductors, which changes its sign under the particle-hole transformation and can be distinguished from the ordinary particle-hole even ``type I" Lifshitz invariant. We show that the type II Lifshitz invariant appears only in superconductors that break time-reversal symmetry and allows the Higgs mode to be visible in the optical conductivity spectrum. We provide a classification of all pairs of irreducible corepresentations of order parameters in the magnetic point groups that admit a type II Lifshitz invariant. We also numerically calculate the optical conductivity for various models of time-reversal symmetry broken multiband superconductors, finding agreement with the group-theoretical analysis. Our results establish a universal class of time-reversal symmetry broken superconductors hosting an optically active Higgs mode.

</details>


### [13] [Quantum fluctuations and the emergence of in-gap Higgs mode in superconductors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15120)
*Sida Tian,Naoto Tsuji,Dirk Manske*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该研究将s波超导体中希格斯模（Higgs mode）的作用扩展到包含量子涨落（quantum fluctuations），发现单圈量子修正会使希格斯传播子的本征频率低于超导能隙2Δ，导致更尖锐的实验信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于将s波超导体中已确立的希格斯模（Higgs mode）作用扩展到包含量子涨落（quantum fluctuations），以理解量子修正对振幅模式的影响。

Method: 方法包括计算希格斯传播子的单圈量子修正（one-loop quantum corrections），并通过计算三谐波产生（Third Harmonic Generation, THG）和非弹性拉曼散射（inelastic Raman scattering）信号来展示修正后的特征指纹。

Result: 结果显示量子涨落使希格斯模的本征频率移至超导能隙2Δ以下，形成准粒子连续谱（quasiparticle continuum）下方的无阻尼极点（undamped pole），导致实验信号显著锐化。

Conclusion: 结论表明即使任意弱的量子涨落也会导致频率偏移和新极点的产生，这一发现对理解其他振幅模式（包括电荷密度波、反铁磁体和冷原子费米凝聚体）具有重要意义。

Abstract: We extend the well-established action of the Higgs mode in $s$-wave superconductors to include quantum fluctuations (QFs). We find that already one-loop quantum corrections to the Higgs propagator shift its eigenfrequency below the superconducting energy gap $2Δ$. Consequently, the Higgs mode appears as an undamped pole below the quasiparticle continuum, leading to drastically sharper experimental signatures. We demonstrate this by calculating two characteristic fingerprints of the Higgs mode, namely in Third Harmonic Generation (THG) and inelastic Raman scattering signals. More generally, gaps measured in $s$-wave superconductors with different experimental techniques (such as scanning tunneling microscope and Raman scattering) may be different due to fluctuation corrections. Since already arbitrarily weak QFs lead to the shift and to the new pole, our results shed some light on other amplitude modes even for systems with weak QFs, including charge density waves, (anti-) ferromagnets, or cold atom fermionic condensates.

</details>


### [14] [Abrikosov vortices in altermagnetic superconductors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15204)
*A. A. Mazanik,F. S. Bergeret*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了交变磁性（altermagnetism）超导体中磁场穿透的独特行为：磁场产生椭圆涡旋而非圆形阿布里科索夫涡旋，且涡旋取向受磁场与奈尔矢量相对方向调控，导致非互易磁化曲线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在理解具有共线d波交变磁序（collinear $d$-wave altermagnetic order）的超导体中外部磁场的穿透机制，探索交变磁性与超导性共存体系的物理特性。

Method: 通过理论分析交变磁性诱导的有效质量各向异性，研究磁场与奈尔矢量（Néel vector）耦合对涡旋形状和取向的影响，并考虑钉扎缺陷对磁化行为的作用。

Result: 磁场产生椭圆涡旋（elliptical vortices），其长轴沿自旋劈裂最大的晶轴方向；反转磁场平行分量使涡旋重新取向；钉扎缺陷导致磁场反转时出现非互易磁化曲线（nonreciprocal magnetization curves）。

Conclusion: 交变磁性通过磁场-奈尔矢量耦合诱导有效质量各向异性，导致涡旋形状和取向的独特调控，为探索交变磁性与超导共存体系中的超电流涡旋开辟了新实验途径。

Abstract: We study the penetration of an external magnetic field into a superconductor with collinear $d$-wave altermagnetic order. We demonstrate that instead of circular Abrikosov vortices, the magnetic field generates elliptical vortices with their major axis oriented along one of the crystallographic axis, along which the altermagnetic spin splitting is maximal. Upon reversing the component of the magnetic field parallel to the altermagnetic Néel vector, the vortices reorient towards the other crystallographic axis with maximal spin splitting. We demonstrate that this effect originates from an altermagnetism-induced anisotropy of the effective mass, which is controlled by the coupling between the external magnetic field and the Néel vector. As a consequence, a superconducting film hosting such altermagnetic order and containing pinning defects exhibits nonreciprocal magnetization curves under reversal of the magnetic field parallel to its Néel vector, due to the different vortex--vortex interaction energies for the two field orientations. Our results broaden the understanding of the coexistence of altermagnetism and superconductivity, both in materials hosting these orders intrinsically or in superconductor/altermagnet hybrid structures, and open new experimental avenues for exploring supercurrent vortices in these systems.

</details>

### [15] [Phonon mediated spin-spin interactions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14731)
*J. Fransson*

Main category: cond-mat.other

TL;DR: 该论文研究了绝缘体中局域磁矩之间的声子介导相互作用机制，证明了这种机制可以产生可量化的对称和反对称各向异性自旋-自旋相互作用，并解释了手性化合物中观察到的弱铁磁有序现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 绝缘体和半导体中由于缺乏传导载流子，局域磁矩之间的长程相互作用通常很小或可忽略。然而，磁性有序绝缘体（如金属氧化物）的存在促使研究者探索支持这种有序的各种可能机制，声子介导相互作用是其中之一。

Method: 论文考虑了局域磁矩之间的声子介导相互作用作为机制，分析其能否产生可量化的对称和反对称各向异性自旋-自旋相互作用（spin-spin interactions）。

Result: 研究表明，对称各向异性相互作用存在于所有类型的声子中，而反对称各向异性相互作用的存在需要反演对称性破缺（broken inversion symmetry）。该机制可以解释手性化合物（如CuO和CoO）中观察到的弱铁磁有序（weak ferromagnetic order）。相互作用在低温下几乎与温度无关，在高温下呈线性增长；空间上具有振荡幂律衰减特性。

Conclusion: 声子介导相互作用为绝缘体中局域磁矩之间的长程相互作用提供了可行的物理机制，能够产生对称和反对称各向异性自旋-自旋相互作用，特别是反对称相互作用需要反演对称性破缺，这解释了某些手性化合物中的磁性有序现象。

Abstract: Indirect long range interactions between localized magnetic moments are in metals mediated by itinerant electrons. In insulators and semi-conductor, such interactions need to be small, if not negligible, due to the absence of mediating carriers. The existence of magnetically ordered insulators, for instance, metal-oxides, is therefore an everlasting source for proposals of various mechanisms that may support the order. Here, phonon mediated interactions between localized magnetic moments is considered as a mechanism that can provide quantifiable symmetric and anti-symmetric anisotropic spin-spin interactions. It is demonstrated that while a symmetric anisotropic interaction exists for all types of phonons, the existence of anti-symmetric anisotropic interactions requires broken inversion symmetry. The latter mechanism may explain the weak ferromagnetic order observed in chiral, e.g., CuO and CoO compounds. Furthermore, the interaction is nearly independent of the temperature at low temperature while approaches a linear growth at high. Spatially, the interactions have an oscillatory power law decay with the inter-nuclei distance.

</details>


### [16] [Static heterogeneity generates apparent universality in first-passage bursty dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15084)
*Morten Møller,Philipp Rahe,Sadegh Ghaderzadeh,Elena Besley,Philip Moriarty*

Main category: cond-mat.other

TL;DR: 该研究通过扫描隧道显微镜探测二维分子扩散系统，发现其脉冲间隔时间分布与人类活动（如电子邮件、网页浏览）具有相同的截断幂律形式。最大似然估计和模型比较表明Kohlrausch-Williams-Watts-调和的幂律分布（α∼1）优于纯幂律模型，证明观测到的α∼1标度源于尖端诱导的空间异质性而非内在的无标度动力学。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在解决关于观测到的幂律指数α=1是否反映内在无标度动力学（scale-free dynamics）还是源于异质基础速率的长期争论。该问题在人类动力学中已有广泛讨论，但需要在物理系统中进行验证。

Method: 采用扫描隧道显微镜（scanning tunnelling microscope）尖端探测二维分子扩散这一典型物理系统，研究首次通过动力学（first-passage dynamics）。使用最大似然估计（maximum-likelihood estimation）和模型比较分析脉冲间隔时间分布，并通过动力学蒙特卡洛模拟（kinetic Monte Carlo simulations）验证结果。

Result: 脉冲间隔时间分布呈现与人类活动相似的截断幂律形式（truncated power-law form）。模型比较明确支持Kohlrausch-Williams-Watts-调和的幂律分布（α∼1），而非纯幂律分布。模拟表明α∼1标度仅存在于有限时间窗口，源于尖端诱导的空间异质性（tip-induced spatial heterogeneity），而非标度不变性。

Conclusion: 观测到的α∼1标度行为并非反映内在无标度动力学，而是由探测尖端引起的空间异质性所产生。这一发现为人类动力学中类似的幂律分布提供了物理机制解释，表明表观标度行为可能源于系统异质性而非真正的标度不变性。

Abstract: Processes involving bursts of activity separated by quiescent periods occur across diverse systems and scales. In human dynamics, these phenomena have been described by power-law inter-event time distributions, $P(t)\sim t^{-α}$, with putative universality classes $α=1$ and $α=\frac{3}{2}$ having been proposed. Whether the observed $α= 1$ scaling reflects intrinsic scale-free dynamics or instead emerges from heterogeneous underlying rates has been debated at length. We address this question in a canonical physical system for first-passage dynamics: two-dimensional molecular diffusion detected by the tip of a scanning tunnelling microscope. The resulting inter-pulse time distributions exhibit the same apparent truncated power-law form reported for human activities such as email communication, web browsing, and library loans. Maximum-likelihood estimation and model comparison decisively favor a Kohlrausch-Williams-Watts--tempered power law, $P(t)\propto t^{-α}\exp\left(-(t/t_c)^β\right)$, with $α\sim 1$. Kinetic Monte Carlo simulations reproduce this behavior, showing that the apparent $α\sim 1$ scaling is confined to a finite time window and arises from tip-induced spatial heterogeneity, not scale invariance.

</details>

### [17] [Constraining Quintessential Inflation with ACT: A Gauss-Bonnet Gateway](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14659)
*Yogesh,Imtiyaz Ahmad Bhat,Mayukh R. Gangopadhyay,M. Sami*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文重新审视了爱因斯坦-高斯-博内（Einstein-Gauss-Bonnet，EGB）引力框架下的本质暴胀（quintessential inflation）模型。研究表明，指数型和双曲正割型耦合可以将预测的$r$和$n_s$值调整到ACT观测允许的$1σ$区域内，而双曲正切型耦合仍与观测不符。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 阿塔卡马宇宙学望远镜（Atacama Cosmology Telescope，ACT）的最新观测结果显示标量谱指数（scalar spectral index）$n_s = 0.9743 \pm 0.0034$更高且约束更紧，这使得多个暴胀模型面临张力，特别是本质暴胀模型在$r$-$n_s$平面中接近或超出$2σ$边界。

Method: 在爱因斯坦-高斯-博内（Einstein-Gauss-Bonnet，EGB）引力框架下重新研究本质暴胀模型，其中标量场与高斯-博内不变量（Gauss-Bonnet invariant）非最小耦合。考虑了三种代表性耦合函数：指数型、双曲正割型和双曲正切型，并使用模型无关的参数化方法研究了再加热（reheating）阶段。

Result: 指数型和双曲正割型（sech-type）耦合可以将张量-标量比（tensor-to-scalar ratio）$r$和标量谱指数$n_s$的预测值调整到ACT观测允许的$1σ$区域内，从而恢复与观测的一致性。双曲正切型（tanh-type）耦合仍与观测不符，这突显了暴胀可观测量对耦合结构的敏感性。再加热温度符合大爆炸核合成（Big Bang nucleosynthesis）的界限。

Conclusion: EGB修正为本质暴胀提供了一个可行且稳健的扩展，使其与当前精确宇宙学数据相协调。研究确定了相应的允许参数空间，并证明即使在没有势能最小值的情况下也能实现可行的热历史。

Abstract: Recent results from the Atacama Cosmology Telescope (ACT), indicating a higher and more tightly constrained scalar spectral index, $n_s = 0.9743 \pm 0.0034$, place several inflationary models under tension, with quintessential inflation pushed close to or beyond the $2σ$ boundary in the $r$--$n_s$ plane. In this work, we revisit quintessential inflation within the framework of Einstein--Gauss--Bonnet (EGB) gravity, where a scalar field non-minimally coupled to the Gauss--Bonnet invariant modifies the inflationary dynamics.
  We consider three representative coupling functions -- exponential, hyperbolic secant, and hyperbolic tangent -- and show that the exponential and sech-type couplings can shift the predicted values of $r$ and $n_s$ into the $1σ$ region allowed by ACT, thereby restoring consistency with observations. In contrast, the tanh-type coupling remains disfavored, underscoring the sensitivity of inflationary observables to the coupling structure.
  We further investigate the reheating phase using a model-independent parametrization and demonstrate that viable thermal histories can be realized even in the absence of a potential minimum, with reheating temperatures consistent with Big Bang nucleosynthesis bounds. Overall, our analysis shows that EGB corrections provide a viable and robust extension that reconciles quintessential inflation with current precision cosmological data, and we identify the corresponding allowed parameter space.

</details>


### [18] [Nonperturbative stochastic inflation in perturbative dynamical background](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15219)
*Xiao-Quan Ye,Shao-Jiang Wang*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 该研究从弯曲时空量子场论出发，推导了准德西特（quasi-de Sitter）时空中的一阶随机方程，建立了一个系统处理量子扩散和背景非线性引力响应的框架，并将其应用于包含超慢滚（ultra-slow-roll）相的两个暴胀模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 包含瞬态超慢滚（ultra-slow-roll）相的暴胀模型会展现强烈的非微扰（non-perturbative）动力学，使得通常的宇宙学扰动微扰处理变得不完整。在此类机制中，量子扩散（quantum diffusion）和背景的非线性引力响应都起着重要作用，因此需要建立一个在弯曲时空量子场论（quantum field theory in curved spacetime）中系统处理它们的框架。

Method: 从Schwinger-Keldysh形式体系推导了准德西特时空中的一阶随机方程，并开发了一种实用程序来获得紧凑的随机方程，这些方程通过经典的Arnowitt-Deser-Misner方程一致地包含了度规扰动。该方法系统地捕捉了经典非微扰效应，同时保留了主导的一阶量子扩散。

Result: 将该形式体系应用于两个包含超慢滚相的暴胀情景：Starobinsky分段线性模型和临界希格斯暴胀（critical Higgs inflation）。对于Starobinsky模型，数值晶格模拟验证了随机描述并与解析结果吻合良好。对于临界希格斯暴胀，研究发现动力学导致功率谱（power spectrum）轻微抑制并伴有额外的振荡特征。

Conclusion: 该研究在弯曲时空量子场论的第一性原理与用于研究非微扰暴胀动力学的随机-δN形式体系（stochastic-δN formalism）之间建立了具体桥梁。整个分析限于小度规扰动机制，确保了微扰随机处理的自洽性。

Abstract: Inflationary models that contain a transient ultra-slow-roll phase can exhibit strong non-perturbative dynamics, making the usual perturbative treatment of cosmological fluctuations incomplete. In such regimes, quantum diffusion and the nonlinear gravitational response of the background can both play important roles, motivating a framework that treats them systematically within quantum field theory in curved spacetime. In this work, we derive the first-order stochastic equations in quasi-de Sitter spacetime from the Schwinger-Keldysh formalism and develop a practical procedure to obtain compact stochastic equations that consistently incorporate metric perturbations via the classical Arnowitt-Deser-Misner equations. Our approach systematically captures classical non-perturbative effects while retaining the leading first-order quantum diffusion. We apply the formalism to two inflationary scenarios with an ultra-slow-roll phase, namely the Starobinsky piecewise-linear model and critical Higgs inflation. For the Starobinsky model, numerical lattice simulations validate the stochastic description and agree well with analytical results. For critical Higgs inflation, we find that the dynamics lead to a minor suppression of the power spectrum with an additional oscillation feature. Throughout, our analysis is restricted to the regime of small metric perturbations, ensuring the self-consistency of the perturbative stochastic treatment. These results establish a concrete bridge between first-principles quantum field theory in curved spacetime and the stochastic-$δN$ formalism for investigating non-perturbative inflationary dynamics.

</details>


### [19] [Gravitational-wave lensing beyond rays: a disordered-system approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15313)
*Ripalta Amoruso,Ginevra Braga,Alice Garoffolo,Francescopaolo Lopez,Nicola Bartolo,Sabino Matarrese*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 该研究建立了描述引力波在弱引力透镜随机分布中传播的框架，超越了几何光学极限，统一处理干涉、衍射和统计涨落效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于描述引力波在随机分布的弱引力透镜中传播时超越几何光学极限的效应，需要统一处理干涉、衍射和透镜分布的统计涨落。

Method: 方法包括：将透镜分布建模为静态随机背景场，使用淬火无序（quenched disorder）语言描述问题，采用Schwinger-Keldysh形式构建平均密度矩阵的路径积分表示，并对合适的耦合类别进行微扰展开。

Result: 结果得到平均密度矩阵的显式形式，自然分离为控制相位敏感贡献抑制的二次指数项和修正相干传播的纯振荡贡献，识别了控制相干损失起始的物理尺度，并以高斯波包为例进行了说明。

Conclusion: 该框架为引力波透镜提供了统一描述，适用于相同作用量类别的任何系统，使其在超越引力波透镜的波在无序介质中传播领域具有更广泛的相关性。

Abstract: We develop a framework to describe gravitational wave propagation through a stochastic distribution of weak gravitational lenses beyond the geometric optics limit. We model the lens distribution as a static random background field and formulate the problem in the language of quenched disorder, treating the disorder averaged density matrix as the fundamental object from which observables are computed. Using the Schwinger Keldysh formalism, we construct a path-integral representation of the averaged density matrix and derive its explicit form perturbatively for a suitable class of couplings. The result naturally separates into a quadratic exponential term, which governs the suppression of phase sensitive contributions in the averaged description, and a purely oscillatory contribution, which modifies coherent propagation through a disorder-induced correction to the propagation kernel. This provides a unified description of interference, diffraction, and statistical fluctuations of the lens distribution within a single framework. We also identify the physical scales controlling the onset of coherence loss and illustrate the formalism in the case of Gaussian wave packets. More generally, the derivation applies to any system described by the same class of actions, making the framework relevant beyond gravitational wave lensing to wave propagation in disordered media.

</details>

### [20] [Electromagnetic, gravitational wave, and static gravitational transmission through throat spacetimes: a constraint-wave asymmetry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14238)
*Jeff Riley*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究计算了电磁波、引力波和静态引力扰动在球对称时空几何喉道中的传输特性，揭示了传播辐射（ℓ≥1）与静态单极子（ℓ=0）之间的结构约束-波不对称性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在理解电磁扰动、引力波扰动和静态引力扰动在球对称时空几何喉道中的传输特性，特别是不同多极模式在通过喉道时的行为差异。

Method: 在超静态Ellis-Bronnikov背景下，将四维麦克斯韦方程分解为矢量球谐函数，得到具有离心势垒的有效薛定谔问题。对于静态引力单极子，分析线性化爱因斯坦方程。研究扩展到具有不同剖面形状的单参数喉道几何族和反射-史瓦西型虫洞，使用Numerov积分、WKB估计和精确解析解进行比较。

Result: 对于传播辐射（ℓ≥1），低于势垒顶部频率的频率通过亚势垒隧穿被强烈抑制；对于静态引力单极子（ℓ=0），满足无源守恒定律且无势垒，呈现多项式衰减。这种定性不对称性在静态球对称喉道中具有普适性。

Conclusion: 研究建立了源于场方程多极分解的结构约束-波不对称性，这种不对称性与产生几何的物质内容无关，且在固定背景下独立存在。

Abstract: We compute the transmission properties of electromagnetic (EM), gravitational wave (GW), and static gravitational perturbations through geometric throats in spherically symmetric spacetimes. On the ultrastatic Ellis-Bronnikov background, decomposition of the four-dimensional Maxwell equations into vector spherical harmonics yields an effective Schrödinger problem with centrifugal barrier $V_\ell^{(\mathrm{EM})}=\ell(\ell+1)/(σ^2+r_0^2)$ peaked at the throat. For the lowest physical EM mode ($\ell=1$), frequencies below the barrier-top frequency $ω_{\max}=\sqrt{2}/r_0$ are strongly suppressed by sub-barrier tunnelling. Gravitational wave perturbations ($\ell\ge 2$) see a qualitatively similar barrier and are likewise strongly suppressed below their respective barrier-top frequencies. By contrast, the static gravitational monopole ($\ell=0$), governed by the linearised Einstein equations on the same background, satisfies the source-free conservation law $(a^2Φ')'=0$ with no potential barrier, yielding the exact solution $Φ\propto\arctan(σ/r_0)$. We extend these results to a one-parameter family of throat geometries with varying profile shapes, and to a reflected-Schwarzschild (Damour-Solodukhin-type) wormhole, demonstrating that the qualitative asymmetry\emdash strong sub-barrier suppression for all propagating radiation ($\ell\ge 1$) versus polynomial attenuation for the static monopole ($\ell=0$)\emdash is universal for static, spherically symmetric throats. Numerov integration, WKB estimates, and exact analytical solutions are compared throughout. The results establish a structural constraint-wave asymmetry arising from the multipole decomposition of the field equations, independent of the matter content sourcing the geometry, on a fixed background.

</details>

### [22] [Fast neural network surrogate for multimodal effective-one-body gravitational waveforms from generically precessing compact binaries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14270)
*Christopher Whittall,Geraint Pratten*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究开发了SEOBNRv5PHM_NNSur7dq10，这是一个基于机器学习构建的降阶神经网络代理模型，用于快速生成准圆进动双黑洞系统的引力波波形模板，计算效率相比原始物理模型大幅提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 引力波波形模板是探测和表征宇宙中致密双星并合事件的关键工具，但物理精度要求与计算效率需求之间存在矛盾。代理模型（surrogate models）作为数据驱动的快速模型，能够缓解这一矛盾。

Method: 研究将机器学习技术整合到传统的降阶代理框架（reduced order surrogate framework）中，扩展了模型对描述准圆进动双星（precessing quasicircular binaries）的波形模型的覆盖范围。具体构建了SEOBNRv5PHM_NNSur7dq10这一降阶神经网络代理模型。

Result: 该代理模型适用于质量比达1:10、具有任意自旋大小和方向的准圆进动双黑洞系统。在CPU上评估单个波形时，其速度比SEOBNRv5PHM快约5倍；在GPU上批量处理波形时，每个波形的速度提升近1000倍。模型保真度得到验证，并成功应用于真实和注入引力波数据的贝叶斯参数推断。

Conclusion: 研究成功开发了高效准确的引力波波形代理模型，将机器学习技术融入传统降阶代理框架，显著提升了波形生成的计算效率，为引力波天文学的数据分析提供了有力工具。

Abstract: Gravitational waveform templates are a key ingredient for the detection and characterization of gravitational waves emitted by compact binary mergers in the universe. These templates must be physically accurate and extensive, but also highly computationally efficient, two requirements that are often in tension. One solution to this problem is the development of surrogate models, which are fast, data-driven models trained to predict the output of a slower, physically realistic waveform model. In this article we build on existing work to incorporate machine learning techniques into the conventional reduced order surrogate framework, with a focus on extending coverage to waveform models that describe generically precessing quasicircular binaries. In particular, we present SEOBNRv5PHM_NNSur7dq10, a reduced order neural network surrogate of the SEOBNRv5PHM waveform model, valid up to mass ratios 1:10 for precessing quasicircular binary black hole systems with arbitrary spin magnitudes and orientations. The faithfulness of the surrogate to SEOBNRv5PHM is validated, and the surrogate is successfully applied to Bayesian parameter inference using both real and injected gravitational wave data. The surrogate is approximately 5 times faster than SEOBNRv5PHM when evaluating a single waveform on a CPU, and nearly 1000 times faster per-waveform when amortizing the cost over large waveform batches on a GPU.

</details>


### [23] [Emergent structure in the binary black hole mass distribution and implications for population-based cosmology](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14290)
*Vasco Gennari,Tom Bertheas,Nicola Tamanini*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本研究利用B样条（B-splines）对引力波（gravitational waves）事件的主质量分布进行无模型重构，识别了多个质量特征并发现对数层级结构证据。该结构通过群体边界特征影响哈勃常数（Hubble constant）测量，作者提出通过分离低质量事件子群体来减少系统误差。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 引力波为研究黑洞合并的天体物理过程和宇宙动力学提供了有力探针，但这些测量依赖于准确推断未知的底层群体分布。准确重建主质量分布对于理解黑洞群体特征和宇宙学参数测量至关重要。

Method: 采用B样条（B-splines）对主质量分布进行无模型重构（agnostic reconstruction），通过增加模型复杂度来表征结构的出现。使用最新的引力波瞬变目录GWTC-4.0进行分析，并引入分离低质量事件子群体的方法来减少建模系统误差。

Result: 识别了多个质量特征并发现群体中存在对数层级结构（logarithmic hierarchy）的证据。研究表明该结构主要通过群体边界特征直接影响哈勃常数（Hubble constant）的测量结果。

Conclusion: 通过分离低质量事件子群体来减轻建模系统误差的方法，为未来数据集实现稳健的基于群体的宇宙学（population-based cosmology）测量提供了有前景的路径。

Abstract: Gravitational waves provide a powerful probe of both the astrophysical processes driving black hole mergers and the dynamics of the Universe, but these measurements rely on accurately inferring the unknown underlying population. We perform an agnostic reconstruction of the primary mass distribution using B-splines, characterising the emergence of structure with increasing model complexity. Using the latest gravitational-wave transient catalog, GWTC-4.0, we identify multiple mass features and find evidence suggesting a logarithmic hierarchy in the population. We show that this structure directly impacts measurements of the Hubble constant, primarily through features at the population boundaries. Finally, we introduce an approach that isolates a subpopulation of low-mass events to mitigate modelling systematics, providing a promising path toward robust population-based cosmology with future datasets.

</details>


### [24] [Hydrodynamic Analog of the Klein Paradox: Vacuum Instability and Pair Production in a Linear Elastic Medium](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14378)
*Alan F. Tinoco*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文通过流体动力学模型将克莱因佯谬（Klein Paradox）解释为连续介质在超临界应力下的弹性响应，而非量子场论中的抽象粒子对产生过程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 克莱因佯谬揭示了狄拉克方程（Dirac equation）单粒子解释的局限性，虽然量子场论（Quantum Field Theory, QFT）通过粒子对产生（pair production）解决了这一问题，但其微观机制常被抽象形式主义所掩盖。本文旨在通过类比引力（Analog Gravity）和凝聚态物理（Condensed Matter Physics）框架，为这一现象提供更直观的教学模型。

Method: 采用流体动力学模型（hydrodynamic model），将相对论性粒子（relativistic particle）视为连续线性介质中的局域弹性激发（localized elastic excitation）或缺陷（defect）。当外部应力（potential）超过介质结合能阈值（$V > 2mc^2$）时，分析系统发生的机械不稳定性（mechanical instability）。

Result: 该机械不稳定性类似于电介质击穿（dielectric breakdown），并自然产生具有反转拓扑缠绕（inverted topological winding）的模式，这些模式被识别为反粒子（antiparticles）。通过求解弹性系统的边界条件，重现了Hansen和Ravndal的透射系数，并恢复了施温格极限（Schwinger limit）下的粒子对产生率。

Conclusion: 该方法基于连续介质力学（continuum mechanics）提供了一个清晰的教学模型，可视化了真空衰变过程（vacuum decay processes）。研究表明，"佯谬"本质上是介质在超临界应力（supercritical stress）下的弹性响应，该力学类比为凝聚态物理和先进材料科学的研究生提供了连接抽象量子场论推导的具体可视化桥梁。

Abstract: The Klein Paradox -- the anomalous scattering of relativistic fermions off a high potential step -- signals the limit of the single-particle interpretation of the Dirac equation. While Quantum Field Theory (QFT) resolves this via pair production, the microscopic mechanism is often obscured by abstract formalism. In this work, we investigate this phenomenon through the framework of Analog Gravity and Condensed Matter Physics. We utilize a hydrodynamic model wherein a relativistic particle is treated as a localized elastic excitation (defect) within a continuous linear medium. We demonstrate that when the external stress (potential) exceeds the medium's binding energy threshold ($V > 2mc^2$), the system undergoes a mechanical instability analogous to dielectric breakdown. This instability naturally generates modes with inverted topological winding, which we identify as antiparticles. By solving the boundary conditions for this elastic system, we reproduce the transmission coefficients of Hansen and Ravndal and recover the Schwinger limit for pair production rates. This approach provides a clear pedagogical model based on continuum mechanics to visualize vacuum decay processes, suggesting that the "paradox" is simply the elastic response of a medium under supercritical stress. This mechanical analogy serves as a pedagogical bridge for graduate students in condensed matter physics and advanced materials science, offering a concrete visualization of vacuum instability that complements standard abstract QFT derivations.

</details>


### [25] [Entropy considerations in Many-Body Gravity and General Relativity, and the impact on cosmic inflation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14481)
*S Ganesh*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 多体引力（MBG）是一种在5维时空温度框架中构建的新型修正引力理论，能够再现宇宙暴胀（cosmic inflation）而不需要暗物质（dark matter）。该理论通过分析相互作用、时间和引力之间的基本关系，展示了暴胀的自然产生机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前研究表明多体引力（many body gravity, MBG）能够在无需暗物质的情况下解释星系旋转曲线、径向加速度关系和子弹星团的弱引力透镜效应。本研究旨在探索MBG是否能够再现宇宙暴胀（cosmic inflation），并在此过程中分析相互作用、时间和引力之间的基本关系。

Method: 首先使用量子场论（Quantum Field Theory, QFT）分析包含单个大质量粒子或非相互作用大质量粒子集合的假设宇宙，建立时间与相互作用的定量关系。然后引入相互作用的无质量标量场（massless scalar field）来解决暴胀起始时的问题。最后在弗里德曼度规（Friedmann metric）背景下求解MBG场方程。

Result: 研究发现MBG能够再现宇宙暴胀，其场方程中的熵项与QFT结果一致并进一步加速暴胀。慢滚条件（slow-roll condition）被证明是5维时空温度中无质量标量场欧拉-拉格朗日运动方程在暴胀早期的自然结果。研究还探讨了物质时代（matter era）的情况。

Conclusion: 多体引力理论成功再现了宇宙暴胀现象，揭示了相互作用、时间和引力之间的基本关系。该理论为解释早期宇宙演化提供了新的框架，同时保持了与先前暗物质替代解释的一致性。

Abstract: Many body gravity (MBG) is a novel modified theory of gravity formulated in a 5-D space-time-temperature framework, in which the variation in temperature is recast as a variation in the 5-D metric. Previous work on MBG has shown that it can reproduce galaxy rotation curves, radial acceleration relation and the weak gravitational lensing of the bullet cluster, without the inclusion of dark matter. In this work we show that MBG can reproduce cosmic inflation, and in the process, analyze fundamental relations between interaction, time and gravity. To analyze cosmic inflation using interacting massless scalar fields, we first analyze theoretically a hypothetical universe with a single massive particle, or a collection of non-interacting massive particles. A quantitative relation between time and interaction is developed using Quantum Field Theory (QFT), which suggests that the notion of time becomes ill-defined for such a universe. The mass terms in MBG and General Relativity cause a discrepancy with the QFT results. An interacting massless scalar field then becomes a necessity to resolve the issue at the onset of inflation. However, the entropic terms in the MBG field equations are seen to be consistent with the QFT results and further accelerate inflation. The slow-roll condition is shown to be a natural consequence of the Euler-Lagrange equations of motion governing the massless scalar field in 5-D space-time-temperature, during the early phase of inflation. Finally, the MBG field equations are solved in the context of a Friedmann metric, leading to inflation. The matter era is also investigated.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 构建仅传播两个自由度（2-DOF）的修正引力理论具有重要研究价值，但传统哈密顿约束分析难以将2-DOF条件转化为显式的空间协变引力（SCG）拉格朗日量，特别是在拉格朗日量非线性依赖于外曲率的情况下。

Method: 采用微扰方法，考虑多项式型SCG拉格朗日量至d=3阶（d表示每个单项式的总导数数），在宇宙学背景上进行展开。通过要求标量模式在微扰至立方阶被消除，推导出拉格朗日量中系数函数对应的条件。

Conclusion: 该研究通过微扰方法成功构造了在宇宙学背景微扰至立方阶仅传播两个自由度（2-DOF）的空间协变引力（SCG）理论，为构建2-DOF修正引力理论提供了具体可行的方案。

Abstract: There has been considerable interest in constructing modified gravity theories that propagate only two degrees of freedom (DOFs), corresponding to the tensorial gravitational waves of general relativity. Within the framework of spatially covariant gravity (SCG), the conditions for obtaining 2-DOF theories can be derived from Hamiltonian constraint analysis, but it is generally difficult to translate those conditions into explicit SCG Lagrangians, especially when the Lagrangian depends nonlinearly on the extrinsic curvature. In this work, we adopt an alternative perturbative approach. We consider polynomial-type SCG Lagrangians up to $d=3$, where $d$ denotes the total number of derivatives in each monomial, and expand them around a cosmological background. By requiring the scalar mode to be eliminated up to cubic order in perturbations, we derive the corresponding conditions on the coefficient functions in the Lagrangian. We find five explicit Lagrangians that propagate only 2 DOFs up to cubic order in perturbations around a cosmological background. These theories therefore provide concrete candidate 2-DOF SCG models, at least at the perturbative level up to cubic order.

### [27] [Gravitational Lensing Signatures of Hayward-like Black Holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14505)
*Chen-Hung Hsiao,Limei Yuan,Yidun Wan*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了Hayward类正则黑洞（Hayward-like regular black hole）的引力透镜效应，并与史瓦西黑洞（Schwarzschild black hole）进行对比分析。研究发现弱场偏折角存在微小正修正，强场渐近位置相同但透镜系数存在差异，未来高精度观测可能区分这两种黑洞类型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在探索Hayward类正则黑洞的引力透镜特征，并评估其与史瓦西黑洞在观测上的可区分性。研究动机源于理解正则黑洞（regular black hole）的观测特征及其对现有黑洞模型的检验潜力。

Method: 研究方法包括弱场近似（weak-field limit）和强偏折区域（strong-deflection regime）的引力透镜理论分析。在弱场下计算偏折角修正，在强场下分析渐近位置和透镜系数，并应用当前观测数据（如ESO325-G004、Sgr A*、M87*）进行约束。

Result: 弱场偏折角包含正比于$m \ell^2/b^3$的小正修正，表明比史瓦西黑洞有稍强的光偏折，但在大碰撞参数下观测效应可忽略。强场渐近位置$θ_{\infty}$与史瓦西黑洞相同，但正则核尺度$\ell$修改了强透镜系数$\bar a, \bar b$，影响角分离s、相对流量比$r_\mathrm{mag}$和时间延迟$ΔT_{2,1}$。

Conclusion: 当前星系尺度爱因斯坦环（Einstein-ring）数据尚无法约束正则核尺度$\ell$，预测的观测值与现有数据一致。未来高精度强场引力透镜测量可能区分Hayward类正则黑洞与史瓦西黑洞，为黑洞物理提供新的检验途径。

Abstract: We examine the gravitational lensing signatures of a Hayward-like regular black hole and its potential observational distinction from a Schwarzschild black hole. In the weak-field limit, the deflection angle includes a small positive correction proportional to $m \ell^2/b^3$, indicating slightly stronger light bending than in Schwarzschild, though the effect remains observationally negligible at large impact parameters. Current galaxy-scale Einstein-ring data, such as from ESO325-G004, cannot yet constrain the regular-core scale $\ell$. In the strong-deflection regime, for Sgr A* and M87*, the asymptotic position $θ_{\infty}$ is identical to Schwarzschild's. Nevertheless, $\ell$ modifies strong-lensing coefficients $\bar a, \bar b$, influencing angular separations s, relative flux ratio $r_\mathrm{mag}$, and time delays $ΔT_{2,1}$. Our predicted values for these observables remain consistent with current data, suggesting that future high-precision measurements of strong-field lensing may distinguish Hayward-like from Schwarzschild black holes.

### [28] [Probing bulk geometry via pole skipping: from static to rotating spacetimes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14638)
*Cheng Ran,Zhenkang Lu,Shao-Feng Wu*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究扩展了基于极点跳跃（pole-skipping）数据重建体几何（bulk geometry）的解析框架，从静态平面对称黑洞推广到静态拓扑黑洞和旋转黑洞，并建立了真空爱因斯坦方程与边界数据之间的代数关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前方法仅能重建静态平面对称黑洞的视界附近度规导数，本研究旨在将该框架系统性地扩展到更复杂的几何结构，包括静态拓扑黑洞和旋转黑洞，以完善从边界数据重建体几何的算法。

Method: 对于三维旋转黑洞，完全从边界极点跳跃数据重建度规；对于四维旋转时空（如Kerr族），标准近视界极点跳跃重建径向度规函数，引入"角向极点跳跃（angular pole-skipping）"通过近轴分析重建角向度规函数。

Result: 三维旋转黑洞的度规可完全重建；四维旋转时空的径向度规函数成功重建，角向度规函数通过新引入的角向极点跳跃方法完成重建。真空爱因斯坦方程可重写为支配极点跳跃数据的代数方程组，零能条件（null energy condition）对该边界数据施加代数不等式约束。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了完整的几何重建算法，揭示了体几何在边界数据中的高度冗余编码特性，并发现了由度规重建的超定性质决定的一般多项式约束，尽管角向极点跳跃的精确全息对应词典（holographic dictionary）仍是开放问题。

Abstract: We investigate an analytical framework for reconstructing bulk geometries from pole-skipping data. Previously, this method enabled the recursive recovery of near-horizon metric derivatives in static, planar-symmetric black holes. Building on this framework, we systematically extend it to more intricate geometries, specifically static topological black holes and rotating black holes. For three-dimensional rotating black holes, we demonstrate that the metric can be fully reconstructed from boundary pole-skipping data. For four-dimensional rotating spacetimes admitting a separable coordinate system (such as the Kerr family), standard near-horizon pole-skipping successfully reconstructs the purely radial metric functions. To recover the remaining angular metric functions, we introduce a mathematical counterpart termed "angular pole-skipping," defined via a near-axis analysis. Although its precise holographic dictionary remains an open question, this bulk-side formalism completes the geometric reconstruction algorithm. Furthermore, we demonstrate that the vacuum Einstein equations can be recast as a set of algebraic equations governing the pole-skipping data and that the null energy condition imposes algebraic inequalities on this boundary data. Finally, we establish general polynomial constraints dictated by the overdetermined nature of the metric reconstruction, highlighting the highly redundant encoding of bulk geometry in boundary data.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: We construct an analytic geodesic-optics description of quasinormal ringing, black-hole shadows, strong lensing, and grey-body factors for the static spherical metric introduced in Eq.~(9) of Ref.~\cite{BakopoulosEtAl2024}. These invariants are then employed within the Schutz--Will WKB approach to obtain eikonal quasinormal frequencies, mapped to shadow and strong-deflection observables through exact identities for static spherical geometries, and used to build a closed analytic form for the transmission probability $Γ_\ell(ω)$. At leading eikonal order, these relations are controlled by null geodesics and are therefore spin-universal for test scalar/electromagnetic/gravitational sectors, up to subleading corrections. Besides the standard ringdown--shadow correspondence, we present three additional results: (i) an explicit quality-factor correction, (ii) limiting core-size expansions that show when damping ratios are nearly insensitive to the scalarized core, and (iii) a comparative study of grey-body factors for moderate multipoles ($\ell=3,4$) and several core-size ratios. ### [31] [On measuring the Quantum Universe](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15130)
*David Vasak,Johannes Kirsch,Juergen Struckmeier*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文将惠勒-德威特（WDW）量子宇宙学方法扩展到含挠率（torsion）的引力理论，通过经典哈密顿力学描述FLRW宇宙动力学，引入弱测量（weak measurement）避免宇宙波函数坍缩，并探讨了德布罗意-玻姆（de Broglie-Bohm）解释及其边界条件问题。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 宇宙波函数表现为量子哈密顿量本征函数的叠加，其中宇宙时间是其本征值（空间曲率）的共轭变量。研究处理了标准哥本哈根量子理论中的坍缩假设，并引入了有效波函数的德布罗意-玻姆（de Broglie-Bohm）解释，同时探讨了波函数和玻姆引导方程的边界条件问题。

Conclusion: 论文建立了含挠率引力理论中扩展WDW量子宇宙学的理论框架，通过弱测量和德布罗意-玻姆解释解决了宇宙波函数的测量问题。相应的数值计算将在后续论文中发表，为量子宇宙学的进一步发展提供了理论基础。

Abstract: We present a theoretical analysis of the WDW approach to quantum cosmology extended to gravity theories with torsion. The dynamics of the FLRW universe is formulated as a classical Hamiltonian problem of point particle mechanics. Unlike in the WDW formalism, the Hamiltonian is not zero, though, and the 3rd quantization does not enforce the cosmic time to vanish. The wave function of the Universe appears as a superposition of eigenfunctions of the quantum Hamiltonian with the cosmic time being the conjugate to its eigenvalues, spatial curvatures. The notion of weak measurement is then introduced to avoid the collapse of the total universal wave function upon measurements of the parameter set describing matter and spacetime. The collapse postulate of the standard Copenhagen quantum theory is discussed and the de Broglie-Bohm interpretation of the effective wave function introduced. The question of the boundary conditions for both, the wave function and the Bohmian guidance equation, is addressed. The corresponding numerical calculations will be published in a separate paper.

### [32] [Static Tidal Perturbations of Relativistic Stars: Corrected Center Expansion and Love Numbers-I](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15195)
*Emel Altas,Ercan Kilicarslan,Onur Oktay,Bayram Tekin*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在解决标准四极矩公式中的两个技术问题：修正内部偶宇称主函数的正则中心Frobenius展开系数，并将静态偶宇称形式体系扩展到Schwarzschild-de Sitter背景。

Method: 推导了内部偶宇称主函数的正则中心Frobenius展开，获得了修正的次领头阶系数；推导了Schwarzschild-de Sitter背景上的静态偶宇称主方程；展示了Regge-Wheeler规范中一般内部偶宇称系统如何约化为Love数计算中使用的标准四极矩方程。

Result: 修正的中心系数仅影响次领头阶初始数据，在数值精度内不影响提取的Love数k₂；将静态偶宇称形式体系成功扩展到Schwarzschild-de Sitter背景，为标准的四极矩问题提供了正则中心输入。

Conclusion: 这些结果修正了标准四极矩问题中的正则中心输入，并将静态偶宇称形式体系扩展到具有两个视界的Schwarzschild-de Sitter几何背景。

Abstract: We revisit static tidal perturbations of relativistic stars with emphasis on two technical issues in the standard quadrupolar formulation. First, we derive the regular-center Frobenius expansion of the interior even-parity master function and obtain a corrected subleading coefficient, which differs from the expression commonly used in the literature. Second, we derive the static even-parity master equation on a Schwarzschild-de Sitter background, extending the usual asymptotically flat problem to a two-horizon geometry. To place these results on a common footing, we also show how the general interior even-parity system in Regge-Wheeler gauge reduces to the standard quadrupolar equation used in Love-number calculations. Numerical integrations for polytropic equations of state show that the corrected center coefficient affects only subleading initial data and leaves the extracted Love number $k_2$ unchanged within numerical accuracy. Taken together, these results fix the regular-center input to the standard quadrupolar problem and extend the static even-parity formalism to Schwarzschild-de Sitter backgrounds.

</details>


### [33] [Boson star-black hole binaries: initial data and head-on collisions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15240)
*Zhuan Ning*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究通过数值相对论方法分析了可比较质量玻色子星-黑洞（BS-BH）对头碰撞，改进了初始数据构造方法以抑制非物理振荡，并揭示了引力波辐射特性：等质量情况下辐射能量随玻色子星致密性增加而增加，不等质量情况下高阶多极矩模式可作为区分混合系统与纯黑洞双星的关键观测特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用数值相对论（numerical-relativity）方法，通过引入单体共形因子修正（one-body conformal-factor correction）改进初始数据构造，对比分析了等质量和不等质量BS-BH双星系统的引力波辐射，并与匹配的BS-BS和BH-BH基线进行对比。

Result: 改进的初始数据构造方法有效抑制了非物理径向振荡；等质量情况下，BS-BH系统的辐射能量随玻色子星致密性增加而增加，高度致密星体接近BH-BH极限；不等质量情况下，主导(2,0)模式通常接近BH-BH形态，而非主导(3,0)模式在黑洞为较重伴星时具有显著区分能力。

Conclusion: 高阶多极矩（higher multipoles）是区分混合玻色子星-黑洞并合与纯黑洞双星的关键可观测特征，为未来引力波天文学中识别奇异致密天体提供了重要理论指导。

Abstract: We present a numerical-relativity study of comparable-mass boson star-black hole (BS-BH) head-on collisions, focusing on both initial-data construction and gravitational-wave (GW) phenomenology. We show that plain superposition can strongly perturb the BS core, leading to large constraint violations and unphysical radial oscillations. To remedy this problem, we introduce a one-body conformal-factor correction and find that it robustly suppresses these artifacts. Using the improved initial data, we analyze GW emission from equal- and unequal-mass BS-BH binaries and compare with matched BS-BS and BH-BH baselines. For equal masses, the BS-BH radiated energy increases with BS compactness and approaches the BH-BH limit for highly compact stars. For unequal masses, the dominant $(2,0)$ mode often remains close to the BH-BH morphology, whereas the subdominant $(3,0)$ mode provides clear discriminatory power when the BH is the heavier companion. Our results identify higher multipoles as a key observable for distinguishing mixed BS-BH mergers from pure BH binaries.

### [34] [Taming the Aretakis instability: extremal black holes with multi-degenerate horizons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15260)
*Shreyansh Agrawal,Panagiotis Charalambous,Laura Donnay,Stefano Liberati,Giulio Neri*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了黑洞视界的退化程度与Aretakis不稳定性之间的关系，发现随着视界退化阶数的增加，Aretakis不稳定性减弱，并提出了具有无限退化视界的新型黑洞几何结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在理解退化视界（degenerate horizons）的特性及其相关的Aretakis不稳定性。在极端黑洞中，虽然质量膨胀（mass inflation）不存在，但会出现Aretakis不稳定性，这促使研究者探索视界退化程度如何影响这种动力学不稳定性。

Method: 通过研究具有逐渐增高的视界退化阶数（increasingly higher-order horizon degeneracy）的示例，分析退化程度与Aretakis不稳定性的关系。基于这些结果，提出了一种具有无限退化视界（infinitely degenerate horizon）的新型黑洞几何结构。

Result: 研究发现Aretakis不稳定性随着视界退化程度（degree of degeneracy）的增加而减弱。这表明更高阶的退化视界具有更强的稳定性特征。

Conclusion: 具有无限退化视界的黑洞几何结构在Aretakis型扰动下可能是稳定的，这可能为实现这些物体的"墓地"终态（"graveyard" end state）提供了具体实例。

Abstract: Stationary black hole geometries with non-degenerate Cauchy horizons are classically unstable due to mass inflation. At extremality, mass inflation is absent, but a different dynamical instability arises: the Aretakis instability. In this work, we investigate the properties of degenerate horizons and their associated Aretakis instabilities. By studying examples with increasingly higher-order horizon degeneracy, we show that the Aretakis instability weakens as the degree of degeneracy grows. Motivated by these results, we propose a new black hole geometry characterized by an infinitely degenerate horizon, which we argue is stable under Aretakis-type perturbations and may therefore provide a concrete realization of a "graveyard" end state for these objects.

</details>

### [35] [Controlled Loop Expansion for the Topological Heavy Fermion Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14278)
*Yaar Vituri,Erez Berg*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文为魔角扭曲双层石墨烯中的拓扑重费米子模型建立了一个可控理论框架，通过追踪局域电子得到传导电子的有效作用量，并利用小杂化相空间参数进行可控环路展开，获得了准粒子寿命和味磁化率等非微扰结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在为魔角扭曲双层石墨烯（magic-angle twisted bilayer graphene）中的拓扑重费米子模型（topological heavy fermion model）建立一个可控的理论框架。该模型中低密度传导电子与强相互作用的f-位点晶格杂化，需要发展能够处理这种复杂相互作用的理论方法。

Method: 通过追踪局域电子（tracing out the localized electrons），推导出传导电子的有效作用量（effective action），该作用量包含由单f-位点问题的关联函数构建的长程时间有效相互作用。识别出小杂化相空间参数（small hybridization-phase-space parameter），从而实现了可控的环路展开（controlled loop expansion），使得能够在相互作用强度或杂化强度方面推导非微扰结果。

Result: 在树图水平上，结果等价于Hubbard I近似。在更高环路阶次上，推导出两个适用于温度高于味有序温度（flavor ordering temperature）且低于在位充电能量（on-site charging energy）的关键结果：1）准粒子寿命（quasi-particle lifetime），2）系统的味磁化率（flavor susceptibility）。值得注意的是，尽管系统具有强相互作用，但发现磁化率在参数上接近居里温度时精确遵循居里-外斯定律（Curie-Weiss law）。

Conclusion: 本文成功为拓扑重费米子模型开发了一个可控理论框架，通过小杂化相空间参数实现可控环路展开，获得了包括准粒子寿命和味磁化率在内的非微扰结果。特别重要的是，发现强相互作用系统的磁化率在接近居里温度时仍遵循居里-外斯定律，这为理解魔角扭曲双层石墨烯的物理性质提供了重要理论工具。

Abstract: We develop a controlled theoretical framework for the topological heavy fermion model relevant to magic-angle twisted bilayer graphene, where low density conduction electrons hybridize with a lattice of strongly interacting f-sites. By tracing out the localized electrons, we derive an effective action for the conduction electrons with long-range in time effective interactions, built from correlators of the single f-site problem. We identify a small hybridization-phase-space parameter resulting in a controlled loop expansion, enabling the derivation of nonperturbative results in either the interaction or the hybridization strength. To tree-level, the results are equivalent to the Hubbard I approximation. At higher loop order, we derive two key results applicable to temperatures above the flavor ordering temperature and below the on-site charging energy: 1) the quasi-particle lifetime, 2) the flavor susceptibility of the system. Remarkably, despite being strongly interacting, we find the susceptibility to accurately obey a Curie-Weiss law parametrically close to the Curie temperature.

</details>


### [36] [Divergent spin conductivity on the verge of ferromagnetic quantum criticality](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14286)
*Sondre Duna Lundemo,Asle Sudbø*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探索金属在接近铁磁量子临界点（ferromagnetic quantum critical point）时自旋输运性质的异常行为，特别是自旋电导率（spin conductivity）的发散性修正，这构成了超导体反常电导率（paraconductivity）理论的自旋类比。

Method: 采用线性响应理论（linear response）推导自旋电流，并在高斯近似水平（Gaussian-level treatment）下处理具有易平面磁各向异性（easy-plane magnetic anisotropy）系统的有效作用量（effective action）。通过验证沃德恒等式（Ward identity）和正常态自旋刚度（spin stiffness）消失来确认理论自洽性。

Result: 研究显示自旋电导率在接近铁磁量子临界点时存在发散性涨落修正，这一临界增强效应被解释为量子临界区域中初生的自旋超流性（incipient spin superfluidity）。基于易平面铁磁体的电流环表示（current-loop representation）提供了直观物理图像支持。

Conclusion: 自旋电导率的临界增强效应构成了Aslamazov-Larkin反常电导率理论的自旋类比，预示着量子临界区域中自旋超流性的出现，为理解铁磁量子临界点附近的自旋输运行为提供了新视角。

Abstract: We show that the spin conductivity of a metal approaching a ferromagnetic quantum critical point exhibits divergent fluctuation corrections. This effect arises from critical spin fluctuations and constitutes a spin analog of the Aslamazov-Larkin theory of paraconductivity in superconductors. The spin current is derived in linear response within a Gaussian-level treatment of the effective action for a system with easy-plane magnetic anisotropy. We demonstrate the consistency of our spin transport theory by showing that it (i) fulfills the Ward identity and (ii) yields vanishing spin stiffness in the normal state. The critical enhancement of the spin conductivity is interpreted as incipient spin superfluidity in the quantum critical region. This is further supported by an intuitive picture based on the current-loop representation of the easy-plane ferromagnet.
