### [37] [Quantum Charge-4e Superconductivity and Deconfined Pseudocriticality in the Attractive SU(4) Hubbard Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14289)
*Zhou-Quan Wan,Huan Jiang,Xuan Zou,Shiwei Zhang,Shao-Kai Jian*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究通过量子蒙特卡洛模拟发现，在SU(4)哈伯德模型中存在电荷-4e超导相，并揭示了从电荷-2e到电荷-4e超导的相变具有非传统的分数化特征，可通过Sp(4)规范-希格斯理论描述。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 电荷-4e超导体（charge-4e superconductor）作为电子四重态（electron quartets）的长程相干系统，在零温下的明确实现案例仍然稀少。研究旨在探索SU(4)哈伯德模型中电荷-4e超导性的存在及其相变特征。

Method: 采用数值精确的大规模量子蒙特卡洛（quantum Monte Carlo, QMC）模拟方法，克服了主要技术障碍，研究了吸引性SU(4)哈伯德模型的零温相图。

Result: 研究识别出电荷-2e和电荷-4e超导相，随着相互作用增强，电荷-2e关联被抑制并最终消失，而电荷-4e关联保持稳健且随系统尺寸收敛。相变过程中单电子保持能隙，但电荷-2e关联表现出与传统朗道描述不一致的标度行为。

Conclusion: 研究建立了电荷-4e超导性作为真实的零温相，为未来数值精确框架下的研究提供了简单模型，并揭示了通向超导临界性的非传统路径。通过Sp(4)规范-希格斯理论实现了希格斯（电荷-2e）相与禁闭（电荷-4e）相之间的去禁闭量子伪临界性。

Abstract: Unlike conventional charge-2e superconductors, a charge-4e superconductor exhibits long-range coherence of electron quartets rather than Cooper pairs. Clear zero-temperature realizations of charge-4e superconductivity remain rare. Here, we investigate the zero-temperature phase diagram of the attractive SU(4) Hubbard model with numerically exact, large-scale quantum Monte Carlo (QMC) simulations overcoming major technical hurdles. We identify both charge-2e and charge-4e superconducting phases. Upon increasing interaction, charge-2e correlations are suppressed and eventually vanish, while the charge-4e correlations remain robust and converge with system size, signaling the onset of a quartet-condensed phase. Interestingly, across the charge-2e--charge-4e transition, single electrons remain gapped, while charge-2e correlations exhibit a scaling behavior inconsistent with a conventional Landau description. These features are naturally captured by a fractionalized framework in which the physical charge-2e order parameter is a composite field coupled to an emergent non-Abelian gauge structure. We formulate an Sp(4) gauge-Higgs theory that realizes deconfined quantum pseudocriticality between the Higgs (charge-2e) phase and the confined (charge-4e) phase. The Sp(4) gauge-Higgs theory yields pseudocriticality through a fixed-point collision, and its one-loop collision-point exponents quantitatively track the QMC results. Our results establish charge-4e superconductivity as a bona fide zero-temperature phase, provide a simple model for future studies in a numerically exact framework, and reveal an unconventional route to superconducting criticality.

</details>


### [38] [Limits of validity for Migdal-Eliashberg theory: role of polarons/bi-polarons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14293)
*Nikolay Prokof'ev,Ilya Esterlis,Artem Abanov,Andrey Chubukov*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究挑战了传统观点，发现在电子-声子系统中，极化子/双极化子态在声子软化前就会出现，特别是在三维弱耦合情况下。系统通过中间伪隙型混合态演化，最终接近原子极限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统观点认为，在Migdal-Eliashberg理论描述的电子-声子系统中，费米液体态在声子软化前保持稳定。本研究旨在验证这一假设，探索在声子软化前是否存在其他量子态。

Method: 以Holstein模型为原型系统，采用变分方法和解析分析。研究覆盖三维和二维系统中的广泛填充范围，分析不同耦合强度下的相变行为。

Result: 在三维和二维的广泛填充范围内，极化子/双极化子态在声子软化前出现；在三维小填充情况下，弱耦合时即发生此现象。系统通过中间伪隙型混合态演化，其中部分费米子恢复费米液体行为，但Luttinger定理被破坏。

Conclusion: 费米液体态在声子软化前的稳定性假设不成立，极化子/双极化子态更早出现。系统演化路径包括伪隙型混合态，最终在强耦合下密度态逐渐接近原子极限形式。

Abstract: It is widely believed that in an adiabatic limit a Fermi liquid state of an electron-phonon system described by Migdal-Eliashberg theory remains stable before a dressed phonon softens. Using Holstein model as a prototypical example and variational/analytic considerations we demonstrate that in a wide range of fillings both in 3D and 2D, a polaronic/bi-polaronic state emerges before phonon softening; at small filling in 3D this happens already at weak coupling. We show that a polaronic/bi-polaronic state emerges, upon increasing coupling, via an intermediate pseudogap-type mixed state, in which some fermions regain Fermi liquid behavior, yet Luttinger theorem is broken. At even larger couplings the density of states gradually approaches its form in the atomic limit.

</details>


### [39] [Breakdown of the Migdal-Eliashberg theory for electron-phonon systems. Role of polarons/bi-polarons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14294)
*Andrey Chubukov,Ilya Esterlis,Artem Abanov,Nikolay Prokof'ev*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文挑战了传统观点，证明Migdal-Eliashberg理论（MET）在强耦合下会因极化子/双极化子基态的形成而失效，而非仅在声子谱软化时失效。研究建立了FL态向极化子态转变的严格耦合上限，并揭示了密度依赖的相变序列。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统观点认为Migdal-Eliashberg理论（MET）在强耦合下仍然有效，仅在声子谱软化时失效。本研究旨在挑战这一观点，探索另一种可能性：系统向极化子/双极化子（polaron/bipolaron）基态的塌缩，这一现象在一般电子密度下从未被精确量化分析。

Method: 采用数值和解析相结合的方法，通过变分考虑建立严格的上界。基于从在位Holstein模型（on-site Holstein model）精确图解法中提取的线索，进行解析推理，特别关注自旋极化情况。

Result: 在低密度和近最大密度时，FL态向极化子/双极化子态的转变发生在声子谱软化之前。在3D系统中，该转变的耦合上限在低密度或近满密度时趋于零。接近半填充时，增加耦合首先导致电荷密度波（charge-density-wave, CDW）态，MET在接近该不稳定性时存在强耦合区域。

Conclusion: 极化子形成发生在能量与带宽相当的费米子中，超出了MET的适用范围。在CDW有序态之外，极化子/双极化子态在更大耦合下形成，并在一定耦合范围内继承CDW序。

Abstract: The Migdal-Eliashberg theory (MET) describes electrons interacting with phonons in the adiabatic limit when the phonon Debye frequency is much smaller than the Fermi energy. A conventional belief is that MET holds even at strong coupling, when electron self-energy is large, and breaks down only near the point where the dressed phonon spectrum softens to near zero. We analyze numerically and analytically a different option -- collapse to a polaronic/bipolaronic ground state. The last scenario has never been analyzed in precise quantitative terms for a generic electron density. Using variational considerations, we establish rigorous upper bounds on the coupling $λ$, at which a FL state transforms into the bipolaron/polaron state. We show that at small and near-maximum densities, this happens well before a dressed phonon softens. This is true both in 2D and 3D systems; in the latter the upper bound on $λ$ tends to zero in the limit of small or near-full density. We present analytical reasoning for this behavior based on hints extracted from exact diagrammatic treatment of the on-site Holstein model for the spin polarized case and argue that polarons are produced by fermions with energies comparable to the bandwidth; i.e., polaron formation is outside the realm of MET. Closer to half-filling, the leading instability upon increasing $λ$ is towards a charge-density-wave state (CDW), and there exists a strong coupling regime of MET near this instability, while the polaron/bipolaron state develops at larger $λ$ out of a CDW-ordered state and inherits a CDW order over some range of coupling.

</details>


### [40] [Topologically non-trivial gap function and topology-induced time-reversal symmetry breaking in a superconductor with singular dynamical interaction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14295)
*Yue Yu,Andrey V. Chubukov*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究展示了在具有奇异动力学相互作用的模型中，添加有限截断的排斥型哈伯德相互作用可在特定参数范围内选择原本次要的拓扑非平凡配对态，导致拓扑诱导的时间反演对称性破缺中间相。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 目前研究显示，在具有奇异频率依赖性的有效四费米子相互作用系统中，拓扑平凡解通常具有最低能量。本研究旨在探索如何选择原本次要的拓扑非平凡配对态，以理解拓扑非平凡超导态的实现机制。

Method: 采用最小模型方法，在具有奇异动力学相互作用的模型中引入有限截断的排斥型哈伯德相互作用（repulsive Hubbard-type interaction），分析不同参数范围内配对态的能量竞争关系。

Result: 研究发现，在特定参数范围内，添加有限截断的排斥型哈伯德相互作用会选择原本次要的拓扑非平凡解。拓扑平凡与非平凡能隙函数之间的转变必然通过具有拓扑诱导的时间反演对称性破缺（topology-induced breaking of time-reversal symmetry）的中间相发生。

Conclusion: 通过引入有限截断的排斥相互作用，可以实现从拓扑平凡到拓扑非平凡配对态的转变，这一转变过程必然伴随拓扑诱导的时间反演对称性破缺中间相，为设计拓扑非平凡超导态提供了新途径。

Abstract: In many strongly correlated electron systems, non-Fermi liquid behavior and unconventional superconductivity can be viewed as emerging from an effective 4-fermion interaction with a singular frequency dependence. A pairing instability in such a system is qualitatively different from that in a Fermi liquid and generally gives rise to multiple pairing states with topologically distinct gap functions. However, in the systems studied so far, a topologically trivial solution has the lowest energy. Here we show that a repulsive Hubbard-type interaction with a finite cutoff added to a model with a singular dynamical interaction selects, in some parameter range, the theretofore subleading, topologically nontrivial solution. We consider a minimal model that displays this behavior and show that the transformation between the topologically trivial and nontrivial gap functions necessarily occurs via an intermediate phase with topology-induced breaking of time-reversal symmetry.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用拓扑重费米子模型（topological heavy-fermion model）捕捉魔角双层石墨烯的强关联和能带拓扑特性。在可解极限（fc杂化和Hund耦合缺失）附近进行微扰处理，获得单粒子自能（single-particle self-energy）的解析结果。

Result: 推导出Hubbard带激发和低能狄拉克模式的色散重整化（dispersion renormalization）和散射率的显式表达式。分析发现Gamma3和Gamma1,2两类狄拉克电子的散射源于不同机制，并简要研究了应变效应。

Conclusion: 建立了一个分析框架来理解魔角双层石墨烯中的关联激发，并将解析表达式与同一模型的动力学平均场理论（DMFT）结果进行比较验证。

Abstract: Twisted bilayer graphene near integer fillings hosts correlated single-particle excitations whose dispersion and linewidth are increasingly accessible experimentally. We study these excitations using the topological heavy-fermion model, which captures both strong correlations and band topology of twisted bilayer graphene. In the decoupled limit, where both the single-particle fc hybridization and the Hund coupling between f and c electrons are absent, the model admits exact solutions in which free Dirac fermions coexist with interacting f electrons that form zero-width Hubbard bands. By treating the fc hybridization and Hund coupling perturbatively around this solvable limit, we obtain analytical results for the single-particle self-energy. From the resulting self-energy, we derive explicit expressions for both dispersion renormalization and scattering rates of both Hubbard-band excitations and low-energy Dirac modes, thereby establishing an analytical framework for understanding correlated excitations in twisted bilayer graphene. We analyze the scattering of the two kinds, Gamma3 and Gamma1,2, of Dirac electrons and find that they arise from different mechanisms. We also briefly investigate the effect of strain. Finally, we compare these analytical expressions with DMFT results for the same model.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于广义相干态形式化（generalized coherent state formalism）和Simon-Lieb量子配分函数界限，构建计算高维不可约扇区态密度的通用框架。该方法依赖于一般基础对称性，而非特定模型细节。

Result: 以Lipkin-Meshkov-Glick（LMG）模型为测试平台，成功识别了跨自旋扇区的量子相变（QPTs）和激发态量子相变（ESQPTs）。应用于具有幂律相互作用的铁磁横向场伊辛链，发现其最高自旋扇区态密度与LMG型哈密顿量在定性上相同。

Abstract: We develop a general framework to calculate the many-body density of states (DOS) of isolated and interacting quantum systems. Based on the generalized coherent state formalism and the Simon-Lieb bounds for a quantum partition function, our method provides a general method of calculation for the DOS in high-dimensional irreducible sectors. This framework further provides rigorous bounds for the ground state energy in each sector and enables the calculation of microcanonical observables across the entire spectrum. Using the Lipkin-Meshkov-Glick (LMG) model as a test bed, we validate our framework by successfully identifying quantum phase transitions (QPTs) and excited-state quantum phase transitions (ESQPTs) across spin sectors. Unlike existing model-specific numerical or analytical techniques, our formalism relies on general underlying symmetries, making it broadly applicable. Applying our method to the ferromagnetic transverse field Ising chain with power law interactions, we demonstrate that its highest-spin-sector DOS is qualitatively identical to that of LMG-type Hamiltonians. Our work establishes a versatile and computationally efficient bridge between algebraic structure and many-body thermodynamics.

### [43] [Lifetime and spectral function of topological heavy fermions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14369)
*Nemin Wei,Felix von Oppen,Leonid I. Glazman*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究发展了一种解析理论来描述扭曲双层石墨烯中莫特半金属（Mott semimetal）的准粒子色散和寿命，揭示了强关联与非平凡量子几何共同作用下的非常规谱特性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 扭曲双层石墨烯（twisted bilayer graphene）为探索电子拓扑与强关联的相互作用提供了范式平台。在拓扑重费米子模型（topological heavy fermion model）中，拓扑与电子相互作用通过巡游c电子和局域f电子带之间的弱杂化（hybridization）相结合，这促使了莫特半金属相在电荷中性点以上温度存在的理论提议。

Method: 研究将相互作用的平带哈密顿量（flat-band Hamiltonian）重新表述为一组非正交轨道上的在位哈伯德相互作用（on-site Hubbard interaction）。使用运动方程方法（equation-of-motion method）计算电子格林函数（electron Green's function），类似于哈伯德-III近似（Hubbard-III approximation），但该近似在理论中受一个明确定义的小参数控制。

Result: 计算了电子自能（electron self-energy），证明了明确定义的低能准粒子（low-energy quasiparticles）的出现，其色散和弛豫率与相互作用强度成正比。准粒子谱在能量和动量上都能很好分辨，直至非常接近费米能级（Fermi level）。

Conclusion: 研究结果阐明了由强关联和非平凡量子几何（nontrivial quantum geometry）产生的非常规谱特性，对量子扭转显微镜（quantum twisting microscope）等光谱探测实验具有直接相关性。

Abstract: Twisted bilayer graphene provides a paradigmatic platform for exploring the interplay between electronic topology and strong correlations. Within the topological heavy fermion model [Song and Bernevig, Phys. Rev. Lett. 129, 047601 (2022)], topology and electron interactions are brought together by including a weak hybridization between the bands of itinerant $c$- and localized $f$-electrons. Hybridization infuses concentrated Berry curvature into the $f$-band, while leaving it flat. These band features have motivated recent proposals of a Mott semimetal phase above the flavor-ordering temperature at charge neutrality. In this work, we develop an analytic theory of the quasiparticle dispersion and lifetime in the Mott semimetal. We reformulate the interacting flat-band Hamiltonian as an on-site Hubbard interaction defined on a set of non-orthogonal orbitals, and compute the electron Green's function using the equation-of-motion method, in close analogy with the Hubbard-III approximation. Unlike the conventional Hubbard model, in our case this approximation is controlled by a well-defined small parameter in the theory. We evaluate the electron self-energy and demonstrate the emergence of well-defined low-energy quasiparticles with the dispersion and relaxation rate proportional to the interaction strength. The quasiparticle spectrum is well-resolved in energy and in momentum down to the very vicinity of the Fermi level. Our results illustrate unconventional spectral properties arising from strong correlations and nontrivial quantum geometry, and have direct relevance for spectroscopic probes such as quantum twisting microscope experiments.

### [44] [Two pathways to break the insulating state in a correlated transition metal oxide](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14415)
*Joel Kuttruff,Ritwika Mandal,Marina Servol,Céline Mariette,Hiroko Tokoro,Shin-ichi Ohkoshi,Rodolphe Sopracase,Hervé Cailleau,Laurent Cario,Etienne Janod,Maciej Lorenc,Vinh Ta Phuoc*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 关联过渡金属氧化物（correlated transition metal oxides）因其可通过外部刺激调控电子特性而具有器件应用潜力，但其微观机制尚不明确。本研究旨在探究Ti3O5中温度与压力驱动的电子态演化起源。

Method: 研究结合温度与压力调控，通过光学光谱（optical spectroscopy）等手段分析Ti3O5的电子结构变化，重点关注钛二聚体（titanium dimers）的轨道选择性价键（orbital selective valence bonds）行为。

Result: 室温绝缘相由两种钛二聚体形成的一维之字形链（one-dimensional zig-zag chains）构成，具有轨道选择性价键。热相变时一种二聚体解离，导致绝缘体-金属相变（insulator to metal transition）并伴随显著的轨道重布居（orbital repopulation）。压力驱动相变则源于二聚体内与二聚体间跳跃（intra- and inter-dimer hopping）的竞争。

Conclusion: Ti3O5是典型的关联过渡金属氧化物，其电子态演化需同时考虑电子关联（electronic correlations）与轨道相互作用（orbital interactions）。压力诱导的金属相变机制与已知相变完全不同，揭示了新的物理现象。

Abstract: Correlated transition metal oxides present exciting prospects as switches or memory and storage devices owing to the possibility to control electronic properties using various external stimuli. While their complex behaviour is known to stem from interplay between electronic correlations, atomic structure and orbital physics, they remain poorly understood on the microscopic level. Here, we investigate such origins as a function of temperature and pressure in the transition metal oxide Ti3O5. We find that the insulating room-temperature phase is characterized by one-dimensional zig-zag chains composed by two types of titanium dimers forming orbital selective valence bonds. At the thermal phase transition, one type of titanium dimer breaks up, resulting in an insulator to metal transition with a large orbital repopulation between the two states. Moreover, optical spectroscopy reveals that an additional pressure-driven insulator to metal transition occurs in Ti3O5 at room temperature. The phenomenology of this novel pressure-induced metallic transition is completely different from the insofar studied transitions and results from a competition between intra- and inter-dimer hopping. Our combined results suggest that Ti3O5 is a prototypical correlated transition metal oxide, where both correlations as well as orbital interactions need to be considered to fully understand the evolution of the electronic states.

### [45] [The Two Orbital, Interacting Hatano-Nelson Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14533)
*Jonah Huang,Rubem Mondaini,Nancy Aggarwal,Richard Scalettar*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文研究具有非厄米性（non-Hermiticity）的二维链（two-chain）哈伯德模型（Hubbard model）中纯实数谱（purely real spectrum）的存在条件及其稳定性。通过分析相互作用强度、非厄米程度和链间跃迁（interchain hopping）对谱性质的影响，探索了周期性边界条件（PBC）双粒子态（doublon states）与开放边界条件（OBC）皮肤模（skin modes）的关系，并利用林德布拉德演化（Lindbladian evolution）验证了非厄米描述在低填充下的定性有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Hatano-Nelson哈密顿量（Hatano-Nelson Hamiltonian）为理解由左右跃迁不对称引起的非厄米性（non-Hermiticity）及其与局域化（localization）的联系提供了深刻见解。本文旨在探索在具有厄米链间跃迁（Hermitian interchain hopping）的二维链几何中，自旋ful情况（哈伯德模型）下相互作用双粒子区域（interacting, two-particle sector）中实数本征值（real eigenvalues）的存在条件。

Method: 研究采用二维链（two-chain）几何结构，包含厄米链间跃迁（Hermitian interchain hopping）。通过分析相互作用强度、非厄米程度和链间跃迁对谱性质的影响，构建了纯实数谱（purely real spectrum）存在的"相"图（"phase" diagrams）。利用绕数分析（winding number analysis）研究边界条件敏感性，并探索周期性边界条件双粒子态（PBC doublon states）与开放边界条件皮肤模（OBC skin modes）的关系。

Result: 获得了纯实数谱（purely real spectrum）存在的"相"图（"phase" diagrams），揭示了相互作用强度、非厄米程度和链间跃迁（interchain hopping）对谱性质的影响。通过绕数分析（winding number analysis）表明谱性质对边界条件敏感，并建立了周期性边界条件双粒子态（PBC doublon states）与开放边界条件皮肤模（OBC skin modes）的联系。林德布拉德演化（Lindbladian evolution）计算显示，在低填充条件下，非厄米描述能够定性描述此类非平衡系统（non-equilibrium systems）的动力学稳定性。

Conclusion: 研究表明，在具有厄米链间跃迁（Hermitian interchain hopping）的二维链哈伯德模型（two-chain Hubbard model）中，相互作用、非厄米性和链间跃迁共同决定了纯实数谱（purely real spectrum）的存在条件。非厄米描述在低填充条件下能够定性描述非平衡系统（non-equilibrium systems）的动力学行为，为理解此类系统的稳定性提供了理论框架。

Abstract: The single orbital, one-dimensional, Hatano-Nelson Hamiltonian provides deep insight into the physics of non-Hermiticity, resulting from asymmetric left/right hopping, and its connections to localization. In the absence of disorder, its single particle eigenvalues $E_α$ lie on an ellipse in the complex plane whose extent in the imaginary direction is controlled by the degree of asymmetry. When randomness is introduced, two sets of real eigenvalues emerge at the extremes of the largest and smallest real part of $E_α$. These real eigenvalues are associated with localized eigenvectors. For spinless fermions, increasing near-neighbor interactions first cause a transition to a charge density wave phase, and ultimately, on finite lattices, a collapse of all eigenvalues to the real axis. In this paper, we explore the presence of real eigenvalues in the interacting, two-particle sector for the spinful case (Hubbard model) in a two-chain (two-band) geometry with a Hermitian interchain hopping. Our key results are to obtain the ``phase" diagrams for the existence of a purely real spectrum, as a function of the interaction strength, degree of non-Hermiticity, and interchain hopping. We study the sensitivity to boundary conditions of the spectral properties of our two-chain model with winding number analysis and explore the relationship between PBC doublon states and OBC skin modes. To address the question of stability in such non-equilibrium systems, we solve the dynamics at low filling according to Lindbladian evolution and find that the non-Hermitian description is able to qualitatively describe such systems.

### [46] [Discovery of an odd-parity f-wave charge order in a kagome metal](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14538)

Abstract: The spontaneous breaking of symmetries is a cornerstone of physics, defining the phases of matter from the cosmological scale to the quantum realm. In condensed matter, electronic orders are classified by their behavior under fundamental symmetries like spatial inversion (parity). While even-parity orders, such as conventional superconductivity and charge density waves, are ubiquitous, their odd-parity counterparts--predicted to host exotic phenomena such as gapless quasiparticle excitations and novel collective modes--are comparatively elusive states of quantum matter. Here, using high-resolution scanning tunneling microscopy and angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy on the kagome metal CsV$_3$Sb$_5$, we report the discovery of an inversion symmetry-breaking $f$-wave charge bond order. We show that this phase, which preserves translation symmetry, is stabilized by the spontaneous opening of a spectral gap at a previously overlooked Dirac point, providing a textbook condensed-matter realization of the Gross-Neveu model for dynamical mass generation and parity breaking. Intriguingly, this $f$-wave order is itself a intervening phase, vanishing abruptly below a temperature of 10\,K and pointing to a subsequent transition into a `hidden' electronic state that is invisible to local STM probes. Our findings establish odd-parity charge order as a novel phase of matter, here, embedded within the intricate hierarchy of correlated electronic orders on the kagome lattice.

### [47] [Level statistics of the disordered Haldane-Shastry model with $1/r^α$ interaction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14695)
*Vengatesan Ganapathy,Pranay Patil,Ajit C. Balram*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了长程相互作用自旋系统中无序类型对能级统计和许多体局域化（MBL）的影响。研究发现，单独的位置无序或随机磁场均无法产生纯净的泊松统计，但两者共存时会出现泊松统计，表明MBL的出现需要两种无序类型共同作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解相互作用范围和各种无序类型如何影响多体量子系统的能级统计并导致许多体局域化（many-body localization, MBL）的出现是一个具有挑战性的开放前沿。研究旨在探索长程相互作用系统中不同类型无序对MBL相的影响机制。

Method: 研究采用变体的自旋-1/2 Haldane-Shastry模型，该模型具有1/r^α相互作用（其中α≥0参数化相互作用范围），并在存在位置无序（position disorder）和/或随机磁场（random magnetic fields）的条件下进行。通过分析系统的能级统计特性来研究MBL相的出现。

Result: 研究发现，在这个长程相互作用系统中，单独的位置无序或随机磁场均无法产生纯净的泊松统计（pristine Poisson statistics）。然而，当两种无序类型共存时，泊松统计出现，表明许多体局域化（MBL）在两种无序共存时出现。有趣的是，一旦随机磁场破坏了SU(2)对称性，位置无序的强度δ似乎起着重要作用，这通过以单一参数αδ参数化的无序平均能隙比（disorder-averaged gap ratios）的近似标度坍塌（scaling collapse）得到证实。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明，在长程相互作用的Haldane-Shastry模型中，许多体局域化（MBL）的出现需要位置无序和随机磁场两种无序类型的协同作用。这一发现揭示了不同无序类型在诱导MBL相中的互补作用机制，特别是当SU(2)对称性被破坏时，位置无序强度δ与相互作用范围参数α的乘积αδ成为描述系统行为的关键参数。

Abstract: Understanding how the interaction range and various types of disorder affect the level statistics of many-body quantum systems and lead to the emergence of many-body localization (MBL) is a challenging open frontier. We study the level statistics of a variant of the spin-$1/2$ Haldane-Shastry model with $1/r^α$ interactions, where $α{\geq}0$ parametrizes the range of the interactions, in the presence of position disorder and/or random magnetic fields. We find that neither position disorder nor random magnetic fields alone yields pristine Poisson statistics in this long-range interacting system; however, Poisson statistics emerge in their combined presence, suggesting the emergence of MBL when both types of disorder coexist. Interestingly, once random magnetic fields break the $SU(2)$ symmetry, the strength of the position disorder, $δ$, appears to play an important role, as evidenced by an approximate scaling collapse of the disorder-averaged gap ratios that is parametrized in terms of a single parameter, $αδ$.

</details>


### [48] [Nontrivial three-sublattice magnetization in the easy-axis spin-1/2 XXZ antiferromagnet on the triangular lattice](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14767)
*Masahiro Kadosawa,Masaaki Nakamura,Yukinori Ohta,Satoshi Nishimoto*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 使用密度矩阵重整化群方法研究三角晶格自旋-1/2 XXZ反铁磁体在易轴区的基态磁结构。通过螺旋边界条件避免几何各向异性，发现基态保持非平凡的三亚晶格有序态而非简单的饱和伊辛态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究三角晶格自旋-1/2 XXZ反铁磁体在易轴区（easy-axis regime）的基态磁结构，特别关注量子涨落如何从宏观简并的伊辛流形中选择特定的有序态。

Method: 采用密度矩阵重整化群（density-matrix renormalization group, DMRG）方法，通过施加螺旋边界条件（spiral boundary conditions）将有限L×L簇精确映射到一维链，避免了圆柱几何固有的空间各向异性。

Result: 在易轴区，有序磁矩在较宽的Δ范围内保持接近零磁化的三亚晶格结构形式(2m,-m,-m)。外推至Δ→∞时，正亚晶格磁矩为0.41873，负亚晶格磁矩为0.20832，均低于经典饱和值1/2。Y态在零场下比上下下态更稳定。

Conclusion: 易轴基态并非简单地过渡到平凡的饱和共线伊辛态，而是保持由量子涨落从宏观简并的伊辛流形中选择出的非平凡三亚晶格有序态，Y态是基态的首选构型。

Abstract: We investigate the ground-state magnetic structure of the spin-$1/2$ XXZ antiferromagnet on the triangular lattice in the easy-axis regime using the density-matrix renormalization group. By applying spiral boundary conditions, we exactly map finite $L\times L$ clusters onto one-dimensional chains while avoiding the spatial anisotropy inherent in cylindrical geometries. From symmetry-broken local magnetization profiles, we extract the three-sublattice moments and track their evolution with anisotropy. At the isotropic point, we obtain a positive sublattice moment of $0.21671$, consistent with previous numerical estimates. In the easy-axis regime, the ordered moments remain close to a zero-magnetization three-sublattice structure of the form $(2m,-m,-m)$ over a broad range of $Δ$. Extrapolation in $1/Δ$ shows that the positive sublattice moment stays well below the classical saturation value $1/2$, approaching $0.41873$ as $Δ\to\infty$, while the magnitude of the negative sublattice moment approaches $0.20832$. We further compare the energies of the Y state and the up-down-down state and find that the Y state is favored at zero field. Independent thermodynamic-limit energy calculations, performed without assuming any particular ordered pattern, yield an energy consistent with the Y-state solution. These results show that the easy-axis ground state does not simply cross over to a trivially saturated collinear Ising state, but instead remains a nontrivial three-sublattice ordered state selected from the macroscopically degenerate Ising manifold by quantum fluctuations.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 开发了一种全第一性原理方法，将密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT）与动力学平均场理论（dynamical mean-field theory, DMFT）相结合，用于研究等离激元激发。

Result: 该方法成功调和了Sr₂RuO₄中相互矛盾的电子能量损失谱（electron energy-loss spectroscopy, EELS）结果：电子关联效应再现了等离激元色散，并在电子-空穴连续谱以下产生了较大的本征宽度。还识别出反映非相干特征间跃迁的高能峰，以及等离激元能量-动量色散的急剧增加（类似于光电子能谱中的瀑布效应），这些均为真实的关联效应。

Conclusion: 研究揭示了强关联材料中等离激元激发的新特征，包括本征宽度、高能峰和类瀑布色散行为，这些均为电子关联的直接结果，为理解强关联体系中的集体激发提供了新视角。

Abstract: Plasmon modes, their dispersion, and the onset of damping when approaching the electron-hole continuum are well understood when electron correlations are weak. However, we know little about how this picture is modified and what additional features emerge in strongly correlated materials. Here, we present a fully ab initio approach to plasmon excitations that combines density functional theory with dynamical mean-field theory, and we use it to reconcile controversial electron energy-loss spectroscopy results in Sr$_2$RuO$_4$. In particular, we show that electronic correlations reproduce the plasmon dispersion, while generating a large intrinsic width already below the electron-hole continuum. An additional high-energy peak reflecting transitions between incoherent features and a sharp increase of the plasmon's energy-momentum dispersion, akin to waterfalls in photoemission spectroscopy, are identified as genuine correlation effects.

### [50] [High-temperature charge-4e superconductivity in SU(4) interacting fermions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15056)
*Shao-Hang Shi,Zhengzhi Wu,Jiangping Hu,Zi-Xiang Li*

Method: 研究引入了非人工设计且无符号问题（sign-problem-free）的模型，采用无偏量子蒙特卡洛（quantum Monte Carlo）模拟来研究电荷-4e超导相。通过分析零温和有限温度下的相图，以及超流刚度（superfluid stiffness）的普遍跃变来识别相变。

Result: 在零温下，相图显示电荷-4e超导在强耦合区域是主要的基态。在有限温度且无电荷-2e超导的情况下，通过Berezinskii-Kosterlitz-Thouless（BKT）转变识别了电荷-4e超导，其转变温度Tc随相互作用强度近似线性增加。谱分析揭示了Tc以上的显著赝隙（pseudogap）源于强相位涨落。

Conclusion: 该研究为电荷-4e超导建立了一个规范且数值精确的模型系统，为在莫尔材料（moiré materials）和超冷原子系统（ultracold atomic systems）等实验平台中实现这一相提供了关键指导。

Abstract: The condensation of electron quartets, known as charge-4e superconductivity (SC), represents a novel quantum state of matter beyond the standard paradigm of Cooper pairing. However, concrete microscopic models realizing this phase in two dimensions remain a central challenge. Here, we introduce a non-engineered and sign-problem-free model, unambiguously demonstrating the emergence of a robust and high-temperature charge-4e SC phase using unbiased quantum Monte Carlo simulations. At zero temperature, the phase diagram reveals that charge-4e SC is the primary ground state in the strong-coupling regime. At finite temperature in the absence of charge-2e SC, we identify charge-4e SC through a Berezinskii-Kosterlitz-Thouless transition, marked by a universal jump in the superfluid stiffness consistent with a condensate of charge 4e. Remarkably, the transition temperature Tc increases nearly linearly with interaction strength, providing a robust mechanism for high-Tc quartet superconductivity. Furthermore, spectral analysis reveals a prominent pseudogap above Tc arising from strong phase fluctuations. Our results establish a canonical and numerically exact model system for charge-4e superconductivity, offering crucial guidance for its realization in experimental platforms such as moiré materials and ultracold atomic systems.

### [51] [Universal magnetic energy scale in the doped Fermi-Hubbard model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15234)
*Radu Andrei,Ivan Morera,Jonathan B. Curtis,Immanuel Bloch,Eugene Demler*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究通过自洽形式理论分析掺杂莫特绝缘体（Mott insulators）的磁关联，揭示了一个普适的磁性能量尺度$J^*$，该尺度决定了静态关联、动力学响应以及赝隙（pseudogap）现象的出现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 掺杂莫特绝缘体的磁关联是理解许多量子材料异常特性的关键。最近光学晶格中超冷原子实验为方晶格上费米-哈伯德模型（Fermi-Hubbard model）的磁性性质提供了新信息，需要理论解释这些实验发现。

Method: 采用自洽形式理论描述反铁磁磁振子（antiferromagnetic magnons）与掺杂空穴之间的耦合。通过分析单磁振子和双磁振子（bimagnon）的谱性质，研究有限掺杂下的磁激发。

Result: 发现一个普适的磁性能量尺度$J^*$，它决定了系统的静态关联和动力学响应。该尺度设定了晶格调制光谱中双磁振子峰的出现频率，并控制着赝隙现象的起始（$k_BT^* = c J^*$）。此外，识别出另一个低能尺度控制着奈尔序（Néel order）的稳定性。

Conclusion: 有限掺杂下共线反铁磁相的稳定性可通过引入额外准粒子展宽（如无序或低频噪声）进行实验调控。该分析建立了磁性能量尺度与赝隙现象、相变以及费米子准粒子性质之间的联系。

Abstract: Magnetic correlations of doped Mott insulators hold the key to the unusual characteristics of many quantum materials. Recent experiments with ultracold atoms in optical lattices have provided new information about the magnetic properties of the Fermi-Hubbard model on a square lattice. We demonstrate that recent measurements indicate that a single doping-dependent energy scale determines both static correlations and dynamical response of these systems. To understand these experimental findings, we employ a self-consistent formalism to describe the coupling between antiferromagnetic magnons and doped holes, and we uncover the emergence of a universal magnetic energy scale at finite doping, which we denote by $J^*$. We present the single- and two-magnon spectral properties at finite doping and discuss the appearance of a bimagnon peak in lattice-modulation spectroscopy, at frequencies set by $J^*$. Furthermore, we argue that this same energy scale sets the onset of pseudogap phenomena, leading to the hypothesis $k_BT^* = c J^*$, with $c$ an order one number. We identify another low-energy scale emerging from our analysis of magnetic excitations, and argue that it controls the stability of Néel order at the lowest temperatures, ultimately driving a transition to an incommensurate spin-density-wave at finite doping. We discuss the relation between this low-energy scale and the nature of fermionic quasiparticles. Our analysis suggests that stability of the commensurate antiferromagentic phase at finite doping can be controlled experimentally by introducing additional quasiparticle broadening via disorder or low-frequency noise.

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究Korteweg-de Vries方程在具有特定支撑条件的初始数据下的柯西问题，特别是针对同时满足L¹和L²可积性且支撑在正半线上的实值初始数据。该研究旨在超越标准的短程（short-range）设置，为更广泛的初始数据类提供严格的数学分析框架。

Method: 采用逆散射方法，利用左反射系数（left reflection coefficient）和Hardy空间H²上的Hankel算子。证明基于紧支撑势的近似、远离原点时相关反射系数的一致收敛性，以及所得Hankel算子的连续性性质，从而推导出解的迹型表示（trace-type representation）。

Result: 成功推导出Korteweg-de Vries方程在给定初始条件下的解的迹型表示。建立了对于超越标准短程设置的可积半线支撑初始数据类的严格逆散射构造，为这类初始数据的柯西问题提供了新的解析表示方法。

Conclusion: 该研究为Korteweg-de Vries方程在具有特定支撑和可积性条件的初始数据下提供了严格的数学框架。通过结合反射系数和Hankel算子方法，成功扩展了逆散射技术的适用范围，为处理更广泛的初始数据类奠定了基础。

Abstract: We consider the Cauchy problem for the Korteweg--de Vries equation with real initial data $q$ that is both $L^1$ and $L^2$ summable and supported on (0,\infty). Using the left reflection coefficient and Hankel operators on the Hardy space $H^2$, we derive a trace-type representation for the corresponding solution. The proof is based on approximation by compactly supported potentials, uniform convergence of the associated reflection coefficients away from the origin, and continuity properties of the resulting Hankel operators. This yields a rigorous inverse scattering construction for a class of summable half-line supported initial data beyond the standard short-range setting.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机是推导波前在空间异质性存在下的传播定量判据，理解几何障碍如何影响双稳态反应扩散系统的波前传播行为。

Method: 采用守恒律方法，结合精确的一维行波解，构建了简化的解析模型来预测阻塞阈值。该方法将反应项的积分视为波前的有效驱动力。

Abstract: We investigate numerically the blocking of two-dimensional bistable reaction diffusion fronts by geometric obstacles. Our goal is to derive quantitative criteria for front propagation in the presence of spatial heterogeneities. Combining this insight with the exact one-dimensional traveling wave solution, we construct a reduced analytical model that predicts blocking thresholds. Finally, we extend the analysis to more complex geometries, including checkerboard-like obstacles, and derive simple heuristic rules governing front propagation. ~

Abstract: Affine subgroups having the same Coxeter number with the affine Coxeter groups W(An), W(Dn), and W(En) are constructed by graph folding technique. The affine groups W(Cn) and W(Bn) are obtained from the Coxeter groups W(A2n-1) and W(D2n-1) respectively. The affine groups W(E6), W(D6) and W(E8) lead to the affine groups W(F4), W(H3), and W(H4) respectively by graph folding. ### [58] [Landau damping on expanding backgrounds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14911)
*David Fajman,Liam Urban*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 该研究首次在宇宙学背景下证明了非线性朗道阻尼（Landau damping）现象，分析了牛顿宇宙学膨胀对接近泊松平衡的带电自相互作用等离子体渐近行为的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于分析牛顿宇宙学（Newtonian cosmology）膨胀对接近泊松平衡（Poisson equilibria）的带电自相互作用等离子体渐近行为的影响，探索在宇宙学背景下朗道阻尼现象的存在性。

Method: 方法基于研究在相空间（phase space）中$3$-环面（$3$-torus）上的弗拉索夫-泊松系统（Vlasov-Poisson system），该环面随尺度因子$a(t)$膨胀，其中$a(t)=t^q$且$q\in(0,\frac12)$。

Result: 结果表明，对于相对于适当强Gevrey类（Gevrey class）足够小的初始数据，该系统的解表现出非线性朗道阻尼，即等离子体的电荷密度对比度（charge density contrast）超多项式衰减（decays superpolynomially）。

Conclusion: 这是首个在宇宙学背景下展示朗道阻尼的结果，且发现当$q$在此范围内取值更大时，初始数据要求变得更严格，而衰减则减弱。

Abstract: We analyse the effect of expansion in Newtonian cosmology on the asymptotic behaviour of charged self-interacting plasmas close to Poisson equilibria. To this end, we study the Vlasov-Poisson system on the phase space of a $3$-torus which is expanding with respect to the scale factor $a(t)$. We show that, for $a(t)=t^q$ with $q\in(0,\frac12)$, solutions to this system exhibit nonlinear Landau damping for initial data that is small with respect to a suitably strong Gevrey class, i.e., the charge density contrast of the plasma decays superpolynomially. For larger choices of $q$ within this range, the initial data requirements become stricter while the decay weakens. To our knowledge, this is the first result showing Landau damping in a cosmological setting.

</details>

### [59] [Grading the Unspoken: Evaluating Tacit Reasoning in Quantum Field Theory and String Theory with LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14188)
*Xingyang Yu,Yinghuan Zhang,Yufei Zhang,Zijun Cui*

Main category: physics.comp-ph

TL;DR: 该研究构建了一个量子场论和弦理论领域的专家数据集，并引入五级评分标准来评估大语言模型在高度抽象理论物理问题上的表现，发现模型在稳定概念框架内的显式推导表现良好，但在需要重构隐含推理步骤或重组表示时出现系统性退化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型在数学和物理多个领域展现出优异性能，但能否支持量子场论和弦理论等高度抽象理论研究仍存疑问。评估面临核心挑战：这些领域的正确性是多层次的、隐含的且非二元的，标准答案匹配指标无法捕捉中间概念步骤的重构或隐含结构约束的遵循情况。

Method: 研究构建了一个紧凑的专家策划数据集，包含12个涵盖量子场论和弦理论核心领域的问题。引入五级评分标准，分别评估陈述正确性、关键概念意识、推理链存在性、隐含步骤重构和丰富性。使用该框架评估了多个当代大语言模型。

Result: 评估显示，在稳定概念框架内的显式推导任务上，模型表现接近天花板水平。但当任务需要重构被省略的推理步骤或在全局一致性约束下重组表示时，出现系统性退化。这些失败不仅源于缺失中间步骤，更源于表示选择的不稳定性：模型常无法识别解决隐含张力所需的正确概念框架。

Conclusion: 高度抽象的理论物理为当前评估范式的认知极限提供了独特敏感视角。研究结果表明，标准评估方法在捕捉理论物理推理的复杂性和隐含性方面存在根本局限，需要更精细的评估框架来理解模型在抽象科学推理中的能力边界。

Abstract: Large language models have demonstrated impressive performance across many domains of mathematics and physics. One natural question is whether such models can support research in highly abstract theoretical fields such as quantum field theory and string theory. Evaluating this possibility faces an immediate challenge: correctness in these domains is layered, tacit, and fundamentally non-binary. Standard answer-matching metrics fail to capture whether intermediate conceptual steps are properly reconstructed or whether implicit structural constraints are respected. We construct a compact expert-curated dataset of twelve questions spanning core areas of quantum field theory and string theory, and introduce a five-level grading rubric separating statement correctness, key concept awareness, reasoning chain presence, tacit step reconstruction, and enrichment. Evaluating multiple contemporary LLMs, we observe near-ceiling performance on explicit derivations within stable conceptual frames, but systematic degradation when tasks require reconstruction of omitted reasoning steps or reorganization of representations under global consistency constraints. These failures are driven not only by missing intermediate steps, but by an instability in representation selection: models often fail to identify the correct conceptual framing required to resolve implicit tensions. We argue that highly abstract theoretical physics provides a uniquely sensitive lens on the epistemic limits of current evaluation paradigms.

</details>

Abstract: We present a meshless numerical method for simulating the dynamics of axisymmetric vesicles in a viscous medium. The method achieves high accuracy and computational efficiency for simulating lipid bilayer dynamics and related problems in soft matter physics.

Aside from the bright solitonic solution, we also report double bright and dark soliton states. Our results indicate that NNQS provides a powerful framework for uncovering coherent structures in nonlinear wave systems.

### [62] [Mean-field phase diagrams of spinor bosons in an optical cavity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14771)
*Maksym Prodius,Mateusz Łącki,Jakub Zakrzewski*

TL;DR: 该研究重新审视了自旋玻色子在外部晶格和腔体中的多种可能基态，通过平均场方法揭示了包括反铁磁莫特绝缘体、铁磁密度波以及三种不同类型的超固态相在内的丰富相图。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用巨正则平均场（grand-canonical mean-field）方法分析问题，同时考虑均匀系统和非均匀系统（含谐振囚禁势）。在均匀情况下，采用双重处理方式：施加物理相关的总磁化约束，同时讨论完全无约束问题的极小化景观。结合解析论证和基于Gutzwiller ansatz的数值计算进行分析。

Result: 系统展现出两种磁性相：反铁磁莫特绝缘体（AFM）和铁磁密度波（FDW）。此外，出现了三种不同的超固态相，其特征是自旋和密度不平衡的不同模式。在总磁化强度为零的情况下，只有两种超固态相存在，FDW相被纠缠密度波（EDW）取代，这些新基态呈现玻色子基础自旋分量的密度调制叠加态。

Conclusion: 研究揭示了自旋玻色子在外部晶格和腔体系统中的复杂相行为，特别是提出了直接适用于未来实验的囚禁系统相图，展示了该系统丰富的多相结构。

Abstract: The plethora of possible ground states of spinor bosons placed in an external lattice and a cavity is revisited. We discuss the simplest case when the external lattice nodes coincide with the antinodes of the cavity field. We analyze the problem within the grand-canonical mean-field approach, considering both the homogeneous system and the nonhomogeneous case with a harmonic trapping potential. Due to the spin degree of freedom, in the homogeneous case we treat the system in a twofold manner: we impose the physically relevant total-magnetization constraint, while also discussing the minimization landscape for the full unconstrained problem. In the latter, by combining analytical arguments with numerical calculations based on the Gutzwiller ansatz, we show that the system exhibits two types of magnetic phases: an antiferromagnetic Mott insulator (AFM) and a ferromagnetic density wave (FDW). In addition, three distinct supersolid phases emerge, characterized by different patterns of spin and density imbalances. In case of the zero total magnetization, only two of the three supersolid regimes survive, and the FDW phases are replaced by entangled density waves (EDW). These new ground states present density-modulated superpositions of the underlying spin components of the bosons. Finally, we present the phase diagram of the trapped system, which is directly relevant for future experiments.

Abstract: The electric and magnetic dipole moments of the electron and of the muon provide stringent tests of the Standard Model and sensitive probes of new physics. ### [65] [Astrophysical bounds on the high-energy evolution of neutrino mixing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14409)
*Mauricio Bustamante,Qinrui Liu,Gabriela Barenboim*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该研究利用高能天体物理中微子的味成分（flavor composition）来约束中微子混合参数在高能标下的重整化群演化（renormalization-group evolution），为超出传统实验能量范围的混合参数演化提供了新的探测方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统振荡实验虽能精确测量中微子混合参数，但其测量范围严格限制在亚TeV能标。高能标下，重整化群效应可能导致这些参数随转移动量Q演化，而高能和超高能天体物理中微子（TeV至EeV能量）能够探测传统实验无法达到的高Q值，为高能混合提供了前所未有的测试机会。

Method: 研究利用高能天体物理中微子的味成分（ν_e、ν_μ、ν_τ的相对比例）来约束这种演化，采用现象学方法和六维标准模型有效场论（dimension-6 Standard Model Effective Field Theory）框架进行分析。同时考虑了天体物理不确定性，这是获得现实结果不可避免的要求。

Result: 当前IceCube测量缺乏探测这种演化的灵敏度，但预测即将到来的多探测器组合将为中微子混合参数的高能演化提供前所未有的约束界限。尽管天体物理不确定性削弱了约束强度，但多探测器组合有望显著改善探测能力。

Conclusion: 高能和超高能天体物理中微子为探测中微子混合参数在高能标下的重整化群演化提供了独特窗口。虽然当前实验灵敏度有限，但未来多探测器组合有望实现对混合参数高能演化的强有力约束，为超出标准模型物理提供重要测试。

Abstract: While conventional oscillation experiments measure neutrino mixing parameters with high precision, these measurements are strictly confined to sub-TeV scales. At higher energies, renormalization-group effects can cause these parameters to evolve with the transferred momentum, $Q$. High-energy and ultra-high-energy astrophysical neutrinos, spanning TeV to EeV energies, probe high values of $Q$ unreachable by conventional experiments, offering an unprecedented test of high-energy mixing. We use the flavor composition of these neutrinos -- the relative proportions of $ν_e$, $ν_μ$, and $ν_τ$ -- to constrain this evolution, both phenomenologically and within dimension-6 Standard Model Effective Field Theory. We account for astrophysical uncertainties -- an unavoidable requirement to obtain realistic results, even though this weakens the bounds. Although present IceCube measurements lack the sensitivity to detect this running, we forecast that upcoming multi-detector combinations will place unprecedented bounds on the high-energy evolution of neutrino mixing.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: 该spurion分析方法可推广到更高点振幅和非零汤川耦合（Yukawa couplings）情形，为系统研究SMEFT低能物理提供了有效的理论框架。

Abstract: We use the amplitude formulation of the SMEFT to introduce a spurion analysis of the SMEFT low-energy amplitudes in terms of the Higgs VEV. Each SMEFT contact-term is given as a sum of a few spurion structures, whose number depends on the electroweak charges of the external legs. The coefficients of these structures involve singlet combinations of Higgses from higher-order SMEFT contributions. We use this to derive the spurion expansions of the W- and Z-boson masses and mixing, and their three-point couplings to fermions. The textures of these couplings are saturated by the dimension-eight SMEFT. Our analysis can be generalized to higher-point amplitudes and nonzero Yukawa couplings.

### [68] [Dilaton-Flattened Axion Inflation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15194)
*Pirzada,Ali Muhammad,Tianjun Li,Imtiaz Khan,Mussawir Khan*

Main category: hep-ph

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 方法包括：1）构建可解的同扇区有效理论，通过径向场的树级消除将动态反作用重整化为闭式朗伯W函数势能；2）推导精确的谷底度规（trough metric），在完全约化的一场作用量上评估所有可观测量；3）在N_*=56处进行校准，分析再加热兼容分支。

Result: 结果显示：再加热兼容分支产生张量标量比r≈0.033-0.036和跑动谱指数α_s≈-(4.6-4.7)×10^-4，满足当前ACT/SPT/BICEP观测约束。演化保持严格绝热（m_⊥^2/H^2≳6.1，Ω/H≲7.6×10^-4），声速和度规修正可忽略。

Conclusion: 结论认为朗伯W函数骨架（Lambert-W backbone）为禁闭轴子暴胀（confining axion inflation）建立了精确可形变的基准，微观匹配和再加热微观物理可作为系统有效场论（EFT）改进进行访问。

Abstract: We present a solvable same-sector effective theory for anomaly-inspired axion inflation, in which a heavy trace-anomaly mode dynamically backreacts on the axion potential. The tree-level elimination of the radial field resums the backreaction into a closed-form Lambert-$W$ potential, naturally flattening the hilltop potential without external plateau operators. By deriving the exact trough metric, we evaluate all the observables on the fully reduced one-field action, bypassing uncontrolled kinetic approximations. Calibrated at $N_\star=56$, reheating-compatible branches yield $r\simeq0.033$--$0.036$ and $α_s\simeq-(4.6$--$4.7)\times10^{-4}$, comfortably satisfying the current ACT/SPT/BICEP constraints. The evolution remains strictly adiabatic ($m_\perp^2/H^2\gtrsim6.1$, $Ω/H\lesssim7.6\times10^{-4}$) with negligible sound-speed and metric corrections. We provide analytic control over the constant-$w_{\rm eff}$ reheating map, the $N_{\rm re}=0$ boundary, and robustness against vacuum-offset deformations. This Lambert-$W$ backbone establishes a precise, deformable benchmark for confining axion inflation, with microscopic matching and reheating microphysics accessible as systematic EFT refinements.

Abstract: Axion-like particles (ALPs), the QCD axion, and dark photons in the MeV-GeV mass range are motivated by various dark matter models and the strong CP problem, and are ubiquitous in extensions of the Standard Model. A long-standing blind spot for experimental searches is the sub-100 MeV mass range, where the particle lifetime is too long to be constrained by prompt-decay collider searches yet too short to be reached by beam-dump experiments. We investigate and estimate the sensitivity of the Light Dark Matter eXperiment (LDMX) to such axions and dark photons, motivated by the clean environment in which these particles can be produced and by the near-target tracking capabilities of LDMX. With reasonable charged track and momentum reconstruction capabilities, we find that LDMX could close much of this low-mass blind spot for axions and dark photons.

### [70] [Phenomenology of Vanishing Effective Majorana Mass with a Sterile Neutrino under Cosmological and JUNO Constraints](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14983)
*Rushi Chambyal,Tapender,Labh Singh,Surender Verma*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: 在3+1中微子框架下，考虑宇宙学对中微子质量和的最新约束，可以识别导致无中微子双β衰变振幅为零的参数空间。JUNO实验的精确测量对惰性中微子参数的约束可能因CP破坏相位驱动的相消效应而减弱。

Abstract: In the present work we investigate the phenomenological implications of a vanishing effective Majorana neutrino mass within a $3+1$ neutrino framework adding a eV-scale sterile neutrino beside three active neutrino states in light of latest cosmology driven bounds on sum of neutrino masses ($\sum_{i}m_i$). We explore the parameter space where the destructive interference between active and sterile states leads to vanishing amplitude, $M_{ee}$, of neutrinoless double beta ($0νββ$) decay. The allowed parameter space has been identified and predictions have been obtained taking into account the latest Planck and DESI+CMB bound on $\sum_{i}m_i$. We find that these bounds restrict the sterile mixing angle $θ_{14}$ and the lightest active neutrino mass. Furthermore, we incorporate the refined precision data from JUNO experiment regarding solar oscillation parameters ($θ_{12}, Δm_{21}^2$). We find that the sterile neutrino parameters like $θ_{14}$ may not be sensitive to the JUNO precision measurements as the constraint imposed by precise $θ_{12}$ is washed out by new cancellations driven through additional CP violating phases leading to vanishing $|M_{ee}|$.

### [71] [Symmetry Preserving Contact Interaction Approaches: An Overview of Meson and Diquark Form Factors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15122)
*L. X. Gutiérrez-Guerrero,Roger José Hernández-Pinto*

Conclusion: 接触相互作用模型是强子结构研究的实用工具，具有应用于重子和多夸克态的潜力。未来FAIR、Jefferson Lab和电子离子对撞机（Electron Ion Collider）的实验测量将为模型预测提供关键基准，推动强子结构研究的进一步发展。

Abstract: We present an updated overview of the symmetry preserving Contact Interaction model in hadronic physics, developed a little over a decade ago to describe the mass spectrum and internal structure of mesons and diquarks composed of light and heavy quarks. Over the years, the Contact Interaction has evolved into a framework capable of treating both ground and excited states, providing a simple yet consistent approach to nonperturbative QCD. In this review, we examine the mass spectrum and elastic form factors of forty mesons with different spins and parities, together with their corresponding diquark partners. Importantly, we update the comparison of Contact Interaction predictions using recent results from the literature, offering a fresh perspective on the model's performance, strengths, and limitations. The analysis presented here refines previous conclusions and supports the Contact Interaction as a practical tool for hadron structure studies, with potential applications to baryons and multiquark states. We also present comparisons with other theoretical models and approaches, including lattice quantum chromodynamics, and comment on future prospects in view of ongoing and planned hadron structure experimental programs.
  In particular, forthcoming measurements at FAIR, together with future studies at Jefferson Lab and the Electron Ion Collider, are expected to provide key insights into hadron structure, with FAIR offering indirect constraints via hadron spectroscopy, hadronic interactions, and in-medium properties, while high-precision data on meson structure and form factors from Jefferson Lab and the Electron Ion Collider will provide valuable benchmarks to confront Contact Interaction based predictions.

### [72] [Understanding jump discontinuity in disordered system](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14830)
*Anjan Daimari,Diana Thongjaomayum*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 该研究通过分析稀释系统中非平衡零温随机场伊辛模型（nonequilibrium zero-temperature random field Ising model）的磁滞响应，揭示了在临界点附近磁化强度跳跃不连续性的微观机制。研究发现总磁化强度的不连续性源于不同配位数（coordination number）子晶格跳跃的叠加，且主要贡献来自高浓度和高配位数的格点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 复杂系统对外部缓慢变化力的响应常在临界点附近出现序参量（order parameter）的跳跃不连续性。然而这种不连续性通常不是单一跳跃，而是分解为多个小跳跃，使得仅基于模拟结果在缺乏精确解的情况下难以准确定位临界点。本研究旨在通过分析稀释系统中非平衡零温随机场伊辛模型的磁滞响应来理解这些跳跃的分解机制。

Method: 研究采用配位数z=4的贝特晶格（Bethe lattice），稀释(1-c)比例的格点，形成具有不同配位数(z=4,3,2,1,0)的格点分布。通过精确求解整个晶格以及不同配位数字晶格的磁化曲线m(h)，分析总磁化强度不连续性的微观来源。同时也在立方晶格（cubic lattices）上进行测试验证。

Result: 总磁化强度的不连续性源于不同配位数子晶格跳跃在相同外部磁场h_crit处的叠加。跳跃的主要贡献来自高浓度和高配位数的格点，而触发大跳跃的格点主要是z≥3的格点。在立方晶格上的测试也支持这一结论，尽管无法获得精确解。

Conclusion: 该分析有助于理解数值模拟和实验中跳跃周围的涨落现象。研究揭示了复杂系统中临界点附近磁化强度跳跃不连续性的微观机制，为基于模拟结果定位临界点提供了理论依据。

Abstract: The response of a complex system to a slow varying external force often displays a jump discontinuity in the order parameter near the critical point. However, this discontinuity is not usually a single jump but rather breaks into smaller jumps which makes it difficult to locate the critical point on approaching its vicinity based only on simulations, in the absence of exact results. Our work is a small effort in understanding these breaks in jump through the hysteretic response of a classical Ising spin system to an external field, $h$, in the context of a nonequilibrium zero-temperature random field Ising model on dilute systems. We consider a Bethe lattice with coordination number, $z = 4$, and dilute a fraction $(1-c)$ of the sites. Therefore the lattice now consists of sites with varying $z = 4, 3, 2, 1$ and possibly few isolated sites $(z=0)$, depending on the concentration $c$. We obtain the exact solution of the magnetization curve, $m(h)$ vs $h$, for the entire lattice as well as for each sublattice of different $z$ coordinated sites, $m_4(h), m_3(h), m_2(h), m_1(h), m_0(h)$. The discontinuity in total magnetization is the result of the superposition of the jumps of different $z$ coordinated sites and observed at the same value of external field, $h_{crit}$. The dominant contribution to the jump comes from those sites with higher concentration and larger $z$. However, the triggering sites responsible for large jumps are mostly $z\ge3$. We test this on cubic lattices as well, where exact results are not available. We hope our analysis will help in understanding fluctuations around a jump in numerical simulations as well as experiments.

</details>

### [73] [Polyformer: a generative framework for thermodynamic modeling of polymeric molecules](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14241)
*Alessio Valentini,David Pekker,Chungwen Liang,Todd Martinez,Swagatam Mukhopadhyay*

Main category: q-bio.BM

TL;DR: Polyformer是一个生成式框架，用于聚合物分子的热力学建模，能够根据序列和温度生成符合热力学构象系综的构象，解决了分子折叠、构象系综及其随温度变化三个问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统结构生物学范式认为生物分子序列决定其构象，进而决定功能，但现有方法如AlphaFold仅预测单一最佳构象。生物分子并非静态结构，其构象系综（conformational ensemble）才真正决定功能，因此需要能够建模热力学系综的方法。

Method: 提出Polyformer——一个用于聚合物分子热力学建模的生成式框架（generative framework）。该方法以分子序列和温度（或其他热力学变量）为输入，生成符合分子热力学构象系综的构象。

Result: 将Polyformer应用于50-111个残基的蛋白质结构域，模型预测与分子动力学（Molecular Dynamics, MD）轨迹显示出良好的一致性（good agreement）。

Conclusion: Polyformer是首个同时解决分子如何折叠、其构象系综是什么以及构象系综如何随物理温度变化三个问题的生成模型，为热力学构象系综建模提供了新框架。

Abstract: The classic paradigm of structural biology is that the sequence of a biomolecule (protein, nucleic acid, lipid, etc) determines its conformation (shape) which determines its biological function. Protein folding programs like AlphaFold address this paradigm by predicting the single best conformation given a sequence that defines the molecule. However, biomolecules are not static structures, and their conformational ensemble determines their function. We present the Polyformer -- a generative framework for thermodynamic modeling of polymeric molecules. Given the sequence and temperature (or another thermodynamic variable), the Polyformer generates conformations faithful to the molecule's thermodynamic conformational ensemble. It is the first generative model that solves three problems simultaneously: how does a molecule fold, what is its conformational ensemble, and how does the conformational ensemble change as we change physical temperature. As a concrete test case, we apply Polyformer to protein domains with 50-111 residues and report good agreement of model predictions to Molecular Dynamics (MD) trajectories.

</details>

### [74] [Could the high-mass black holes from gravitational-wave observations be explained by lensing?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14247)
*Ritesh Harshe,R. Prasad,Parameswaran Ajith*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 该研究通过模拟引力透镜效应下的双黑洞并合事件，检验了BDS模型能否解释LIGO-Virgo观测到的高质量黑洞。分析发现该模型与多方面的观测数据均不一致，表明引力透镜放大并非高质量黑洞的可行解释。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LIGO和Virgo引力波观测发现的高质量黑洞（M≳30M⊙）令天文学家感到意外。虽然贫金属大质量恒星坍缩可能产生此类黑洞，但Broadhurst、Diego和Smoot（BDS）提出引力透镜放大效应是高质量观测结果的原因，并提出了相应的双黑洞并合红移分布模型。

Method: 研究采用模拟方法，基于BDS模型生成受引力透镜影响的双黑洞并合事件，并与观测数据从四个方面进行对比：1）观测到的并合事件数量；2）红移总质量和视光度距离分布；3）强透镜事件未探测到的情况；4）随机引力波背景未观测到的现象。

Result: 模拟与观测对比显示，无论选择何种BDS模型参数，都无法同时满足所有观测方面的要求。引力透镜放大效应不能合理解释LIGO-Virgo发现的高质量黑洞现象。

Conclusion: 研究结论表明，BDS提出的引力透镜模型与多方面的引力波观测证据不一致，因此透镜放大效应不能作为LIGO-Virgo观测到高质量黑洞的可行解释。

Abstract: The high-mass ($M \gtrsim 30 M_\odot$) black holes (BHs) from the gravitational-wave (GW) observations of LIGO and Virgo came as a surprise to many astronomers. While the collapse of metal-poor massive stars could produce such BHs, gravitational lensing has been invoked to explain their high masses. Broadhurst, Diego, and Smoot (henceforth BDS) argued that the mass distribution of BHs in coalescing binaries is very similar to that of the galactic BHs, and the inferred high masses are the result of neglecting the lensing magnification. They also proposed a redshift distribution of binary BH (BBH) mergers to explain the observed LIGO-Virgo mass distribution. We ask whether such a model is consistent with different aspects of the GW observations: 1) the observed number of BBH mergers, 2) the distribution of their redshifted total mass and apparent luminosity distance, 3) the non-detection of strongly lensed events, and 4) the non-observation of the stochastic GW background. By simulating lensed BBH mergers with the BDS model and comparing them with observations, we conclude that no choice of BDS model parameters is consistent with all aspects of the observations. Lensing magnification is not a viable explanation for the high-mass BHs discovered by LIGO and Virgo.

</details>

### [75] [Emergence of Open Chemical Reaction Network Thermodynamics within Closed Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14848)
*Benedikt Remlein,Massimiliano Esposito,Francesco Avanzini*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究阐明了开放化学反应网络（CRNs）如何作为封闭CRNs的渐近行为出现，当满足时间尺度分离和丰度分离两个条件时，开放CRNs的动力学和热力学结构可以从封闭系统中涌现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 开放化学反应网络（CRNs）是描述非平衡化学系统的标准框架，但实际系统是有限的并最终弛豫至平衡态。这引发了关于开放CRNs描述在概念上的地位问题，特别是基于理想化恒化器（chemostats）交换选定物种的开放CRNs如何从底层封闭CRNs中涌现。

Method: 研究通过分析封闭CRNs的渐近行为，识别出两个最小且物理透明的条件：时间尺度分离（fast reactions effectively act as exchange mechanisms）和丰度分离（a subset of species behaves as chemostats with diverging chemical capacity）。在此机制下，开放CRNs的行为作为封闭CRNs的渐近机制出现。

Result: 在满足时间尺度分离和丰度分离的条件下，开放CRNs的随机动力学和热力学结构——包括局部细致平衡（local detailed balance）、熵产生（entropy production）和自由能平衡（free-energy balance）——从底层封闭CRNs中主导性地涌现。这些结果适用于任意化学计量关系。

Conclusion: 恒化器无需作为外部理想化引入，而是作为封闭系统内涌现的热力学结构出现。这为化学反应网络的非平衡热力学提供了统一且物理基础坚实的理论基础。

Abstract: We address a fundamental question: under which conditions do the dynamics and thermodynamics of open chemical reaction networks (CRNs), grounded on the notion of idealized chemostats that exchange selected species, emerge from underlying closed CRNs? While open CRNs provide the standard framework to describe out-of-equilibrium chemical systems, real systems are finite and ultimately relax to equilibrium, leaving the status of this description conceptually unresolved. Here we show that open-CRN behavior arises as an asymptotic regime of closed CRNs when two minimal and physically transparent conditions are met: a time-scale separation, whereby fast reactions effectively act as exchange mechanisms, and an abundance separation, whereby a subset of species behaves as chemostats with diverging chemical capacity. In this regime, both the stochastic dynamics and the thermodynamic structure \ -- including local detailed balance, entropy production, and free-energy balance \ -- emerge to leading order from the underlying closed CRN. Our results apply to arbitrary stoichiometries. They show that chemostats need not be introduced as external idealizations, but instead arise as emergent thermodynamic structures within closed systems, providing a unified and physically grounded foundation for the nonequilibrium thermodynamics of CRNs.

### [76] [Coarse Graining Reveals a Fluctuation-theorem-like Asymmetry in Financial Markets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14962)
*Jian Gao,Lufeng Zhang,Ping Fang,Pu Ke,Jin Wu,Yue Liu,Haijun Zhou*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究将涨落定理（fluctuation theorem）的对称性诊断框架应用于金融市场，通过对称的止盈（take-profit）和止损（stop-loss）交易规则，发现长、短持仓的持有时间分布对数比在尾部呈现线性关系，揭示了市场存在指数型方向不对称性，并定义了有效的市场温度（market temperature）作为波动强度的操作度量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索是否能为金融市场构建类似涨落定理（fluctuation theorem）的对称性诊断工具。涨落定理展示了粗粒化（coarse graining）如何将微观对称性转化为可观测的不可逆性，而金融市场在微观层面每笔交易都包含买卖双方的配对，但交易决策通常基于粗粒化的价格历史做出。

Method: 研究方法采用对称的止盈（take-profit）和止损（stop-loss）交易规则，比较基于相同价格序列生成的长仓（long）和短仓（short）交易组合的持有时间分布（holding-time distributions）。该方法应用于股票指数、个股和加密货币等多种资产类别，分析其分布对数比（log-ratio）的变化模式。

Result: 研究结果显示，长、短持仓持有时间分布的对数比呈现稳健的交叉（crossover）模式：在短持续时间段保持近似恒定，而在尾部（tail）则呈现线性关系，暗示存在指数型方向不对称性（exponential directional asymmetry）。尾部斜率定义了有效的市场温度（market temperature），作为选定观测尺度下波动强度的操作度量。Bachelier首次通过基准（first-passage benchmark）能捕捉指数尾部但无法解释不对称性，而重叠持仓间的短时相关性（short-time correlations）通过生成方向依赖的次主导弛豫谱（subleading relaxation spectra），为不对称性提供了最小机制解释。

Conclusion: 该研究为金融市场建立了一个类似涨落定理的不可逆性诊断工具，更广泛地，为仅能通过粗粒化可观测量（coarse-grained observables）访问的复杂系统提供了分析框架。研究揭示了粗粒化马尔可夫描述（coarse-grained Markov description）中方向依赖的弛豫动力学如何产生市场不对称性。

Abstract: Fluctuation theorems show how coarse graining transforms microscopic symmetry into observable irreversibility. Here we ask whether an analogous symmetrybased diagnostic can be constructed for financial markets. At the microscopic level, each transaction pairs a buyer and a seller, whereas trading decisions are typically made from coarse-grained price histories. Using symmetric takeprofit and stop-loss rules, we compare the holding-time distributions of long and short trading ensembles generated from the same price series. Across equityindices, individual stocks and cryptocurrencies, the log-ratio of the two distributions shows a robust crossover. It remains nearly constant at short durations but becomes linear in the tail, implying an exponential directional asymmetry. The tail slope defines an effective market temperature, an operational measure of fluctuation intensity on the chosen observation scale. A Bachelier first-passage benchmark captures the exponential tails but not the asymmetry, because long and short positions share the same leading decay rate. By contrast, short-time correlations between overlapping positions provide a minimal mechanism for the asymmetry by generating direction-dependent subleading relaxation spectra in a coarse-grained Markov description. Together, these results establish a fluctuation-theorem-like diagnostic of irreversibility in financial markets and, more broadly, in complex systems accessible only through coarse-grained observables.

</details>


### [77] [Thermodynamic Geometry of Relaxation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15000)
*Hao Wang,Li Zhao,Shuai Deng,Yu-Han Ma*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究提出了基于瑞利商（Rayleigh quotient）的热几何度量，将弛豫过程重新表述为熵刚度与摩擦耗散之间的基本竞争，并以范德瓦尔斯气体为例展示了弛豫景观，发现临界温度附近慢模弛豫率线性趋零，揭示了临界慢化现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 虽然平衡态和驱动非平衡过程的几何描述已很清晰，但弛豫向平衡过程的几何描述仍然缺乏。本研究旨在填补这一空白，完善热力学几何框架。

Method: 提出基于瑞利商（Rayleigh quotient）的热几何度量，将弛豫重新表述为熵刚度（entropic stiffness）与摩擦耗散（frictional dissipation）之间的竞争。以具有两个耗散通道的范德瓦尔斯气体（van der Waals gas）为例，明确展示其弛豫景观（relaxation landscape）。

Result: 研究发现，当接近临界温度 $T_c$ 时，慢模弛豫率（slow-mode relaxation rate）线性趋零：$λ_s \propto (T-T_c)/T_c$，表明存在临界慢化（critical slowing down）现象。该研究明确展示了弛豫景观。

Conclusion: 该研究完善了热力学几何框架（thermodynamic geometry framework），为表征复杂系统的弛豫动力学（relaxation dynamics）提供了一个通用工具。

Abstract: While the geometry of equilibrium states and driven non-equilibrium processes is clearly understood, a geometric description for relaxation towards equilibrium is still lacking. Here, we propose a thermo-geometric measure based on the Rayleigh quotient, reformulating relaxation as a fundamental competition between entropic stiffness and frictional dissipation. Taking a van der Waals gas with two dissipation channels as an example, we explicitly demonstrate its relaxation landscape. Particularly, we find that upon approaching the critical temperature $T_c$, the slow-mode relaxation rate vanishes linearly as $λ_s \propto (T-T_c)/T_c$, indicating critical slowing down. This study completes the thermodynamic geometry framework, providing a general tool for characterizing the relaxation dynamics of complex systems.

</details>

### [78] [Iron spin crossover in ferropericlase and its effect on lower-mantle thermal conductivity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14183)
*Alexander F. Goncharov,Irina Chuvashova,Eric Edmund,JungFu Lin,Zena Younes,Nicolas Jaisle,Axel Phelipeau,Carmen Sanchez-Valle,Christoph Otzen,Clemens Prescher,Hanns-Peter Liermann,Nico Giordano,James McHardy,Karen Appel,Michal Andrzejewski,S. V. Rahul,Minxue Tang,Jolanta Sztuk-Dambietz,Thomas Michelat,Torsten Laurus,Malcolm McMahon,Mark Robertson,Rachel Husband,Efim Kolesnikov,Sebastien Merkel,Silvia Boccato,Carsten Baehtz,Guillaume Morard,Emma S. Bullock,Cornelius Strohm,Zuzana Konopkova,Ryan Stewart McWilliams*

Main category: physics.geo-ph

TL;DR: 该研究首次在同时模拟下地幔压力和温度条件下测量了铁方镁石（ferropericlase）的热导率，发现60-100 GPa范围内热导率显著降低与铁自旋交叉（iron spin crossover）一致，结合先前数据建立了下地幔热导率剖面，约束了地幔热流和地幔柱浮力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 下地幔热导率控制着核幔边界（core-mantle boundary, CMB）的热传递，并强烈影响地幔对流过程。然而，缺乏铁方镁石（ferropericlase）在同时模拟下地幔压力和温度条件下的热导率数据，限制了我们对地幔热传输机制的理解。

Method: 采用金刚石压砧（diamond-anvil cells）结合光学激光闪光（optical laser flash）和X射线自由电子激光加热技术，在高达~2200 K和130 GPa条件下直接测量单晶铁方镁石（Mg₁₋ₓFeₓO, x=0.09-0.13）的热导率。

Result: 实验首次获得了铁方镁石在同时模拟下地幔压力和温度条件下的热导率数据。在~1700 K时，60-100 GPa范围内热导率的显著降低与铁自旋交叉（iron spin crossover）现象一致。结合先前含铁和铁铝的布里奇曼石（bridgmanite）数据，建立了下地幔热导率剖面，显示热导率随压力增加至核幔边界附近达到~10 W·m⁻¹·K⁻¹。

Conclusion: 该研究提供了下地幔热导率的直接实验约束，这些数据对理解地幔热流、地幔柱（plume）浮力以及长期地球动力学演化具有重要意义，为地球内部热传输机制提供了关键实验证据。

Abstract: Thermal conductivity of Earths lower mantle controls heat transfer across the core-mantle boundary (CMB) and strongly influences mantle convection. We report direct measurements of the thermal conductivity of single-crystal ferropericlase (Mg$_{1-x}$Fe$_x$O, $x = 0.09$-0.13), the second most abundant lower-mantle mineral, using optical laser flash and X-ray free-electron laser heating in diamond-anvil cells up to $\sim2200$~K and 130~GPa. These experiments provide the first conductivity data for ferropericlase at simultaneous lower-mantle pressures and temperatures. A marked reduction in conductivity between 60 and 100~GPa at $\sim1700$~K is consistent with the iron spin crossover. Combined with our previous results for Fe- and Fe,Al-bearing bridgmanite, the data define a lower-mantle conductivity profile that increases with pressure to $\sim10$~W\,m$^{-1}$\,K$^{-1}$ near the CMB, constraining mantle heat flux, plume buoyancy, and long-term geodynamic evolution.

### [79] [Correlative Microstructural Analysis of a Weathered Nantan Meteorite Fragment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14187)
*Graeme J. Francolini,Brendan V. Dyck,Paul Mack,Ben Britton*

Main category: physics.geo-ph

TL;DR: 本研究通过多种分析技术对自然风化的南丹（Nantan）陨石碎片进行相关性和比较性分析，揭示了铁镍金属在风化过程中的多阶段相变机制，包括高镍区和低镍区的不同形成路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 陨石中铁富集相的风化是一个多阶段过程，其微观结构和化学成分会显著改变，这种改变既取决于陨石降落点的环境条件，也取决于陨石坠落后的暴露时间。本研究旨在通过相关性和比较性方法探究这一过程产生的相变结果。

Method: 采用多种分析技术对自然风化的南丹陨石碎片进行研究：使用X射线光电子能谱（XPS）、能量色散X射线光谱（EDX）和X射线荧光光谱（XRF）进行成分测定；使用X射线衍射（XRD）和电子背散射衍射（EBSD）进行相鉴定和微观结构分析。

Result: 分析显示陨石基质主要由磁铁矿（magnetite）组成，并存在明显的高镍含量区域。高镍（≥2.6 at%）区域的晶粒结构非常细小（约5 μm），与低镍（≤0.9 at%）区域（晶粒平均尺寸为数十μm）之间存在100-200 μm的可见边界。基质中还发现了其他常见风化产物，包括针铁矿（goethite）、纤铁矿（lepidocrocite）、水铁矿（feroxyhyte）以及Ni(OH)₂。此外，样品中发现了一个角砾岩相，表现为一个大的陨碳铁（cohenite）晶粒，显示出水化风化迹象，包括由NiO和磁铁矿组成的脉状结构，以及铁和镍碳酸盐沉积物。

Conclusion: 这些结果表明，不同的基质区域是通过离散原生相的风化机制形成的：高镍区域来自陨铁（kamacite）的水化蚀变，而低镍区域则来自源Fe-Ni金属的直接溶解和氧化。

Abstract: The weathering of iron-rich phases within meteorites is a multi-stage process that significantly alters the microstructure and chemical composition based both on the environmental condition at the location of landing and the exposure time since the fall. This work investigates the resulting phases of this process in a correlative and comparative manner using a naturally weathered Nantan meteorite fragment. Techniques including X-ray Photoelectron Spectroscopy, Energy Dispersive X-ray Spectroscopy, and X-ray Fluorescence Spectroscopy were used for compositional determination and X-ray Diffraction and Electron Backscatter Diffraction for phase determination and microstructural analysis.
  Use of these techniques revealed the meteorite matrix to be predominantly composed of magnetite, with distinct regions of high Ni content. The grain structure was found to be very fine (approx. 5 $μ$m) in areas of high Ni ($\geq$2.6 at%) content with a visible boundary of 100-200 $μ$m extending into the low Ni ($\leq$0.9 at%) regions, wherein the grains averaged 10s of $μ$m in size. Other common products of weathering, including goethite, lepidocrocite, and feroxyhyte, were also found within the matrix alongside Ni(OH)$_2$. Additionally, a brecciated phase was found within the sample and appeared to be a large cohenite grain which exhibits signs of aqueous weathering, including in a vein-like structure, composed of NiO and magnetite, and deposits of iron and nickel carbonates. These results indicate that the distinct matrix regions formed through the weathering mechanism of discrete primary phases, with the high Ni regions forming from aqueous alteration of kamacite and the low Ni regions forming from direct dissolution and oxidation of the source Fe-Ni metal.

</details>

### [80] [A convex-geometric framework for fully phase-locked states in the finite Kuramoto model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14772)
*Antonio Garijo,Sergio Gómez,Alex Arenas*

Main category: physics.soc-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究全连接有限尺寸仓本模型（Kuramoto model）中完全相位锁定（fully phase-locked）平衡态的存在条件，通过凸几何方法建立了临界耦合强度的显式上界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究具有异质自然频率的全连接仓本振荡器（Kuramoto oscillators）中完全相位锁定平衡态的存在条件，特别是确定所需的最小耦合强度。该问题对于理解同步现象（synchronization）的临界行为具有重要意义。

Method: 采用降维共转参考系（reduced co-rotating frame）消除均匀相移简并性，通过雅可比矩阵（Jacobian）负定性判断稳定性。利用凸几何结构将稳定性区域映射到频率空间，通过分析可计算边界点构建显式多面体（polytope）。

Result: 建立了临界耦合强度（critical coupling strength）$K_{\ell}$的几何解释：对应射线$t\hat{\mathbfω}$与凸集边界的首次交点。构造了显式多面体，提供了闭式上界$K_b \ge K_{\ell}$，该上界在频率向量与多面体顶点对齐时精确。

Conclusion: 研究揭示了仓本模型中稳定完全锁定态（stable fully-locked states）的凸几何结构，提供了实用的外近似方法。虽然上界在定量意义上并非处处尖锐，但该构造暴露了稳定完全相位锁定解的底层几何特性。

Abstract: We study the finite-size Kuramoto model of all-to-all coupled phase oscillators with heterogeneous natural frequencies and characterize the minimal coupling strength required for the existence of a fully phase-locked equilibrium (in a co-rotating frame). To remove the degeneracy due to uniform phase shifts, we move to a reduced co-rotating frame and assess stability through the Jacobian of the reduced system: a fully phase-locked state is stable when this Jacobian is negative definite. This defines a stability region in the phase space. The Kuramoto vector field maps this region to a convex set in frequency space, so a fully-locked state at coupling $K$ exists exactly when the rescaled frequency vector $\hat{\mathbfω}/K$ lies inside that convex image. The critical coupling $K_{\ell}$ is defined as the smallest coupling strength for which a fully phase-locked equilibrium exists; geometrically, it corresponds to the first intersection of the ray $t\hat{\mathbfω}$ with the boundary of this convex set. Building on this convex-geometric structure, we construct an explicit polytope from analytically computable boundary points of the stability region, providing a closed-form upper bound $K_b \ge K_{\ell}$. The bound is exact for frequencies aligned with polytope vertices and offers a fully explicit outer approximation for general frequency vectors. While not uniformly sharp in a quantitative sense, this construction exposes the underlying geometry of stable fully phase-locking solutions. These results provide a practical use the convex-geometric structure underlying stable fully-locked states in the Kuramoto model.

</details>

### [81] [The Agentification of Scientific Research: A Physicist's Perspective](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14718)
*Xiao-Liang Qi*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文认为AI革命（尤其是大语言模型）的核心意义在于根本性地改变了复杂信息和人类专有知识的承载、复制与共享方式，而AI for Science（AI4S）将不仅提升研究效率，更可能重塑科学合作、发现、出版与评估的结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在探讨AI革命（特别是大语言模型的兴起）的最重要意义，强调其不仅在于自动化，更在于对复杂信息和人类专有知识（know-how）的承载、复制与共享方式的根本性变革。

Method: 文章采用论证性分析框架，从AI作为研究工具到AI作为科学合作者的渐进路径进行阐述，并讨论AI如何可能从根本上重塑科学出版体系。

Result: 分析表明，AI for Science（AI4S）具有特殊重要性，因为它可能不仅改变研究效率，还会影响科学合作、发现、出版和评估的结构性变革。

Conclusion: 要使AI在原创性科学发现中发挥有意义的作用，持续学习和思想多样性至关重要；AI革命的核心在于根本性地改变了知识传播和共享的方式。

Abstract: This article argues that the most important significance of the AI revolution, especially the rise of large language models, lies not simply in automation, but in a fundamental change in how complex information and human know-how are carried, replicated, and shared. From this perspective, AI for Science is especially important because it may transform not only the efficiency of research, but also the structure of scientific collaboration, discovery, publishing, and evaluation. The article outlines a gradual path from AI as a research tool to AI as a scientific collaborator, and discusses how AI is likely to fundamentally reshape scientific publication. It also argues that continuous learning and diversity of ideas are essential if AI is to play a meaningful role in original scientific discovery.

</details>

### [82] [Spontaneous Emission, Free Energy, and Relaxation-Limited Processes in Setting Limits on Solar Energy Conversion Efficiency](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14982)
*Sumanta Mukherjee*

Main category: physics.app-ph

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种评估辐射自由能的简化方法，用于分析光能到可用能量转换的热力学极限。模型预测理论最大转换效率约为74%，并通过准确再现Shockley-Queisser极限（约33%）验证了方法的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解辐射热力学及光与物质的量子力学相互作用对于理论研究和技术进步至关重要，特别是确定光能到可用能量转换效率的极限。现有描述在评估能量收集效率方面存在局限性，需要更完善的分析框架。

Result: 理论预测光能到可用能量转换的热力学最大极限约为74%。模型准确再现了Shockley-Queisser极限（约33%），验证了自由能估计的有效性。在特定条件下（如多结太阳能电池或光子上转换），最大转换效率可达约48%。

Conclusion: 光能转换的真实热力学极限可能远高于现有估计（约74%），但准确评估需要更全面地理解光的热力学、光-物质相互作用及其关联。该框架为评估各种光能转换效率提供了理论基础。

Abstract: Understanding the thermodynamics of radiation and the quantum-mechanical interactions between light and matter is important both for theoretical purposes and for technological advances, such as determining the limits of key processes like light-to-usable-energy conversion efficiencies. In this report, we discuss the physics of these two aspects, considering spontaneous emission as a pathway, and highlight the limitations of such descriptions in assessing energy-harvesting efficiency. In view of these limitations, we adopt a simplified approach to evaluate the free energy of radiation, providing a framework to assess various aspects of light-to-usable-energy conversion efficiencies. Our approach allows a theoretical estimate of the thermodynamic maximum limit for light-to-usable-energy conversion, which is approximately 74%. We validate this free energy estimate by modeling and accurately reproducing the Shockley-Queisser limit (~ 33%), which imposes a practical constraint on solar-to-usable-energy conversion efficiency. Beyond free-energy considerations, our model incorporates various processes, such as spontaneous emission, nonradiative thermal losses, and photon upconversion, allowing us to evaluate their roles. The model further suggests that, under certain conditions, the maximum conversion efficiency can reach approximately 48%, for example with multijunction solar cells or via photon upconversion. These findings further suggest that the true thermodynamic limit for light-to-usable-energy conversion may be much higher (approximately 74%). However, accurately estimating this limit requires a more complete understanding of the thermodynamics of light, light-matter interactions, and the connection between them.

### [83] [3D Finite Element-Based Multiphysics Simulation of a Shape Memory Alloy Hybrid Composite Module](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15211)
*Lukas Handl,Max Kaiser,Miro Duhovic,Martin Gurka*

Main category: physics.app-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种用于形状自适应形状记忆合金混合复合材料（SMAHCs）执行器的三维多物理场有限元方法，该方法在ANSYS LS-DYNA中集成了机械、热和电磁求解器，能够准确模拟SMA的复杂热机械相变行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管已有多种分析和有限元模型用于预测SMAHCs的瞬态响应，但许多方法在热机械耦合和全面实验验证方面存在局限性。因此，需要开发更精确的耦合多物理场模拟方法。

Method: 本文提出了一种耦合的多物理场三维有限元方法，在ANSYS LS-DYNA中集成了机械、热和电磁求解器。该方法采用微观力学本构模型，通过预设马氏体预应变来初始化材料状态，并显式考虑焦耳加热、机械载荷和环境温度变化。

Result: 模拟结果与实验数据和完全耦合的瞬态交错方案模型进行了验证。结果显示良好的定性一致性，再现了执行器偏转随温度变化的特征迟滞现象。定量上，预测偏转处于正确的数量级，尽管略微超出95%实验置信区间。

Conclusion: 模拟与实验之间观察到一致的趋势，这为模拟更复杂的SMAHC系统提供了可能性。所提出的三维方法在预测SMAHC执行器行为方面具有良好潜力。

Abstract: Shape adaptive shape memory alloy hybrid composites (SMAHCs) are composites that incorporate shape memory alloys (SMAs) to realize shape transformation. Despite the availability of numerous analytical and finite element models for predicting the transient response of SMAHCs, many approaches exhibit limitations with respect to the thermomechanical coupling and comprehensive experimental validation. Therefore, this paper presents a coupled, multiphysics, 3D finite element approach for the simulation of a SMAHC actuator, integrating mechanical, thermal and electromagnetic solvers in the Finite Element Code ANSYS LS-DYNA. The proposed approach employs a micromechanical constitutive model implemented in ANSYS LS-DYNA, to accurately capture the complex thermomechanical phase transformation of SMAs. A key feature of the model is the ability to prescribe a defined martensitic pre-strain through a preceding simulation step, in which an initially scaled SMA wire is mechanically loaded and stretched to its nominal length. This procedure enables partial detwinning of the martensitic microstructure and provides a physically motivated initialization of the material state. Joule heating of the SMA wires, as well as varying mechanical loads and ambient temperature conditions, are explicitly considered. The simulation results are validated against experimental data and a fully coupled transient staggered scheme model to assess the predictive capability of the 3D approach. The results show good qualitative agreement, reproducing the characteristic hysteresis of actuator deflection as a function of temperature. Quantitatively, the predicted deflections are of the correct order of magnitude, although marginally outside the 95 % experimental confidence interval. Overall, a consistent trend between simulation and experiment is observed, giving rise to possibility of simulating more complex SMAHC systems.
