### [84] [Bayesian Inference of Heavy-Quark Dissipation and Jet Transport Parameters from D-Meson observables in heavy-ion collisions at the LHC energies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.07169)
*Xu-Fei Xue,Zi-Xuan Xu,Wei Dai,Jiaxing Zhao,Ben-Wei Zhang*

Main category: nucl-th

TL;DR: 首次同时贝叶斯推断（Bayesian inference）重夸克空间扩散系数 $2πT\mathcal{D}_s$ 与标度化喷注输运系数 $\hat{q}/T^3$，利用Pb-Pb碰撞中$D$介子核修正因子$R_\text{AA}$和椭圆流$v_2$数据，揭示两者非单调温度依赖关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在首次同时约束夸克-胶子等离子体（quark-gluon plasma）中两个关键输运性质：温度依赖的重夸克空间扩散系数（heavy-quark spatial diffusion coefficient）$2πT\mathcal{D}_s$和标度化喷注输运系数（scaled jet transport coefficient）$\hat{q}/T^3$，以探究它们在强耦合介质中的相互关系。

Method: 采用统一的改进朗之万输运模型（improved Langevin transport model），同时包含碰撞和辐射能量损失机制，随后通过聚结加碎裂（coalescence plus fragmentation）实现强子化。利用Pb-Pb碰撞在$\sqrt{s_\text{NN}} = 5.02\ \text{TeV}$能量下的$D$介子核修正因子$R_\text{AA}$和椭圆流$v_2$数据进行贝叶斯推断。

Result: $\hat{q}/T^3$和$2πT\mathcal{D}_s$的参数后验分布得到良好约束，其中30-50%中心度数据比0-10%数据提供更强的约束。提取的喷注输运与重夸克扩散系数比值$\hat{q}/κ$呈现非单调温度依赖性，偏离定义估计值2，对应参数均值区间为0.25-0.8。

Conclusion: 该工作首次在同一观测量中建立了这两个基本输运性质之间的数据驱动定量关系，为理解它们在强耦合介质中的相互作用提供了关键见解，揭示了$\hat{q}/κ$比值与理论预期不同的温度依赖行为。

Abstract: We perform the first simultaneous Bayesian inference of the temperature-dependent heavy-quark spatial diffusion coefficient $2πT\mathcal{D}_s$ and the scaled jet transport coefficient $\hat{q}/T^3$ in the quark-gluon plasma, utilizing $D$-meson nuclear modification factor $R_\text{AA}$ and elliptic flow $v_2$ data from Pb-Pb collisions at $\sqrt{s_\text{NN}} = 5.02\ \text{TeV}$. The analysis employs a unified improved Langevin transport model that incorporates both collisional and radiative energy loss, followed by coalescence plus fragmentation hadronization. The posterior distributions of the parameters of $\hat{q}/T^3$ and those of $2πT\mathcal{D}_s$ are well constrained, and compared with the results of theoretical models or other experimental data extraction, respectively. The $30-50\%$ centrality data provide significantly stronger constraints than the $0-10\%$ data. The extracted ratio $\hat{q}/κ$ between the quark jet transport and heavy-quark diffusion coefficients exhibits a non-monotonic temperature dependence, deviating from the value $2$ estimated from the definition, with a value interval spanning 0.25--0.8 corresponding to the mean values of the inferred parameters. This work establishes a data-driven quantitative relationship between these two fundamental transport properties in the same observables, offering crucial insight into their interplay in the strongly coupled medium.

### [85] [Pool model: a mass preserving multi particle aggregation process](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14851)
*Zhenhao Cai,Eviatar B. Procaccia,Yuan Zhang*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 本文提出并研究了二维空间中的池模型（Pool model），这是一种旋转对称的多粒子扩散限制聚集（MDLA）类比模型，其中粒子（"液滴"）进行连续时间随机游走，并在进入初始位于原点的圆形池时被吸收，池体随质量增加而膨胀。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究旨在探索旋转对称的扩散限制聚集过程，通过池模型为多粒子扩散限制聚集（MDLA）提供一种自然的质量守恒动力学框架，研究粒子吸收与池体膨胀之间的相互作用机制。

Method: 提出池模型作为MDLA的旋转对称类比，粒子执行连续时间随机游走（continuous-time random walks）并在接触池边界时被吸收；每个被吸收粒子增加池体质量，池体相应膨胀以保持面积与质量成正比；核心方法是建立该模型的Kurtz定理版本，将条件于池体生长的粒子场描述为独立的非齐次泊松点过程（independent non-homogeneous Poisson point process）。

Result: 建立了池模型的数学框架，证明了描述粒子场的Kurtz定理版本，该定理具有独立的理论价值，能够将条件于池体生长过程的粒子场表征为独立的非齐次泊松点过程。

Conclusion: 池模型为研究扩散限制聚集过程提供了有效的旋转对称框架，所建立的Kurtz定理版本是该模型的核心分析工具，具有独立的数学理论意义，能够简化粒子场在池体生长条件下的概率描述。

Abstract: We present and study the Pool model in $\mathbb{R}^2$, a rotationally symmetric analogue of Multi-Particle Diffusion-Limited Aggregation (MDLA), in which particles ("droplets") perform continuous-time random walks and are absorbed upon entering a circular pool initially centered at the origin. Each absorbed particle increases the pool's mass, and the pool expands so that its area grows accordingly, yielding a natural mass-preserving dynamics. A central tool which is of independent interest is a version of Kurtz's theorem for this model, depicting the field of particles conditioned on the growth of the pool as an independent non-homogeneous Poisson point process.

### [86] [Renormalised two-point functions of CLE$_4$ gaskets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15146)
*Juhan Aru,Titus Lupu*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 本文研究了单连通域中的嵌套CLE₄，计算了重整化概率：两点属于同一CLE₄栅格（gasket）的概率，以及两点属于最外层CLE₄栅格的概率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在计算嵌套共形环系（conformal loop ensemble，CLE₄）中的重整化概率（renormalised probabilities）。这些概率对应于Ashkin-Teller（AT）模型临界线上单自旋（single spins）猜想标度极限（scaling limit）的两点函数（two-point function）。

Method: 方法结合了可积性（integrability）与概率计算。可积性根植于Ashkin-Teller模型的共形场论（conformal field theory），而概率计算则通过布朗环汤（Brownian loop soups）和二维连续高斯自由场（2D continuum Gaussian free field）的几何实现。

Result: 计算了多种重整化概率：两点属于同一CLE₄栅格的概率、两点属于最外层CLE₄栅格的概率，以及两点属于与高斯自由场的特定二值集（two-valued sets）交替采样的CLE₄栅格的概率。在解耦点（decoupling point），结果恢复了Ising模型关联，并提出了基于CLE₄的AT自旋模型的FK表示（FK representation）。

Conclusion: 研究结果为Ashkin-Teller模型临界线上单自旋的标度极限提供了两点函数的具体计算，并在解耦点建立了与Ising模型关联的联系，同时提出了基于CLE₄的AT自旋模型的FK表示方案。

Abstract: We consider nested CLE$_4$ in a simply-connected domain and compute the following renormalised probabilities: the probability that two points belong to the same CLE$_4$ gasket and the probability that two points belong to the outermost CLE$_4$ gasket. While the integrability is rooted in the conformal field theory of the Ashkin-Teller (AT) model, we provide a purely probabilistic calculation via Brownian loop soups and the geometry of the 2D continuum Gaussian free field. More generally, we also calculate renormalised probabilities that two points belong to CLE$_4$ gaskets sampled in alternation with certain two-valued sets of the Gaussian free field. These quantities correspond to the two-point function of the conjectured scaling limit of the AT single spins on the critical line. At the decoupling point, our results recover the Ising model correlations and suggest a CLE$_4$-based FK representation of the AT spin model.

### [87] [Magic and Non-Clifford Gates in Topological Quantum Field Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14271)
*William Munizzi,Howard J. Schnitzer*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文展示了非克利福德门（non-Clifford gates）如何自然地从拓扑量子场论（topological quantum field theories）的路径积分中产生，其产生魔性（magic-generating）的特性由理论的代数数据决定。研究在Chern-Simons理论和Dijkgraaf-Witten理论中构造了多种量子门，揭示了拓扑路径积分在克利福德层级（Clifford hierarchy）多个层次上构建量子门的机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非克利福德门（non-Clifford gates）对于产生量子魔性（quantum magic）和实现通用量子计算至关重要。本研究旨在探索这些门如何从拓扑量子场论（topological quantum field theories）的路径积分中自然产生，并理解其魔性生成特性与理论代数结构之间的关系。

Method: 通过拓扑量子场论（topological quantum field theories）的路径积分方法进行研究。在Chern-Simons理论中，通过简单三边界流形（three-boundary manifolds）的路径积分构造了Ising相互作用门（Ising interaction gate）。同时分析了SU(2)₁和SU(2)₃理论中Toffoli门的可实现性，并在Dijkgraaf-Witten理论（gauge group ℤ₄）中展示了T门如何通过边界环面（boundary torus）上的单个Dehn扭曲产生。

Result: 研究成功构造了Ising相互作用门，该门在离散克利福德点（discrete Clifford points）之外产生非局域魔性（non-local magic）。发现Toffoli门在SU(2)₁理论中受到ℤ₂融合结构（ℤ₂ fusion structure）的阻碍，而SU(2)₃是最小支持所需条件逻辑的理论。此外，在Dijkgraaf-Witten理论中，边界环面上的单个Dehn扭曲精确产生了T门，无需近似。

Conclusion: 拓扑路径积分能够在克利福德层级（Clifford hierarchy）的多个层次上构建量子门，并且这一机制跨越了不同类别的场理论。这些发现对拓扑量子计算（topological quantum computing）具有重要意义，揭示了量子门与拓扑场论代数结构之间的深刻联系。

Abstract: Non-Clifford gates, used to generate quantum magic, are essential for universal quantum computation. We show that non-Clifford gates arise naturally from path integrals in topological quantum field theories, where their magic-generating properties are determined by the algebraic data of the theory. In Chern-Simons theory, we construct the Ising interaction gate, whose generator is prepared by path integration over simple three-boundary manifolds, and show that it produces non-local magic away from discrete Clifford points. We show that the Toffoli gate is obstructed in $SU(2)_1$ by the $\mathbb{Z}_2$ fusion structure, while $SU(2)_3$ is the minimal theory supporting the required conditional logic, given the density of the mapping class group in the projective unitary group on the manifold boundary. Finally, we demonstrate that the T gate arises as a path integral in Dijkgraaf-Witten theory, with gauge group $\mathbb{Z}_4$, where a single Dehn twist on the boundary torus produces the gate without approximation. These results show that topological path integrals construct gates in multiple levels of the Clifford hierarchy, and across distinct classes of field theories, with implications for topological quantum computing.

### [88] [Generalized Complexity Distances and Non-Invertible Symmetries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14275)
*Jonathan J. Heckman,Rebecca J. Hicks,Chitraang Murdia*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文探讨量子场论（QFT）中非可逆对称性（non-invertible symmetries）作为量子计算门的应用，提出了一种包含后选择（post-selection）的并行量子计算方案，并建立了适用于此类对称性的距离/可区分性度量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子场论中的非可逆对称性作为幺正对称性的自然推广，其算子乘积不满足群乘法律。研究这些对称性在量子计算中的潜在应用，特别是作为包含后选择/投影门的并行量子计算方案中的量子门，具有重要理论意义。

Method: 作者将非可逆对称性操作视为量子计算门，推广了门复杂度（gate complexity）和几何复杂度度量。提出了一类距离/可区分性度量，将李群的标准距离概念扩展到连续和离散的非可逆对称性，以及更一般的幺正量子门的线性组合。

Result: 通过计算一些4D和2D量子场论中非可逆对称性之间的距离，发现对称性范畴（symmetry category）的简单对象在计算上可能具有高度复杂性。提出的距离度量能够有效区分不同类型的非可逆对称性操作。

Conclusion: 非可逆对称性为量子计算提供了新的资源，特别是作为包含后选择操作的量子门。对称性范畴的简单对象虽然数学结构简单，但在计算复杂度方面可能表现出高度复杂性，这为量子计算和量子场论的交叉研究开辟了新方向。

Abstract: Non-invertible symmetries of a quantum field theory (QFT) are a natural generalization of unitary symmetries, but in which the product of operators does not satisfy a group multiplication law. We show that such symmetry operations on states define a collection of quantum gates for a parallel quantum computation scheme that includes post-selection / projection as a gate. Structures such as gate complexity and more geometric complexity measures generalize to this setting. We provide a class of distance / distinguishability measures that extend the standard notion of distance for Lie groups to both continuous and discrete non-invertible symmetries, as well as more general linear combinations of unitary quantum gates. We illustrate these considerations by computing the distance between non-invertible symmetries in some 4D and 2D QFTs. We find that the simple objects of a symmetry category can be highly complex computationally.

### [89] [Beyond the Dilute Instanton Gas: Resurgence with Exact Saddles in the Double Well](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14279)
*Aurélien Dersy,Matthew D. Schwartz*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该研究通过采用精确鞍点（exact saddles）和有限欧几里得时间（finite Euclidean-time）方法，绕过了传统稀薄瞬子气体近似（dilute instanton gas approximation）的限制，系统计算了双势阱（double well）的配分函数和能级分裂。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 长期以来，双势阱问题的路径积分方法受限于稀薄瞬子气体近似。该研究旨在通过考虑有限欧几里得时间结构，使用精确鞍点来克服这一限制，从而更系统地计算配分函数和能级。

Method: 采用有限温度（finite $T$）方法，利用精确鞍点（Weierstrass椭圆函数描述）、准零模（quasi-zero modes）上的有限维Picard-Lefschetz围道积分，以及Lamé算符处理涨落，Picard-Fuchs方程处理周期。

Result: 该方法绕过了稀薄瞬子气体近似，能够系统计算所有激发态的非微扰能级分裂（non-perturbative energy splittings），包括对能级数的完整依赖关系。稀薄瞬子气体近似仅能处理基态分裂，而有限温度计算则能处理所有激发态。

Conclusion: Weierstrass椭圆函数、Lamé算符和Picard-Fuchs方程构成了一个连贯的数学框架，该框架与精确WKB（Exact WKB）方法既有重叠又相互补充，为双势阱问题提供了更完整的非微扰描述。

Abstract: The path-integral approach to the double well has long been limited by the dilute instanton gas approximation. We show that if the finite Euclidean-time structure is taken seriously by using exact saddles, the dilute gas can be sidestepped, allowing the partition function and energy levels to be computed systematically. At each instanton order, the full resurgent structure -- which saddles contribute, what asymptotic growth is expected and how ambiguities cancel -- is encoded in a finite-dimensional Picard--Lefschetz contour integral over the quasi-zero modes with a clear geometric interpretation. Working at finite $T$ is essential: the dilute instanton gas can only access the ground-state splitting, whereas the exact finite-$T$ computation systematically produces the non-perturbative energy splittings for all excited states, including their full dependence on the level number. The key ingredients -- Weierstrass elliptic functions for the saddles, Lamé operators for the fluctuations and Picard--Fuchs equations for the periods -- form a coherent mathematical framework that both overlaps and complements that of Exact WKB.

</details>

Abstract: In the framework of Soft de Sitter Effective Theory (SdSET), the Fokker-Planck equation for the late-time dynamics of the massless minimally coupled scalar field and its extension to the Kramers-Moyal equation are obtained from operator mixing of composite operators of the effective superhorizon field. Abstract: We derive the reduced Dirac Hamiltonian on the non-rotating BTZ background and use its redshift structure to construct a gauge-covariant single-band lattice model on the constant-time BTZ cylinder. In equal-area coordinates the AdS radius $L$ fixes the local Gaussian curvature, while the horizon radius $r_h$ fixes the throat size and the strength of the near-horizon redshift. The lattice model therefore has a direct geometric interpretation and is not presented as an unshown reduction of the two-component Dirac lattice. Its angular Fourier transform yields an exact curved Harper equation with BTZ-dependent hopping amplitudes and a consistent dimensionless angular quasi-momentum. We then supplement global parameter scans with state-resolved diagnostics: spectra color-coded by mean radius, local density of states, direct flux-response versus radius correlations, and Aharonov--Bohm spectral flow and persistent current on the BTZ cycle. Abstract: We present a theoretical analysis of the one-loop effective potential of a self-interacting real scalar field in the presence of two parallel conducting plates with geometric roughness. ### [95] [Emergent States and Algebras from the Double-Scaling limit of Pure States in SYK](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14387)
*Harshit Rajgadia,Jiuci Xu*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究AdS/CFT中大N极限的微妙性：微观理论的纯态在涌现可观测量代数下可能不保持纯态性质。通过分析SYK模型双标度极限中的Kourkoulou-Maldacena（KM）态，发现其系综平均代数描述取决于哪些算符在极限中存活，展示了通过添加态适应算符可恢复底层态的纯度。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近期研究强调了AdS/CFT中大N极限的微妙性：微观理论中的纯态序列在涌现可观测量代数下可能不保持纯态性质。本文旨在通过SYK模型双标度极限中的Kourkoulou-Maldacena（KM）态来具体研究这一现象。

Method: 研究SYK模型双标度极限中的Kourkoulou-Maldacena（KM）态，分析不同算符在极限中的存活情况。对于大小为N^{1/2}的费米子算符，一般算符收敛到双标度SYK的标准弦算符；同时识别出一类适应KM态且在双标度极限中存活的算符。

Result: 一般算符导致冯·诺依曼代数为标准Type II₁因子，无限温度下的KM纯态收敛到迹态，微观纯度对一般探测不可访问。添加适应KM态的算符后，极限代数变为Type I∞，极限态变为纯态。推导了修饰弦算符关联函数的精确修正弦图规则，分析了有限温度半经典和Schwarzian极限。

Abstract: Recent work has emphasized a subtlety of large- $N$ limits in AdS/CFT: a sequence of pure states in the microscopic theory need not remain pure with respect to the emergent algebra of observables. We study this phenomenon for Kourkoulou-Maldacena (KM) states in the double-scaling limit of the SYK model, and show that their ensemble-averaged algebraic description depends crucially on which observables survive the limit. For fermionic operators of size $N^{1/2}$, generic operators converge to the usual chord operators of double-scaled SYK. The resulting von Neumann algebra is the standard Type II$_1$ factor, and the KM pure states at infinite temperature converge to the tracial state, so generic probes lose access to microscopic purity. We then identify a class of operators adapted to the KM state that also survives the double-scaling limit. Since the KM state may be viewed as a projection inside the tracial state, these become dressed chord creation and annihilation operators. Once included, the limiting algebra becomes Type I$_\infty$ and the limiting state becomes pure. This gives a concrete example in which adding a sufficiently state-adapted operator to the emergent algebra restores access to the purity of the underlying state.
  We further show that correlators of the dressed operators admit exact modified chord-diagram rules, derive analytic expressions for uncrossed $2n$-point and crossed four-point functions, analyze their finite-temperature semiclassical and Schwarzian limits, study a deformation of the chord Hamiltonian that produces bound states and extends the correspondence with JT gravity plus an EOW brane to general brane tension, and identify an emergent $U(1)$ symmetry together with its finite-$N$ violation. Finally, we discuss analogies with boundary algebras proposed for black hole interiors and closed universes, and suggest lessons from our construction for both.

Focusing on static interface-type configurations, we determine the half-BPS condition on the spurion background and the corresponding supersymmetry projector. In the resulting half-BPS sector we derive the associated first-order BPS equation for static bosonic matter configurations and establish an exact Bogomol'nyi completion of the static energy, yielding a sharp bound saturated by BPS solutions. We further comment on how explicit coordinate dependence and derivative-dependent impurity couplings can obstruct the Bogomol'nyi structure, thereby motivating spurionic extensions that retain supersymmetric control over inhomogeneous deformations.

### [97] [Thermality Breakdown in Null-Shifted Rindler Wedges](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14453)

TL;DR: 本文研究了零移（null-shifted）Rindler楔形中量子场的行为，分析了与这些零形变相关的加速观测者感知到的粒子谱。研究发现，与标准Unruh效应不同，质量项的引入破坏了共形对称性，导致热性（thermality）基本失效，表现为非热响应。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Unlike the standard Unruh effect, our analysis compares two accelerated frames connected by a null displacement. We consider both massive scalar and Dirac fields, constructing their corresponding mode solutions in Rindler coordinates. Using normalised field expansions, we compute the Bogoliubov transformations between modes defined in the two null-shifted wedges. Our results demonstrate a fundamental breakdown of thermality: the presence of mass modifies the mode structure, rendering the characteristic exponential mixing of frequencies absent. This suggests that the massive field remains unexcited on this background, leading to a manifestly nonthermal response. These findings highlight that thermality in accelerated frames depends sensitively on the conformal symmetry of the field, which is broken by the introduction of a mass term.

</details>


### [98] [Spinning States and Unitarity in 3D Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14492)
*Ziyi Li*

Main category: hep-th

Abstract: We revisit the proposal to cure the negative density of states in the three-dimensional gravitational path integral by adding spinning states whose spin scales with the central charge. We show that sub-extremal and extremal spinning states below the black hole threshold can cancel the known negativities, and interpret these states as bulk spinning defects. Additionally, certain overspinning states above the black hole threshold can cure these negativities while preserving the spectral gap. Previously interpreted as classical spinning strings, we instead identify these overspinning states with overspinning BTZ geometries, which are smooth pure gravity quotients of AdS$_3$ with no fixed points. Abstract: Quasi-primary correlators in two-dimensional conformal field theories deformed simultaneously by $T\bar T$ and root-$T\bar T$ are studied. In this way, the mixed $T\bar T$/root-$T\bar T$ deformation is incorporated into the geometric description of irrelevant deformations, and the structure of local correlators beyond the pure $T\bar T$ case is characterized more explicitly.

### [107] [Monodromy Defects for Electric-Magnetic Duality, Hyperbolic Space, and Lines](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15117)
*Vladimir Bashmakov*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过共形映射到$AdS_{3} \times S^{1}$，研究了麦克斯韦理论中非可逆对称性的单值性缺陷（monodromy defects），并分析了威尔逊/'t Hooft线在这些缺陷附近的行为特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在探索麦克斯韦理论中非可逆对称性（non-invertible symmetries）的单值性缺陷，利用共形映射技术来研究这类缺陷的物理特性。

Method: 采用共形映射方法将问题映射到$AdS_{3} \times S^{1}$时空，通过这种几何框架分析单值性缺陷的谱结构，并详细研究威尔逊/'t Hooft线（Wilson/'t Hooft lines）在缺陷附近的行为。

Result: 成功恢复了缺陷共形原初场（defect conformal primaries）的谱，并发现威尔逊/'t Hooft线具有三个关键行为：i) 线可以在缺陷处终止；ii) 单位电荷的线可能不再是不可分解的，可以表示为更基本线的整数幂；iii) 线在接近缺陷时表现为拓扑对象，其行为由陈-西蒙斯理论（Chern-Simons theory）支配。

Conclusion: 通过$AdS_{3} \times S^{1}$的共形映射方法，系统地分析了非可逆对称性单值性缺陷的物理特性，揭示了威尔逊/'t Hooft线在缺陷附近的丰富拓扑行为，这些行为由陈-西蒙斯理论描述。

Abstract: In this note we explore monodromy defects for non-invertible symmetries in Maxwell theory, exploiting the conformal mapping to $AdS_{3} \times S^{1}$. With this approach we recover the spectrum of the defect conformal primaries. We also dedicate some time discussing the behaviour of Wilson/'t Hooft lines in the presence of such a monodromy defect, and highlight the following aspects of their behaviour: i) the lines can terminate on the defect, ii) lines of the unit electric (magnetic) charge may seize to be indecomposable, and can be represented as integer powers of some more elementary lines, and iii) they behave as topological objects when brought close to the defect, and this behaviour is governed by a Chern-Simons theory.

*Oleksandr Diatlyk,Zimo Sun,Yifan Wang*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究采用Gross-Neveu-Yukawa模型作为理论框架，针对一类缺陷重整化群流（defect renormalization group flows）进行分析。通过获得精确的红外解（infrared solutions）来揭示费米子反常（fermionic anomalies）在表面动力学中的编码机制。

Result: 获得了缺陷重整化群流的精确红外解，展示了费米子反常如何编码在表面动力学中。进一步发现了缺陷耦合空间（defect coupling space）中涌现的拓扑和几何结构（topological and geometric structures）。

Conclusion: 研究揭示了表面缺陷临界行为的新特征，包括反常编码机制和涌现的拓扑几何结构。这些发现与CFT距离猜想（CFT distance conjecture）的缺陷类似物存在潜在关联。

Abstract: Interacting fermions exhibit a rich landscape of surface defects and associated critical phenomena. We investigate novel surface critical behavior in the three-dimensional Gross-Neveu-Yukawa model. For a class of defect renormalization group flows, we obtain exact infrared solutions and show how fermionic anomalies are encoded in the resulting surface dynamics. ### [109] [Sampling the Graviton Pole and Deprojecting the Swampland](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15235)
*Guangzhuo Peng,Laurentiu Rodina,Anna Tokareva,Yongjun Xu*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该研究开发了一种基于有限分辨率采样（finite-resolution sampling）而非平滑化（smearing）的原始自举（primal bootstrap）框架，用于处理存在引力子极点（graviton pole）的有效场论（effective field theories）。该方法在D≥6时复现了已知的投影界限（projective bounds），在D=5时给出更强的约束，并能直接施加线性化幺正性（linearized unitarity）条件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于开发一种新的自举框架，以处理包含引力子极点的有效场论。传统方法采用平滑化处理，而本研究提出基于有限分辨率采样的方法，同时允许直接控制减除（subtractions）的数量，旨在获得更精确的理论约束。

Method: 该方法基于原始自举（primal bootstrap）框架，采用有限分辨率采样（finite-resolution sampling）而非平滑化（smearing）技术。通过交叉对称色散关系（crossing-symmetric dispersion relations），直接施加线性化幺正性（linearized unitarity）条件，并控制减除（subtractions）的数量。

Result: 在D≥6维度，该方法复现了已知的投影界限（projective bounds）；在D=5维度，获得了更强的约束条件。研究推导出新的非投影界限（non-projective bounds），固定了有效场论耦合（EFT couplings）的整体尺度，例如在D=5中发现M/MP≲7.8，表明有效场论截断（EFT cutoff）不能参数化地大于普朗克尺度（Planck scale）。

Conclusion: 该方法为处理包含引力子极点的有效场论提供了更精确的自举框架。极值谱（extremal spectra）显示出有趣的结构：对于投影界限，谱在类二次Regge轨迹（quadratic Regge-like trajectories）附近出现峰值；对于非投影界限，谱形成尖锐的二次带（quadratic bands），且主导系数（leading coefficients）与带数（band number）呈反二次依赖关系。

Abstract: We develop a primal bootstrap framework for effective field theories in the presence of a graviton pole, based on finite-resolution sampling rather than smearing, while also allowing direct control over the number of subtractions. We show that this approach reproduces the known projective bounds obtained from smearing in $D{\ge}6$, while yielding slightly stronger bounds in $D{=}5$. This method also makes it straightforward to impose linearized unitarity directly and provides an access to the extremal spectra. Applying the method to crossing-symmetric dispersion relations, we derive new non-projective bounds that fix the overall scale of the EFT couplings. In $D{=}5$, for example, we find that $\frac{M}{M_{\rm P}}{\lesssim}7.8$, showing that the EFT cutoff cannot be taken parametrically larger than the Planck scale. At the extremal values of the couplings, the spectra exhibit a surprising structure: for projective bounds, they exhibit peaks around quadratic Regge-like trajectories, while for the non-projective bounds they form sharp quadratic bands. In the latter case, the leading coefficients further display an inverse-quadratic dependence on the band number.

</details>


### [110] [Kontorovich-Lebedev-Fourier Space for de Sitter Correlators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15251)
*Nathan Belrhali,Arthur Poisson,Sébastien Renaux-Petel,Denis Werth*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文构建了(d+1)维德西特（de Sitter）时空关联函数的新颖频率-动量空间，基于时空等距群的不可约表示分解，建立了Kontorovich-Lebedev-Fourier（KLF）变换框架，并展示了其在微扰计算中的简化结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 论文旨在从第一性原理出发，为(d+1)维德西特（de Sitter）时空关联函数构建一个新颖的频率-动量空间。这一构造直接源于对时空等距群（spacetime isometry group）SO(1,d+1)的幺正不可约表示（unitary irreducible representations, UIRs）分解。

Method: 方法基于时空等距群SO(1,d+1)的幺正不可约表示分解：空间动量部分采用标准d维傅里叶变换，而频率空间则通过对角化二次卡西米尔算子（quadratic Casimir operator）获得，从而构建了(d+1)维Kontorovich-Lebedev-Fourier（KLF）变换。研究还应用路径积分公式推导了KLF空间中的in-in微扰理论费曼规则。

Result: 结果表明：平方可积函数仅沿主系列（principal series）分解，而更一般的函数可能包含来自其他UIRs的离散贡献。该框架应用于体CFT两点函数时重现了其Källén-Lehmann表示。KLF空间表述揭示了微扰计算的简单数学结构：传播子呈现为简单有理函数形式，树图可写为已知亚纯函数的谱积分，而圈图动量积分可重铸为SO(1,d+1)克莱布希-戈丹系数（Clebsch-Gordan coefficients）的正交关系。

Conclusion: KLF空间框架为德西特时空关联函数提供了基于群论的统一表述，显著简化了微扰计算结构。该构造通过群论性质将动量积分转化为正交关系，为高维德西特时空量子场论计算提供了系统工具。

Abstract: In this work, we build a novel frequency-momentum space for $(d+1)$-dimensional de Sitter (dS) correlators from first principles. This construction follows directly from the decomposition into unitary irreducible representations (UIRs) of the spacetime isometry group $\mathrm{SO}(1,d+1)$. While the spatial momentum space is given by the standard $d$-dimensional Fourier transform, the frequency space arises from diagonalising the quadratic Casimir operator, leading to the $(d+1)$-dimensional Kontorovich-Lebedev-Fourier (KLF) transform. We show that square-integrable functions decompose only along the principal series, whereas more general functions can receive discrete contributions from other UIRs. Applying this framework to the bulk CFT two-point function reproduces its Källén-Lehmann representation. Using the path integral formulation, we derive the Feynman rules for in-in perturbation theory in KLF space, leading to the introduction of KLF-space correlators, which are simply related to late-time correlation functions through a reduction formula. Furthermore, the KLF-space formulation sheds light on the simple mathematical structure of perturbative computations. In particular, the propagators take the form of simple rational functions, and tree-level diagrams can be written as spectral integrals over known meromorphic functions, as demonstrated in the example of the single-exchange four-point function. At the loop level, we show, through the example of the self-energy correction to the scalar propagator, that the group-theoretical nature of the construction allows the momentum integral to be recast as an orthogonality relation among $\mathrm{SO}(1,d+1)$ Clebsch-Gordan coefficients.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: A search for a resonance heavier than 250 GeV decaying into four leptons via two intermediate bosons is presented. The search uses proton-proton collision data at $\sqrt{s}$ = 13 TeV collected by the CMS experiment, corresponding to an integrated luminosity of 138 fb$^{-1}$. Novel techniques are used to enhance the sensitivity to a collimated pair of dileptons reconstructed as a single merged object, resulting from the decay of an intermediate light boson. No significant excess of data over the background predictions is observed. Upper limits are set on the production cross section for a four-lepton resonance, including the previously unexplored phase space at the LHC with a dilepton mass of 0.4$-$15 GeV.

Beyond this primary objective, LDMX offers a complementary search strategy for long-lived, visibly decaying particles, such as dark photons and axion-like particles.
  We present the first detailed evaluation of the ability of LDMX to identify visibly decaying, long-lived particles that couple to electrons using a detailed simulation, based on the Geant4-toolkit, that incorporates realistic detection efficiencies and background levels.

The models explored in this paper are distinct and complementary to those probed in the LDMX flagship missing-momentum analysis. Abstract: We present the first comprehensive study of the rare Dalitz decay $K^*(892) \rightarrow K \ell^+ \ell^- (\ell = e, μ)$, providing a prediction for the branching fraction and the dilepton mass spectrum. This decay involves the emission of a virtual photon which converts into a lepton pair, offering a probe of the transition form factor $F_{K^*K}(q^2)$ and underlying meson structure. Using a single pole approximation for the form factor, we present the calculation of the branching fraction for this rare decay channel for the first time. Furthermore, we also investigate the potential to search for a light $A^\prime$ boson (dark photon) appearing as a narrow resonance in the dilepton spectrum, and discuss the experimental sensitivity and new physics opportunities at the dedicated BESIII experiment. Our results establish $K^*(892) \rightarrow K \ell^+ \ell^- (l = e, μ)$ as a new laboratory for hadronic structure and dark-sector searches.

### [115] [Multiboson and VBS measurements in ATLAS and CMS](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14753)
*Santiago Folgueras*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文综述了LHC上ATLAS和CMS合作组在多重玻色子（multiboson）和矢量玻色子散射（vector boson scattering, VBS）方面的最新测量结果，包括精确的双玻色子截面测量、Wγ产生中的CP敏感和极化观测量、半轻子和全轻子末态中的VBS观测，以及三玻色子过程的观测，为检验标准模型电弱规范（electroweak gauge）部门提供了全面测试。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在综述大型强子对撞机（LHC）上ATLAS和CMS合作组在多重玻色子和矢量玻色子散射方面的最新测量进展，这些测量构成了对标准模型（Standard Model）电弱规范部门的全面检验，并为有效场论（effective field theory）框架下的反常规范耦合（anomalous gauge couplings）提供了严格约束。

Method: 方法基于对ATLAS和CMS合作组实验数据的分析，包括：精确的双玻色子（diboson）截面测量；Wγ产生中新颖的CP敏感（CP-sensitive）和极化（polarisation）观测量；半轻子（semileptonic）和全轻子（fully leptonic）末态中的矢量玻色子散射观测，其中包含首次在质心能量$\sqrt{s}$ = 13.6 TeV下的测量；以及三玻色子（triboson）过程的观测。

Result: 研究结果报告了多项重要测量：精确的双玻色子截面测量结果；Wγ产生中CP敏感和极化观测量的新发现；在13.6 TeV质心能量下首次观测到的半轻子和全轻子末态中的矢量玻色子散射；以及三玻色子过程的观测结果。这些结果为标准模型电弱规范部门提供了全面测试。

Conclusion: 这些多重玻色子和矢量玻色子散射的测量结果构成了对标准模型电弱规范部门的全面检验，并在有效场论框架下为反常规范耦合提供了严格约束，深化了对电弱相互作用的理解。

Abstract: A review of recent multiboson and vector boson scattering (VBS) measurements from the ATLAS and CMS Collaborations at the LHC is presented. Results are reported from precision diboson cross-section measurements, novel CP-sensitive and polarisation observables in $Wγ$ production, VBS observations in semileptonic and fully leptonic final states including the first measurements at $\sqrt{s}$ = 13.6 TeV, and observations of triboson processes. These results constitute a comprehensive test of the electroweak gauge sector of the Standard Model, and provide stringent constraints on anomalous gauge couplings in the effective field theory framework.

</details>

Zunica*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 首次在LHCb上研究$B^0 \to Λ_c^+ \barΛ_c^- K_S^0$衰变，测量其相对于$B^+ \to Λ_c^+ \barΛ_c^- K^+$的分支比（branching ratio）为$0.53 \pm 0.05 \pm 0.05$，并在$Λ_c^+ K_S^0$系统中发现两个共振态$Ξ_c(2923)^+$和$Ξ_c(2939)^+$的证据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 首次在LHCb实验上研究$B^0 \to Λ_c^+ \barΛ_c^- K_S^0$衰变过程，旨在测量其分支比并探索可能的共振态贡献。该研究利用质子-质子（proton-proton）对撞数据，为理解重子（baryon）衰变机制提供新数据。

Method: 使用LHCb实验在质心能量$\sqrt{s} = 13$ TeV下记录的质子-质子对撞数据，对应积分亮度（integrated luminosity）为5.4 fb$^{-1}$。通过相对分支比测量方法，将$B^0 \to Λ_c^+ \barΛ_c^- K_S^0$衰变与参考衰变$B^+ \to Λ_c^+ \barΛ_c^- K^+$进行比较。

Result: 测得相对分支比为$0.53 \pm 0.05 \pm 0.05$，其中第一项为统计不确定度（statistical uncertainty），第二项为系统不确定度（systematic uncertainty）。在$Λ_c^+ K_S^0$系统中发现两个共振态$Ξ_c(2923)^+$和$Ξ_c(2939)^+$的证据，相对于非共振假设（nonresonant hypothesis）的显著性（significance）为$3.9σ$。

Conclusion: 这两个$Ξ_c^+$态与在$Λ_c^+ K^-$系统中观测到的态一致，表明它们可能是同位旋伙伴（isospin partners）。该研究为理解重子共振态的性质提供了重要实验证据。

Abstract: The decay $B^0 \to Λ_c^+ \barΛ_c^- K_S^0$ is studied at LHCb for the first time using proton-proton collision data recorded by the LHCb experiment at a center-of-mass energy of $\sqrt{s} = 13$ TeV, corresponding to an integrated luminosity of 5.4 fb$^{-1}$. The branching ratio relative to the decay $B^+ \to Λ_c^+ \barΛ_c^- K^+$ is measured to be
  $$ \frac{{\cal B}(B^0 \to Λ_c^+ \barΛ_c^- K_S^0)}{{\cal B}(B^+ \to Λ_c^+ \barΛ_c^- K^+)} = 0.53 \pm 0.05 \pm 0.05, $$ where the first uncertainty is statistical and the second is systematic. Evidence is found for contributions from two resonant states, $Ξ_c(2923)^+$ and $Ξ_c(2939)^+$, in the $Λ_c^+ K_S^0$ system. The two states show a significance of $3.9σ$ relative to the nonresonant hypothesis. These two $Ξ_c^+$ states are consistent with being the isospin partners of the states observed in $Λ_c^+ K^-$ system.

</details>

*Andrea Malara*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文总结了CMS实验在高质量区域的最新物理结果，包括重矢量玻色子搜索组合、W'粒子搜索、双喷注角分布分析以及双喷注重振态对产生搜索，未发现超出标准模型预期的显著偏差。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于CMS实验的Run~2和Run~3数据，采用多种分析方法：重矢量玻色子搜索的组合分析、W'→ℓν衰变道搜索、双喷注角分布分析，以及在包容性和b标记末态中对产生双喷注重振态的搜索。

Result: 在所有分析中均未观测到显著偏离标准模型预期的信号，新结果将CMS实验在多个基准场景中对多TeV能标的敏感性进一步扩展。

Conclusion: CMS实验在高质量区域的系统搜索未发现新物理证据，但显著提升了实验对多TeV能标新物理的探测灵敏度，为未来更高能量的探索奠定了基础。

Abstract: Searches at high object masses probe both resonant production of new particles and nonresonant distortions of Standard Model spectra. This contribution follows the material presented in the Moriond Electroweak 2026 talk and summarizes recent CMS results in this regime: the Run~2 combination of heavy vector boson searches, the Run~3 search for $W^\prime \to \ell ν$, the Run~2 dijet angular analysis, and searches for pair-produced dijet resonances in inclusive and $b$-tagged final states. No significant deviation from the SM expectation is observed, and the new results extend the sensitivity of CMS to multi-TeV scales in several benchmark scenarios.

Method: 研究基于LHCb实验的近期搜索工作，包括多项首次搜索和迄今最严格的限制结果。具体方法涉及对多种稀有衰变过程的系统搜索与分析。

Abstract: Rare and very rare decays of third-generation particles, including $b$-hadrons and $τ$ leptons, provide sensitive probes of physics beyond the Standard Model (SM). Unlike direct searches limited by collider energies, they probe new physics at much higher energy scales. Many of these decays have SM-predicted branching fractions below the sensitivity of current detectors. These proceedings report on recent LHCb searches, including several first searches and results setting the most stringent limits to date. In particular, searches for $b \to s τ^+τ^-$, $b \to s τ^\pm e^\mp$, $b \to s μ^\pm e^\mp$, and $τ^- \to μ^-μ^+μ^-$ are presented, alongside searches for lepton-number-violating processes and loop-suppressed annihilation decays.

### [119] [Evaporative thermo-fluidics and deposition patterns in surface-active droplets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14380)
*Randeep Ravesh,A R Harikrishnan,Purbarun Dhar*

Main category: physics.flu-dyn

TL;DR: 该研究通过实验和理论分析，探讨了含表面活性剂液滴蒸发过程中的热溶质输运现象和沉积模式。研究发现表面活性剂浓度和基底润湿性显著影响蒸发速率和液滴内部对流，其中溶质马兰戈尼对流（Marangoni solutal advection）主导输运过程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探究含表面活性剂液滴蒸发过程中的热溶质输运现象和沉积模式，重点关注表面活性剂浓度和基底润湿性对蒸发动力学的影响。通过实验和理论分析，揭示不同对流机制（如溶质马兰戈尼对流、热马兰戈尼对流和浮力驱动流）的相对重要性。

Method: 采用实验和理论尺度分析相结合的方法。实验使用悬垂液滴（sessile droplet）配置，在丙烯酸（acrylic）腔室中对亲水性和疏水性基底进行研究。采用红外热成像（infrared thermography）和粒子图像测速（particle image velocimetry, PIV）分别测量温度分布和速度分布。通过阴影成像（shadowgraphy imaging）计算蒸发速率，并进行表面张力和粘度测量。

Result: 十二烷基硫酸钠（Sodium dodecyl sulphate, SDS）表面活性剂分子在疏水表面上随浓度增加而提高蒸发速率；而在亲水基底上，蒸发速率在0.5临界胶束浓度（critical micelle concentration, CMC）前增加，随后降低。研究发现液滴内部对流强烈依赖于表面活性剂浓度和润湿性，溶质马兰戈尼对流（Marangoni solutal advection）主导其他对流机制。表面活性剂拥挤（surfactant crowding）和粘性阻力会抑制溶质对流的增加。接触线速度（contact line velocities）计算显示突然波动，表明液滴干燥过程中的粘滑行为（stick slip behaviour）。

Conclusion: 表面活性剂浓度和基底润湿性共同调控液滴蒸发过程中的输运现象。溶质马兰戈尼对流是主导机制，但表面活性剂拥挤和粘性阻力会限制其对流增强效应。实验观察到的粘滑行为与微观视觉观察相互印证，揭示了液滴干燥过程中的复杂动力学。

Abstract: We investigate the thermo solutal transport phenomena and deposition patterns during the evaporation of surfactant laden droplets experimentally and through theoretical scaling based analysis. Experiments were conducted using the sessile droplet configuration in the acrylic chamber for both hydrophilic and hydrophobic substrates. Infrared thermography and particle image velocimetry measurements were conducted during evaporation to illustrate the temperature and velocity distributions, respectively. Sodium dodecyl sulphate SDS surfactant molecules enhanced the evaporation rate with an increase in concentration for the hydrophobic surface. In contrast, the evaporation rate increased up to 0.5 CMC and then decreased for droplets on a hydrophilic substrate. The evaporation rates computed from the shadowgraphy imaging were explained using the average velocities obtained from the PIV analysis. It was found that advection within the droplet is strongly dependent on surfactant concentration and wettability. Further, the theoretically obtained Marangoni velocities were in close agreement with the experimental values. It was found that Marangoni solutal advection dominates other advection mechanisms, such as Marangoni thermal advection and buoyancy driven flow. However, surfactant crowding and viscous resistance with increasing surfactant concentration can dampen the increase in solutal advection. The surface tension and viscosity measurements were also conducted with variation in surfactant concentration to understand the suppression of advection by viscous forces. The computation of contact line velocities showed sudden fluctuations, illustrating stick slip behaviour during droplet drying, complementing microscopic visual observations.

### [120] [Superstatistical Approach to Turbulent Circulation Fluctuations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15277)
*Henrique S. Lima,Rodrigo M. Pereira,Luca Moriconi,Katepalli R. Sreenivasan*

Main category: physics.flu-dyn

TL;DR: 该论文发现湍流环量概率分布函数可采用超统计（superstatistical）的q指数（q-exponential）形式精确描述，这为在非广延统计力学框架下探索湍流级联的统计结构开辟了新途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近期对湍流环量涨落的研究揭示了流动结构统计组织的重要见解，并发现了湍流间歇性（turbulent intermittency）的意外几何特征。特别值得关注的是，环量概率分布函数可接受超统计（superstatistical）表示，即基于"玻尔兹曼-吉布斯系综（Boltzmann-Gibbs ensembles）的系综"的描述。

Method: 该方法的基本唯象要素依赖于耗散场与基本环量承载结构（即小尺度涡旋）空间分布之间的强相关性。在超统计语言中，这对应于通过适当选择条件（类玻尔兹曼）分布和混合分布来表征环量统计特性。

Result: 研究表明，已知在多尺度和非平衡系统中具有广泛适用性的超统计类q指数（q-exponential），能够精确描述均匀各向同性湍流中观测到的环量统计特性。

Conclusion: 这一发现为在非广延统计力学（non-extensive statistical mechanics）背景下探索湍流级联（turbulent cascade）的统计结构开辟了新途径，该理论植根于非可加熵（non-additive entropies）的概念。

Abstract: Recent investigations of turbulent circulation fluctuations have uncovered substantial insights into the statistical organization of flow structures and revealed unexpected geometric features of turbulent intermittency. Of particular interest here is the observation that circulation probability distribution functions admit a superstatistical representation, namely a description based on "ensembles of Boltzmann-Gibbs ensembles". A fundamental phenomenological ingredient of this approach, which serves as a natural starting point for modeling, relies on the strong correlation between the dissipation field and the spatial distribution of elementary circulation-carrying structures, i.e., small-scale vortices. Within the language of superstatistics, this corresponds to characterizing circulation statistics through an appropriate choice of conditioned (Boltzmann-like) distributions and mixing distributions. We show that the superstatistical class of q-exponentials, known to have broad applicability in a wide range of multiscale and non-equilibrium systems, provides an accurate description of the observed circulation statistics in homogeneous and isotropic turbulence. This finding opens avenues for exploring the statistical structure of the turbulent cascade in the context of non-extensive statistical mechanics, rooted in the concept of non-additive entropies.

### [121] [An efficient Wavelet-Based Hamiltonian Formulation of Quantum Field Theories using Flow-Equations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14594)
*Mrinmoy Basak,Debsubhra Chakraborty,Nilmani Mathur*

Main category: hep-lat

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种基于Daubechies小波基的有效哈密顿量（effective Hamiltonian）表述，结合相似重整化群（SRG）的流方程方法，为量子场论分析提供了降维和尺度解耦的高效框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在开发一种能够降低哈密顿量维度并系统解耦不同尺度自由度的量子场论分析框架。通过结合小波基和重整化群方法，解决传统方法在处理多尺度问题时的计算复杂性。

Method: 采用Daubechies小波基在位置空间构建量子场论的有效哈密顿量表述，结合相似重整化群（similarity renormalization group, SRG）的流方程方法。该方法将自由标量场理论（free scalar field theory）重构为耦合局域振子理论，并通过SRG解耦不同分辨率模式。

Result: 哈密顿量被自然组织为固定分辨率块（fixed-resolution blocks）和不同分辨率间相互作用块。应用SRG流方程后，实现了哈密顿量的块对角化（block diagonalized）。随着分辨率增加，低能谱可从哈密顿量的最低分辨率有效块中提取，显著降低了计算成本。

Conclusion: 该框架通过小波基和SRG方法的结合，为量子场论分析提供了高效的多尺度处理工具，实现了哈密顿量维度的显著降低和计算成本的大幅减少，特别适用于低能谱的提取。

Abstract: We propose an effective Hamiltonian formulation of quantum field theories using a Daubechies wavelet basis in position space. Combined with flow-equation methods of the similarity renormalization group (SRG), this approach provides an efficient framework for analyzing quantum field theories by reducing the dimensionality of the Hamiltonian and systematically decoupling degrees of freedom across scales. As an application, the free scalar field theory has been reformulated within this framework to calculate the low-lying energy spectrum of the theory. These basis elements are known to transform the free scalar field theory into a theory of coupled localized oscillators, each of which is labeled by a location and a resolution index. In this representation, the Hamiltonian is naturally organized into fixed-resolution blocks, alongside blocks associated with the interactions between different resolutions. To decouple the different resolution modes and obtain a block diagonalized Hamiltonian with each block associated with a fixed resolution, the flow equation approach of SRG is applied. Finally, we demonstrate that with increasing resolution, the low-energy spectrum can be extracted from the effective lowest-resolution block of the Hamiltonian, leading to a significant reduction in computational cost.

### [122] [A minimal implementation of Yang--Mills theory on a digital quantum computer](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15132)
*Georg Bergner,Masanori Hanada,Emanuele Mendicelli*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究旨在为数字量子模拟设计一个最小化的SU(N)纯杨-米尔斯理论实现方案，以实现在量子计算中的优势。特别关注降低资源需求，特别是通过改进收敛到无限质量极限的方法，避免了对大标量质量的要求。

Method: 研究基于轨道折叠（orbifold）晶格模拟协议，该协议在局部希尔伯特空间截断中具有对数标度。在此基础上引入了进一步简化的哈密顿量，并测试了改进收敛到无限质量极限的简单方法。对于SU(2)理论，通过利用SU(2)≅S³嵌入ℝ⁴的几何特性进一步削减资源需求。使用欧几里得路径积分的蒙特卡洛模拟来基准测试这些新的分析改进。

Conclusion: 这些结果为基于非紧致变量的方法作为非阿贝尔规范理论量子模拟的实用框架提供了进一步支持。该最小化实现方案为在量子设备上实现量子优势铺平了道路。

Abstract: We present a minimal implementation of SU($N$) pure Yang-Mills theory in $3+1$ dimensions for digital quantum simulation, designed to enable quantum advantage. Building on the orbifold lattice simulation protocol with logarithmic scaling in the local Hilbert-space truncation, we introduce further simplified Hamiltonians. Furthermore, we test simple methods that improve the convergence to the infinite mass limit, thereby removing the requirement of a large scalar mass to obtain the Kogut-Susskind Hamiltonian. For the SU(2) theory, we can cut the resource requirement further by utilizing the embedding of $\mathrm{SU}(2)\cong\mathrm{S}^3$ into $\mathbb{R}^4$. Monte Carlo simulations of the Euclidean path integral were used to benchmark the accuracy of these new analytical improvements to the theory. These results provide further support for the noncompact-variable-based approach as a practical framework for quantum simulation of non-Abelian gauge theories.

### [123] [Self-contact in a buckled elastica](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14304)
*Krishnan Suryanarayanan,Parth Patel,Anup Kumar Pathak,Harmeet Singh*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了无摩擦自接触条件下末端加载屈曲弹性杆的力学行为，提出了自接触起始的尺度不变条件，计算了多种屈曲模式的后接触构型，并揭示了奇模对称后接触构型中点接触向线接触转变需要无限大的力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究屈曲弹性杆（buckled elastica）在无摩擦自接触条件下的力学行为，旨在理解自接触起始条件和后接触构型的特性，这对于柔性结构设计和接触力学分析具有重要意义。

Method: 利用与弹性杆相关的两个积分，提出了自接触起始的尺度不变条件（scale-invariant condition）；通过保持哈密顿量（Hamiltonian）积分，计算了固定-固定边界条件下模式三到十的后接触构型。

Result: 自接触起始条件与边界条件无关，不涉及材料点的位置向量，并能给出自接触起始时的压缩载荷值；对于模式八和九，在给定压缩载荷下存在多个后接触构型；奇模对称后接触构型中点接触向线接触转变需要无限大的力。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了屈曲弹性杆自接触起始的普适条件，揭示了后接触构型的多样性，并证明了奇模对称构型中点接触向线接触转变的力学限制，为柔性结构接触分析提供了理论框架。

Abstract: We explore the mechanics of a terminally loaded buckled elastica under frictionless self-contact. With the aid of two integrals associated with the elastica, we propose a scale-invariant condition necessary for the onset of contact. The condition is independent of the boundary conditions, does not involve the position vectors of the material points, and delivers the value of the compressive load at which self-contact initiates. Furthermore, we show that one of the two integrals, namely the \emph{Hamiltonian}, persists after contact. We compute post-contact configurations of modes three through ten for a pinned-pinned buckled elastica. At a given value of the compressive load, we report multiple post-contact configurations for modes eight and nine. Finally, we show that an infinite force is required to transition from a point contact to a line contact in symmetric post-contact configurations of odd modes.

### [124] [Simulating hydrodynamic interactions in colloidal suspensions using multiparticle collision dynamics with rigid-body constraints](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14307)
*Michaela Bush,Jeremy C. Palmer,Michael P. Howard*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文开发了一种使用多粒子碰撞动力学（MPCD）模拟胶体悬浮液的方法，采用刚性体离散粒子模型，相比谐波键模型计算效率显著提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 需要开发更高效的胶体悬浮液模拟方法，特别是针对复杂形状胶体粒子的模拟。现有方法如谐波键模型存在计算开销大和时间步长受限的问题。

Method: 采用多粒子碰撞动力学（multiparticle collision dynamics, MPCD）结合刚性体离散粒子模型。关键步骤包括：在MPCD碰撞步骤前对离散位点速度进行热化处理，然后将动量从位点传递到刚性体。

Result: 刚性体模型对单个球形粒子产生预期的统计结果，对硬球胶体悬浮液产生与谐波键模型相同的输运性质。该模型计算开销更小，允许更大的模拟时间步长，在硬球胶体悬浮液基准测试中实现近一个数量级的加速。

Conclusion: 该方法兼容任意离散化，能够更高效地模拟复杂形状胶体粒子的悬浮液，为MPCD模拟提供了计算优势。

Abstract: We develop a method for simulating colloidal suspensions using multiparticle collision dynamics (MPCD) with a discrete particle model represented as a rigid body. The key steps for incorporating the rigid-body constraints are to thermalize the velocities of the discrete sites before they participate in the MPCD collision step, then transfer momentum from the sites to the rigid body. We demonstrate that the rigid-body model produces the expected statistics for a single spherical particle and the same transport properties for a hard-sphere colloidal suspension as an equivalent model using harmonic bonds to maintain the site geometry. Importantly, the rigid-body model has less computational overhead and permits a larger simulation timestep than the harmonic-bond model, leading to a nearly order of magnitude speedup in benchmark simulations of hard-sphere colloidal suspensions. Our method is compatible with arbitrary discretization, so it enables more efficient MPCD simulations of suspensions of colloidal particles with complex shapes.

</details>


### [125] [Persistent Free Volume Governs (Anti-)plasticization in Chitosan-Water Mixtures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14559)
*Baris E. Ugur,Michael A. Webb*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 壳聚糖（chitosan）作为一种多功能可持续聚合物，在生物和材料工程领域具有广泛应用潜力，但其固有的脆性限制了其更广泛的应用。通过与小分子添加剂（如水分）共混可以调控其热机械性能，但相关分子机制尚需深入理解。

Method: 采用分子动力学（molecular dynamics, MD）模拟研究壳聚糖-水混合物在不同含水量下的行为。通过弹性模量分解分析聚合物-聚合物相互作用与聚合物-水相互作用的竞争关系，并引入基于动态可及自由体积区域的简单模型来解释聚合物迁移率变化。

Result: 模拟结果显示，随着含水量增加，壳聚糖首先经历抗塑化（antiplasticization）随后转变为塑化（plasticization）。弹性模量分解揭示了弱化的聚合物-聚合物相互作用与增强的聚合物-水相互作用之间的竞争关系。研究发现，添加剂可及体积区域（additive-accessible volume regions）的连通性是实现自由体积区域可及性的关键。

Conclusion: 本研究阐明了决定壳聚糖-水混合物性能的分子相互作用机制，提出的动态可及自由体积区域模型能够有效解释弹性性能的（抗）塑化现象。这些发现为壳聚糖基材料及其他水合生物聚合物（hydrated biopolymers）的理性设计提供了重要指导。

Abstract: Chitosan is a highly versatile and sustainable polymer with a broad range of potential biological and materials engineering applications. Despite its versatility, the native brittleness of chitosan limits its broader utilization. This limitation can be addressed by blending chitosan with small-molecule additives to modulate its thermomechanical properties. We employ molecular dynamics (MD) simulations to investigate the mechanism underlying antiplasticization followed by plasticization at increasing water content. Decomposition of the elastic moduli reveals a competition between weakened polymer-polymer interactions and enhanced polymer-water interactions, with their relative strengths governing the resulting properties. We introduce a simple model incorporating dynamically accessible free volume regions as a key driver of polymer mobility, effectively capturing the (anti-)plasticization of elastic properties. We show that accessibility of free volume regions is enabled by connectivity of additive-accessible volume regions. This study provides new insights into the molecular interactions that dictate the properties of chitosan-water mixtures and may inform the rational design of chitosan-based materials and other hydrated biopolymers.

Abstract: Solid phase of dense granular matter is inevitable because of jamming transition when the packing fraction or the pressure suffered is high enough. ### [127] [Highly coarse-grained polarisable water models for mesoscopic simulations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14873)

Inclusion of such phenomena when using larger-than-atomistic techniques such as coarse-grained molecular dynamics (CG-MD) and dissipative particle dynamics (DPD) is still an open question, to which we provide a novel way to consider and justify the necessary and suitable coarse-graining level, enabling us to compare new polar CG models' performance against that of an underlying atomistic model. ### [128] [Effect of sub-critical fluid shear flow on granular bed strength](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14936)
*Dong Wang,Sophie Bodek,Nicholas T. Ouellette,Mark D. Shattuck,Corey S. O'Hern*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究通过离散元方法（DEM）模拟揭示了亚临界流体流动对颗粒床强度方向性增强与减弱的微观机制，发现床面颗粒的可移动性分数与床强度高度相关，且各向异性强度仅持续有限时间尺度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 流体与颗粒材料相互作用在地表普遍存在，亚临界流体流动会导致颗粒床在流动方向上强度增强，而在相反方向上强度减弱。本研究旨在探究控制这种方向性强度变化的颗粒尺度机制。

Method: 采用离散元方法（discrete element method, DEM）模拟颗粒床在二维（2D）和三维（3D）模型流体流动中的行为，通过改变颗粒间静摩擦系数和调节流动速度来研究微观机制。

Result: 研究发现颗粒床在特定方向上的强度与在该方向上可被流体力移动的表面颗粒分数高度相关，且各向异性床强度仅持续由希尔兹数（Shields number）设定的有限时间尺度。颗粒间静摩擦并非床强度各向异性的必要条件，但会影响各向异性的幅度。

Conclusion: 该研究增强了流体流动引起颗粒床侵蚀的颗粒尺度理解，并强调了追踪床面结构历史的重要性，因为床面结构与床强度存在强耦合关系。

Abstract: Interactions between fluids and granular materials are prevalent on the Earth's surface. In the case of fluid flow over a sediment bed, the fluid imparts a shear stress to the granular materials. When the applied shear stress is above a critical value, the grains become entrained in the fluid flow. Prior experimental studies have shown that granular beds subjected to a sub-critical fluid flow can strengthen in the same direction as the sub-critical flow. In contrast, granular beds can become weaker in the direction opposite to the sub-critical fluid flow. To investigate the grain-scale mechanisms that control directional strengthening and weakening, we perform discrete element method (DEM) simulations of granular beds subjected to model fluid flows in two (2D) and three (3D) dimensions with varied inter-particle static friction coefficients and conditioning flow speeds. In these studies, the sub-critical grain motion does not cause significant bed compaction. Instead, we find that the strength of a granular bed in a particular direction is highly correlated with the fraction of {\it surface} grains that can be dislodged by a fluid force applied in that direction. Further, the anisotropic bed strength only persists over a finite time scale that is set by the Shields number. We also show that inter-particle static friction is not required for bed strength anisotropy, but varying the friction affects the magnitude of the anisotropy. This research enhances the grain-scale understanding of erosion of granular beds caused by fluid flows and underscores the importance of tracking the history of the fabric of the bed surface since it couples strongly to bed strength.

### [129] [Multispecific DNA-Coatings for Self-Assembly](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15021)
*T. C. M. Stevens,A. van der Sluis,I. K. Voets,P. G. Moerman*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本研究比较了两种在微米级胶体颗粒上接枝多种DNA序列的方法，发现基于点击化学的方法批次间变异大，而基于等温DNA聚合的方法能精确控制涂层组成但需测量反应速率。自组装实验表明，即使精确控制涂层组成，多种DNA包被颗粒的平衡共组装仍受限于同一窄温度窗口内可逆相互作用的数量，突显了在结构设计中需要明确纳入顺序组装途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: DNA包被颗粒因其序列特异性杂交特性而具有正交相互作用编程能力，是构建功能性和有限尺寸组装体的有前景构建模块。为充分利用这种可编程性，需要开发能结合多种不同DNA序列且比例可调的涂层颗粒，并理解涂层组成如何影响自组装过程。

Method: 研究比较了两种在微米级胶体颗粒上接枝多种DNA序列的策略：基于点击化学的方法和基于等温DNA聚合的方法。通过自组装实验评估了涂层组成对组装过程的影响，特别关注了平衡共组装的限制因素。

Result: 点击化学方法产生的混合涂层在组成上存在较大的批次间变异，而等温DNA聚合方法能产生组成可预测的涂层，精度达几个百分点，但需要测量涂层中每个新序列的反应速率。自组装实验表明，即使精确控制涂层组成，多种DNA包被颗粒的平衡共组装仍受限于同一窄温度窗口内可逆相互作用的数量。

Conclusion: 通过多特异性DNA涂层系统调节相互作用强度和顺序组装是实现有限尺寸和动态结构实验构建的先决条件，这些结构目前仍主要停留在理论层面。研究结果强调了在结构设计中需要明确纳入顺序组装途径，其中涂层组成决定了结合事件的顺序。

Abstract: DNA-coated particles are promising as building blocks for functional and finite-sized assemblies because they can be programmed with orthogonal interactions owing to the sequence-specific hybridization of DNA strands. To fully exploit this programmability, it is important to develop particles with coatings that incorporate multiple distinct DNA sequences in tunable ratios and to understand how the coating composition influences self-assembly. Here, we compared two strategies to graft multiple DNA sequences in tunable and well-defined ratios on micron-sized colloidal particles. We found that a method based on click chemistry yielded mixed coatings with large batch-to-batch variation in the composition, while a method based on isothermal DNA polymerization produced coatings of predictable composition with a precision of a few percent, but requires reaction rate measurements for each new sequence in the coating. Our self-assembly experiments showed that, even with precise control over coating composition, equilibrium co-assembly of multiple types of DNA-coated particles is limited by the number of interactions that are reversible within the same narrow temperature window. This finding highlights the need to explicitly incorporate sequential assembly pathways into structure design, with coating composition dictating the order of binding events, Together, our results show how systematic tuning of interaction strength and sequential assembly through multispecific DNA coatings is a prerequisite for the experimental realization of finite-sized and dynamic structures that have so far remained largely theoretical.

### [130] [Passivity-Driven Order--Disorder Transitions in Self-Aligning Active Matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15105)
*Weizhen Tang,Amir Shee,Zhangang Han,Pawel Romanczuk,Yating Zheng,Cristián Huepe*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索被动组分比例作为活性系统中物理相关控制参数的作用，揭示其在活性-被动混合体系中如何影响自组织动力学（self-organizing dynamics）和相变行为。

Method: 研究方法包括对具有各项同性或各项异性迁移率的密集被动-主动自对准圆盘混合体系进行模拟研究，并从微观朝向动力学（microscopic heading dynamics）推导出平均场方程（mean-field equation）来描述系统行为。

Result: 研究结果表明，被动组分比例控制着有序-无序转变，该转变在各项同性迁移率下为连续相变，在各项异性迁移率下为不连续相变。在转变附近，两种有序体系都能表现出多种亚稳态振荡或旋转态（metastable oscillating or rotating states），具体取决于被动粒子的空间排列和晶格缺陷（lattice defects）。

Conclusion: 研究结论揭示了被动组分比例作为活性系统中物理相关控制参数的重要性，能够导致丰富的自组织动力学。各项同性迁移率体系在模拟过程中会访问多个长寿命吸引子（long-lived attractors），而各项异性迁移率体系则被单一吸引子所捕获，表现出不同的瞬态动力学（transient dynamics）。

Abstract: We study dense mixtures of passive and active self-aligning disks with isotropic or anisotropic mobility. We find that the passive fraction controls an order-disorder transition that is continuous in the isotropic case and discontinuous in the anisotropic one. A mean-field equation derived from the microscopic heading dynamics captures this dichotomy. Near the transition, both ordered regimes can exhibit multiple metastable oscillating or rotating states, depending on the spatial arrangement of passive particles and lattice defects, but with different transient dynamics: Systems with isotropic mobility visit multiple long-lived attractors during each simulation while systems with anisotropic mobility are trapped by a single attractor. Our results reveal the passive fraction as a physically relevant control parameter in active systems, leading to rich self-organizing dynamics.

### [131] [Orientational bistability and field-controlled switching of a superparamagnetic dimer](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15212)
*James R. N. Tett,Finlay Johnston,Brennan Sprinkle,Alice L. Thorneywork*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究分析了超顺磁性胶体二聚体（superparamagnetic colloidal dimers）在磁场中的取向动力学，揭示了其双稳态取向分布和场控动力学响应转变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在理解同时具有感应磁矩（induced magnetic moment）和有效永久磁矩（effective permanent moment）的胶体二聚体在磁场中的取向行为，以揭示其内部磁结构特性。

Method: 通过施加静态均匀磁场（static, uniform magnetic field）和周期性反转磁场，观察二聚体的取向动力学，并建立包含强感应和弱体固定分量的磁响应模型来解释观察到的现象。

Result: 在静态磁场中，二聚体在两个优选平面角之间跳跃，形成双峰稳态取向分布（bimodal steady-state orientation distribution）。周期性反转磁场时，观察到从Δθ≪π的小跳跃到Δθ≈π的完整旋转的场控转变。通过结合取向偏差、分岔场强和短时取向方差，确定了净永久偶极矩（net permanent dipole）的大小和方向。

Conclusion: 二聚体的静态双稳态和切换分岔可由其磁响应特性解释，该响应包含强感应和弱体固定分量，形成了复杂的取向能量/势能景观。这种分析方法能够通过显微技术表征颗粒的内部磁结构细节。

Abstract: We study the orientational dynamics of superparamagnetic colloidal dimers that carry both an induced magnetic moment, proportional to the applied field, and an effective permanent moment. In a static, uniform magnetic field, dimers that are permanently fixed together hop between two preferred in-plane angles, developing a bimodal steady-state orientation distribution. When the same field is periodically reversed, we observe a sharp, field-controlled change in the dynamical response from small hopping events with $Δθ\ll π$ to full $Δθ\approx π$ rotations on each field flip. We show that both the static bistability and the switching bifurcation can be rationalised by a magnetic response in the dimer that consists of both a strong induced and weak body-fixed component. This leads to a complex orientational energy/potential landscape, with coupled roll-yaw rotations of the dimer responsible for the bistable dynamics. By combining the misorientation between dimer axis and field, bifurcation field strength and short-time orientational variance, we determine the magnitude and orientation of the net permanent dipole, thereby characterising details of the internal magnetic structure of the particles via microscopy.

</details>

### [132] [Configuration-dependent electronic and optical properties of 2D Mo$_{1-x}$W$_x$S$_2$ alloys across the full composition range](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14377)
*M. Szyszko,M. Birowska*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究通过密度泛函理论和蒙特卡洛模拟分析了Mo$_x$W$_{1-x}$S$_2$合金的原子构型对其电子和光学性质的影响，发现局部原子排列显著影响能带边缘分裂、谷结构、有效质量各向异性和光学选择定则。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在理解等电子和等结构的Mo$_x$W$_{1-x}$S$_2$合金中，不同对称性不等价的原子构型如何影响其电子和光学性质，特别是局部原子排列对材料特性的调控作用。

Method: 采用密度泛函理论（density-functional theory）和蒙特卡洛模拟（Monte Carlo simulations）方法，分析了整个成分范围内多个对称性不等价的原子构型。

Result: 研究发现：1) 即使无自旋轨道耦合（SOC），整个成分范围内K点处能带边缘均出现分裂；2) 价带顶（VBM）相对稳定，而导带底（CBM）呈现强烈的构型依赖性分裂（几meV至几百meV）；3) 分离良好的导带支持超出传统A和B激子的额外光学活性跃迁；4) 空穴有效质量在VBM处表现出构型依赖的各向异性。

Conclusion: 光学活性跃迁的数量和特性不仅由成分决定，还受原子微观排列的调控；局部对称性破缺导致方向依赖的输运特性，表明原子构型在合金性质设计中具有关键作用。

Abstract: Here we analyze multiple symmetry-inequivalent atomic configurations across the entire composition range of the isovalent and isostructural Mo$_x$W$_{1-x}$S$_2$ alloy using density-functional theory and Monte Carlo simulations. Our results show that although structural stability and energetics are largely composition-driven, the electronic and optical properties exhibit configuration dependence, with local atomic arrangements critically shaping band-edge splitting, valley structure, effective-mass anisotropy, and optical selection rules. In contrast to the pristine monolayers, even in the absence of spin-orbit coupling (SOC), splitting of the band edges at the $K$ point is observed across the entire composition range. In particular, while the valence-band maximum (VBM) remains largely robust, the conduction-band minimum (CBM) shows strong configuration-dependent splitting from few meV up to hundredths of meV. This behaviour leads to a non-trivial dependence of the valley energetics. Configurations with well-separated conduction bands support additional optically active transitions beyond the conventional A and B excitons in MoS$_2$ and WS$_2$ monolayers, whereas nearly degenerate cases exhibit a reduced number of allowed transitions, observed for specific configurations at $x = 1/3$ and $x = 2/3$. These results demonstrate that the number and character of optically active transitions are governed not only by composition, but also by the microscopic arrangement of atoms. Moreover, we found the hole effective masses at the VBM show configuration-dependent anisotropy, reflecting sensitivity to local symmetry breaking and implying direction-dependent transport.

### [133] [Ultra-high-vacuum cluster tool for epitaxial synthesis and optical spectroscopy of reactive 2D materials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14443)
*M. Dembecki,J. Schabesberger,M. Bissolo,A. Thurn,A. Ulhe,P. Avdienko,J. Ulrichs,H. Riedl,G. Koblmüller,E. Zallo,J. J. Finley*

Motivation: 大面积合成高质量二维材料是半导体技术中新材料集成的核心需求。这需要开发能够保持材料原始状态、揭示其本征特性的制备与表征技术，特别是针对在环境条件下不稳定的二维半导体材料。

Method: 研究构建了全超高真空簇系统，结合分子束外延（molecular beam epitaxy）生长二维半导体，并集成了低温（20 K）光致发光（photoluminescence）和拉曼散射（Raman scattering）光谱表征。系统采用闭循环低温恒温器（closed-cycle cryostat）实现20-300 K温度控制，并开发了基于解卷积的算法，利用系统特定的点扩散函数（point-spread function）在振动条件下恢复空间信息。

Result: 该系统展示了微米级空间分辨率、整个晶圆的扫描能力、精确的温度控制和长期保存性能。通过生长后的后过渡金属单硫族化合物（post-transition metal monochalcogenides）验证了系统性能，实现了对生长材料在原始状态下结构特性和光电特性的原位分析。

Conclusion: 该全超高真空簇系统能够对生长后的二维材料在原始状态下进行原位分析，为基础研究和可扩展二维材料生长的优化提供了丰富且可重复的反馈，推动了先进器件集成的发展。

Abstract: The large-area synthesis of high-crystalline-quality two-dimensional (2D) materials is at the core of novel material integration for semiconductor technology. This effort relies on developing fabrication and characterization techniques that can uncover the material's intrinsic properties by preserving its pristine conditions. In this article, we present an all ultra-high-vacuum cluster for the growth using molecular beam epitaxy of 2D semiconductors that are unstable under ambient conditions and optical spectroscopy using low temperature (20 K) photoluminescence and Raman scattering. The optical chamber of the setup provides micrometer scale spatial resolution and the ability to scan the entire wafer. The performance of its setup regarding spatial resolution, temperature control over a temperature range of 20-300 K using a closed-cycle cryostat and long-term preservation are demonstrated using as-grown post-transition metal monochalcogenides. Furthermore, we introduce a deconvolution-based algorithm to recover spatial information under vibration using a system-specific point-spread function. This enables in situ analysis of the structural and optoelectronic properties of as-grown materials in their pristine form, providing rich and reproducible feedback for both fundamental studies and the optimization of scalable 2D material growth toward integration in advanced devices.

### [134] [Environment-dependent tight-binding models from ab initio pseudo-atomic orbital Hamiltonians](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14470)
*Marco Buongiorno Nardelli*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种环境依赖紧束缚（EDTB）框架，通过键屏蔽函数增强Slater-Koster跳跃积分，能够为大型系统生成具有从头算精度的哈密顿量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统紧束缚模型虽然计算高效，但缺乏从头算精度；而从头算方法虽然精确，但计算成本高，难以处理大型系统。需要一种既能保持从头算精度又能高效处理大体系的电子结构计算方法。

Method: 基于从头算赝原子轨道（PAO）哈密顿量与Slater-Koster紧束缚模型的对应关系，开发了环境依赖紧束缚（EDTB）框架。通过键屏蔽函数增强Slater-Koster跳跃积分，捕捉局部配位环境的影响。所有参数通过同时拟合多个原子构型的PAO本征值谱来确定。

Result: 该方法在四个原型系统上展示了效率和精度：块体铂、硅表面、Si/Ge[001]超晶格以及包含多达4,324个原子的扭曲双层石墨烯。该方法能够生成具有从头算精度的大型系统哈密顿量，并实现了物理上有意义且可迁移的模型。

Conclusion: 环境依赖紧束缚框架成功地将从头算精度与紧束缚模型的计算效率相结合，为大型系统的电子、光学和输运性质计算提供了有效工具。该方法已集成到paoflow代码中，能够无缝使用其完整的后处理套件。

Abstract: \textit{Ab initio} pseudo-atomic orbital (PAO) Hamiltonians express the electronic structure of a solid in a compact, localized basis that spans the same Hilbert space as a conventional Slater--Koster tight-binding model, thereby providing an exact \textit{ab initio} representation without any loss of accuracy. Building on this correspondence, we develop an environment-dependent tight-binding (EDTB) framework in which Slater--Koster hopping integrals are augmented with bond-screening functions that capture the local coordination environment. All parameters are determined by fitting to the PAO eigenvalue spectrum across multiple atomic configurations simultaneously, which breaks the degeneracy between screening and hopping parameters and yields physically meaningful, transferable models capable of generating Hamiltonians for large systems with \textit{ab initio} precision. We demonstrate the efficiency and accuracy of the approach on four prototypical systems: bulk platinum, silicon surfaces, Si/Ge~[001] superlattices, and twisted bilayer graphene with up to $4{,}324$ atoms. The method is implemented in the \paoflow{} code and integrates seamlessly with its full post-processing suite, enabling the evaluation of a broad range of electronic, optical, and transport properties.

Method: 开发了一种基于晶体正规形式（Crystal Normal Form）的新算法，该形式提供了晶体构型空间（crystal configuration space）的图表示，并作为路径寻找算法的基础。该方法能够识别亚稳态多晶型物与基态对应物之间的无扩散相变路径（diffusionless transformation pathways）。

Abstract: As the number of theoretically predicted materials continues to grow, it becomes increasingly important to assess not only their thermodynamic stability but also their kinetic viability under realistic synthesis conditions. In this study, we investigate the hypothesis that the kinetic persistence of a metastable polymorph is related to the topography of the potential energy landscape separating it from lower energy phases. To accomplish this, we develop a new method for identifying diffusionless transformation pathways between metastable polymorphs and their ground-state counterparts and discuss the energetics of those pathways with respect to the experimental observation of each phase. This algorithm is underpinned by the recently developed Crystal Normal Form, which provides a graph representation of crystal configuration space and supplies the substrate for our pathfinding algorithm. We focus on the vibrational modes at the zone center to establish the relation between vibrational modes and their corresponding point-group symmetries, which determine the Raman and infrared spectra but also report the full Brillouin zone phonon dispersions and density of states. ### [137] [Anomalous Platinum and Oxygen Transport during Electroforming of NbOx Memristors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14680)
*Shimul Kanti Nath,Sanjoy Kumar Nandi,Xiao Sun,Sujan Kumar Das,Bin Gong,Nicholas J. Ekins-Daukes,Deepak Mishra,Mahesh P. Suryawanshi,William D. A. Rickard,Songyan Yin,Michael P. Nielsen,Robert G. Elliman*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统观点认为金属-氧化物-金属（metal-oxide-metal）忆阻器的电形成过程仅涉及氧化物内部氧空位（oxygen-vacancy）丝的形成，而铂（Pt）等贵金属电极保持化学惰性。本研究旨在探究Pt/NbOx/Nb2O5/Pt器件中电形成和后续操作的真正机制。

Method: 采用飞行时间二次离子质谱（time-of-flight secondary ion mass spectrometry）分析器件内部元素分布，结合有限元（finite-element）和集总参数（lumped-element）建模，模拟电流控制负微分电阻（negative-differential-resistance）操作产生的局部焦耳加热（Joule heating）和高频热循环效应。

Result: 实验发现沿丝状路径存在微米尺度的氧富集区，从Nb2O5层延伸至NbOx层并深入铂顶电极。令人意外的是，同时形成了富铂丝沿相同路径穿透氧化物堆叠。模型表明电流控制负微分电阻操作产生的局部加热和热循环强烈增强了氧迁移，并促进了铂沿空位富集路径的热辅助扩散。

Conclusion: 这些发现揭示了NbOx忆阻器中先前未被认识的金属离子传输机制，强调了电形成后电气动力学在决定丝化学组成、稳定性和器件可靠性方面的关键作用。

Abstract: Electroforming of metal-oxide-metal memristors is generally attributed to the creation of oxygen-vacancy filaments within the oxide, with noble metal electrodes such as Pt and Au remaining chemically inert. Here, we demonstrate that electroforming and subsequent operation of Pt/NbOx/Nb2O5/Pt devices can induce an unexpected and highly correlated redistribution of both oxygen and platinum. Time-of-flight secondary ion mass spectrometry reveals a filamentary pathway characterized by micrometer-scale oxygen enrichment extending from the Nb2O5 layer through NbOx and deep into the Pt top electrode. Surprisingly, this is accompanied by the formation of a Pt-rich filament penetrating the oxide stack along the same filamentary path. Finite-element and lumped-element modelling show that current-controlled negative-differential-resistance operation produces localized Joule heating and high-frequency thermal cycling, which strongly enhances oxygen migration and enables thermally assisted Pt diffusion along vacancy-rich pathways. These findings reveal a previously unrecognized metal-ion transport mechanism in NbOx memristors and highlight the critical role of post-forming electrical dynamics in determining filament chemistry, stability, and device reliability.

### [138] [Morphological Transition: From Meanders to Mound Structures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14750)
*Marta A. Chabowska,Hristina Popova,Magdalena A. Załuska-Kotur*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 平坦与偏切（miscut）晶体表面的丘状结构形成表现出不同的生长行为。平坦表面以丘状结构为主，而偏切表面则根据内外条件从蜿蜒模式平滑过渡到三维丘状结构，需要系统研究这种形态演化的机制。

Method: 采用近邻元胞自动机（vicinal Cellular Automata）建模框架，模拟了从蜿蜒表面模式到面化金字塔结构的形态演化。模拟覆盖了广泛的生长条件，包括沉积通量、表面扩散率、温度和偏切角的变化。

Result: 研究表明，从丘状构型到规则台阶蜿蜒模式的转变由Ehrlich-Schwoebel势垒与台阶平台扩散率（terrace diffusivity）的竞争所控制。在中等势垒强度和足够高的平台扩散率下，系统表现出从丘状构型到规则台阶蜿蜒模式的可逆转变。通过高度-高度相关函数（height-height correlation function）计算了沿台阶和跨台阶的相关长度，并分析了其标度行为。

Conclusion: 研究揭示了动力学势垒与质量输运之间的复杂相互作用，为连接不同类型表面结构的连续体路径提供了见解，并为描述不同晶体生长机制下的模式演化提供了统一框架。

Abstract: Mound formation on flat and miscut crystal surfaces exhibits distinct growth behaviors. While mound structures are the predominant feature on flat surfaces, miscut surfaces display a smooth transition from meandered patterns to three-dimensional mounds, depending on both internal and external conditions. We investigate this morphological evolution-from meander-like surface patterns to faceted pyramidal structures-using a vicinal Cellular Automata modeling framework. The transition is shown to be governed by the competition between the Ehrlich-Schwoebel barrier and adatom mobility on terraces. Under moderate barrier strengths and sufficiently high terrace diffusivity, the system demonstrates a reversible transition from mounded configurations to regular step meandered patterns. This reveals a complex interplay between kinetic barriers and mass transport. Our simulations cover a wide range of growth conditions, including variations in deposition flux, surface diffusion rates, temperature, and miscut angle. By applying the height-height correlation function, we calculate the correlation lengths along and across the steps and analyze their scaling behavior. These results offer insight into the continuum pathways that connect distinct classes of surface structures and provide a unified framework for describing pattern evolution across different crystal growth regimes.

Abstract: Rutile RuO$_2$ has attracted great interest recently, as its magnetic ground state remains controversial. Experimental studies have reported either nonmagnetic or altermagnetic (AM) ground states in different crystalline samples of RuO$_2$, highlighting the need for a reasonable explanation to resolve this contradiction. In this study, density functional theory calculations are performed to reveal the correlation-sensitive and strain-dependent magnetism of bulk RuO$_2$. On one hand, multiple AM phases with different magnitudes of the spin magnetic moment are identified in the Hubbard parameter space for RuO$_2$. On the other hand, when appropriate strains which significantly change the crystal cell volume are applied, the ground state of RuO$_2$ can undergo transitions between the nonmagnetic state with no spin splitting and the magnetic states with spin splitting in the band structure. These findings not only demonstrate intriguing physics in 4d-electron-correlated RuO$_2$, but also retain its potential for spintronic applications.

### [140] [Spin-Valley-Mismatched Altermagnet for Giant Tunneling Magnetoresistance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14776)

Method: 开发了一种基于隧穿的自旋输运理论，明确纳入了交变磁体输运通道中横向波矢（$\bf{k}_\|$）依赖的自旋极化。基于该理论预测了KV₂Se₂O的磁电阻极限，并通过第一性原理输运计算进行验证。

In this work, we develop a tunneling-based spin-transport theory that explicitly incorporates the transverse-wavevector ($\bf{k}_\|$)-dependent spin polarization of an altermagnet's transport channels, enabling the prediction of giant tunneling magnetoresistance (TMR). Based on the theory, we predict that the altermagnet KV$_2$Se$_2$O can reach the extreme limit of magnetoresistance. By performing first-principles transport calculations, we verify that magnetic tunnel junctions using the metallic KV$_2$Se$_2$O as the electrodes and few-layer MgO as the spacer exhibit zero-bias magnetoresistance larger than $7.57\times10^7$\%, which is robust against the bias and thickness of the spacer. Motivation: 本研究旨在探索两相共晶固体的熔化动力学，特别是定向熔化过程中温度梯度下的图案形成机制。研究动机源于对共晶熔化基本物理过程的理解需求，这对于涉及熔化/凝固循环的增材制造等应用具有重要意义。

Method: 研究方法结合了使用透明共晶合金的原位薄样品实验（in situ, thin-sample experiments）与针对同一合金校准的二维相场模拟（two-dimensional phase field simulations）。通过改变熔化速度$V_m$和预凝固层状微观结构的间距$λ$，系统研究图案形成过程。

Result: 研究观察到出乎意料的丰富多样的熔化图案，实验与模拟结果吻合良好。揭示了三种主要的物理机制及其标度行为：(i) 高熔化速度下液体沿固-固界面的渗透，(ii) 低熔化速度下初生相指状物的增厚，(iii) 小间距$λ$值下的周期倍化不稳定性（period-doubling instability）。

Conclusion: 该研究为共晶熔化的进一步研究提供了理论基础，特别是在涉及熔化/凝固循环的增材制造（additive manufacturing）过程中。研究揭示了熔化动力学中复杂的图案形成机制，为相关工业应用提供了科学依据。

Abstract: We present a study of the melting dynamics of a two-phase eutectic solid. In situ, thin-sample experiments using a transparent eutectic alloy and two-dimensional phase field simulations calibrated for the very same alloy are combined to assess pattern formation during directional melting in a temperature gradient. Depending on the melting velocity $V_m$ and the spacing $λ$ of the pre-solidified lamellar microstructure, an unexpectedly rich diversity of melting patterns is observed, with good agreement between experiments and simulations. We unravel the different physical mechanisms leading to this diversity, and establish the scaling behaviors of (i) the penetration of the liquid along the solid-solid interface at large $V_m$, (ii) the thickening of the primary-phase fingers at low $V_m$, and (iii) a period-doubling instability for small $λ$ values. Our study provides a fundamental basis for further investigations of eutectic melting, including additive manufacturing during which melting/solidification cycles take place.

Corrugation is found to provide further stabilization to the layered structures with all methods. We observe that HSE06-D3 method provides results in good agreement with experimental data and with more sophisticated G0W0 calculations. Based on that, we exploited the method to investigate the nature of the bulk triplet excitons in these C3N4 structures to evaluate the S0-T1 energy difference, the selftrapping triplet exciton energy and the photoluminescence emission energy, since this is a promising vis-light photocatalyst. Nanostructuring (0D and 2D) is another relevant aspect of these materials in practical applications, therefore we have considered the effect of single or multilayer exfoliation or space confinement in nanoparticles. Here, we report visualization of bulk altermagnetic domains in MnTe based on scanning magneto-optical Kerr-effect microscopy using telecom infrared wavelength. We found two distinct TRSB domains with large Kerr rotations that do not scale with its tiny bulk magnetization. Method: 研究通过理论计算分析了二维AgBiO3、NaBiO3和SbTlO3在考虑相对论效应时的电子结构变化。通过元素替代（Tl被Pb取代形成SbPbO3）调控能带特征，并计算拓扑不变量和边缘态以确认拓扑性质。

Given the functional properties of ferroelectrics are crucially determined by the crystal symmetry, resolving this matter is imperative. In this work, we settle the controversy through extensive 3D reciprocal space surveys made possible via synchrotron-based grazing incidence diffraction from epitaxial films of both phases.   <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 基于氧化铪的铁电随机存取存储器中有限的剩余极化是密度缩放和可靠性的主要障碍，而材料和工艺优化只能提供渐进式改进。这一限制从根本上源于厚度受限的可切换极化和氧化铪基铁电体的本征极化上限。

Method: 提出了一种全原子层沉积生长的垂直互补铁电随机存取存储器架构，其中顶部和底部堆叠的铁电存储器单元保持互补极化。采用互补极化写入-读取方案，从顶部到底部看，"上-下"极化对存储逻辑'1'，而"下-上"对存储逻辑'0'。

Result: VCF实现了超过100 μC/cm²的有效差分极化，并在1e10次开关循环后保持在90 μC/cm²以上而无电击穿。展示了稳健的保持特性（85°C下超过1e4秒）和强抗干扰能力，在V/3方案下1e6次干扰脉冲后有效差分极化仍超过80 μC/cm²。在5×5无选择器交叉点阵列中验证了阵列级操作。

Conclusion: VCF的性能提升源于全原子层沉积生长工艺、器件架构和操作方案的协同优化，为可扩展的铁电随机存取存储器集成实现了高密度、宽存储窗口和强可靠性。

Abstract: A limited remanent polarization (Pr) in HfO2-based FeRAM remains a key obstacle to density scaling and reliability, while material and process optimizations offer only incremental improvements. This limitation fundamentally originates from the thickness-constrained switchable polarization and the intrinsic polarization ceiling of HfO2-based ferroelectrics. Here, we propose an all-ALD-grown vertical complementary FeRAM (VCF) architecture, in which the top and bottom stacked FeRAM cells maintain complementary polarization. This complementary dipole configuration converts the readout from a single-layer polarization response into a differential polarization summation, thereby amplifying the effective charge window without increasing the switching field of each individual layer or incurring area overhead. Viewed from top to bottom, an "up-down" polarization pair stores logic '1', whereas a "down-up" pair stores logic '0'. Using a complementary polarization write-read scheme, the VCF achieves an effective differential polarization above 100 uC/cm^2 and retains above 90 uC/cm^2 after 1e10 switching cycles without electrical breakdown. Robust retention (longer than 1e4 s at 85 degC) and strong disturb immunity are demonstrated, with an effective differential polarization above 80 uC/cm^2 under a V/3 scheme after 1e6 disturb pulses. Array-level operation is validated in a 5 x 5 selector-free crosspoint array. The performance enhancement of the VCF arises from the co-optimization of the all-ALD-grown process, device architecture, and operation scheme, enabling high density, a wide memory window, and strong reliability for scalable FeRAM integration.

</details>

Result: 通过多维超光谱拟合程序，即使对于强烈重叠的模式，也能从散射强度的角度依赖性中提取相对拉曼张量元素。实验测得的模式频率与第一性原理计算结果吻合良好。

Conclusion: 研究成功识别并归属了正交晶系LaInO₃中大多数Γ点声子到D₂ₕ点群的不可约表示，为理解该材料的晶格动力学性质提供了重要参考。

Abstract: In this study, we present a comprehensive analysis of the Raman active phonon modes in orthorhombic LaInO$_3$ based on a combination of polarization-angle resolved Raman spectroscopy and density functional theory calculations. By using backscattering from multiple crystallographic surface orientations and employing a full symmetry analysis, we identify and assign most of the Raman-active $Γ$-point phonons to their irreducible representations of the D$_{\rm{2h}}$ point group. A multidimensional hyperspectral fitting procedure allows us to extract the relative Raman tensor elements from the angular dependence of the scattering intensities, even for strongly overlapping modes. First-principles calculations yield the phonon dispersion along high-symmetry directions, the phonon densities of states, and atomic displacement patterns, which are found to be in good agreement with the experimental mode frequencies.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 计算确认所有缺陷构型都具有动态和热力学稳定的三重态基态和更高能量的单重态，电子态在带隙内形成尖锐孤立峰，在近红外光谱范围内具有强烈的光学激发，适合作为光学可控自旋量子比特。
