Abstract: By applying our methodology, we propose a defect in 4H-SiC which combines a Si vacancy and a C atom substituted with S (VSiSC) to have a spin-triplet ground state with the spin qubit functionality. Our calculations confirm that all configurations of the defect have a dynamically and thermodynamically stable triplet ground state and higher energy singlet states, essential for the spin-qubit polarization cycle. From GW calculations, we found that the electronic states associated with the defect form sharp and isolated peaks within the band gap for both triplet and singlet states. Further Bethe-Salpeter-equation calculations show that all considered configurations have intense optical excitations in the near infrared spectrum range. Analysis of the excitation energies and rates indicate that the VSiSC defect can be an excellent optically controlled spin qubit. Crucially, the host elements and the dopant have high-abundance isotopes with zero nuclear spin ensuring high spin-coherence time of the qubit.

### [152] [Entanglement and circuit complexity in finite-depth random linear optical networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14277)
*Laura Shou,Joseph T. Iosue,Yu-Xin Wang,Victor Galitski,Alexey V. Gorshkov*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该研究分析了随机被动线性光学网络中纠缠和电路复杂度随电路深度的增长行为。对于纠缠动力学，研究者证明了在随机砖墙电路中，Rényi-2熵的纠缠增长至多为扩散性增长。同时，他们建立了确保平均子系统纠缠接近最大值的深度界限，以及随机线性光学幺正算符与Haar随机幺正算符在L^2 Wasserstein距离上接近的深度界限。对于一维砖墙电路的鲁棒电路复杂度，研究显示其随深度至多为扩散性标度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究随机被动线性光学网络（random passive linear optical networks）中纠缠和电路复杂度随电路深度的演化行为。这类网络在量子光学和量子信息处理中具有重要应用，理解其动力学特性对于设计和分析量子光学系统至关重要。

Method: 采用随机砖墙电路（random brickwall circuits）作为研究模型，从初始高斯态（Gaussian state）出发，所有n个模式均处于压缩态。通过分析Rényi-2熵（Rényi-2 entropy）来量化纠缠增长，并建立深度界限以确保平均子系统纠缠接近最大值。同时，研究随机线性光学幺正算符与Haar随机幺正算符（Haar random unitary）在L^2 Wasserstein距离上的接近程度。对于电路复杂度分析，考虑一维砖墙电路，测量实现近似线性光学幺正算符所需的最小门数量。

Result: 对于随机砖墙电路，纠缠（以Rényi-2熵衡量）随深度的增长至多为扩散性增长。建立了确保平均子系统纠缠在常数因子内接近最大值的深度界限，以及确保随机线性光学幺正算符在L^2 Wasserstein距离上接近Haar随机幺正算符的深度界限。对于一维砖墙电路的鲁棒电路复杂度（robust circuit complexity），研究显示其随深度至多为扩散性标度，且相应的近似高斯幺正算符在约束期望光子数的纯态上保持高输出保真度。

Conclusion: 随机被动线性光学网络中的纠缠增长和电路复杂度均呈现扩散性标度行为。这些结果为理解量子光学系统中纠缠和复杂度的演化提供了理论界限，对于设计高效的量子光学电路和评估其性能具有重要意义。

Abstract: We study the growth of entanglement and circuit complexity in random passive linear optical networks as a function of the circuit depth. For entanglement dynamics, we start with an initial Gaussian state with all $n$ modes squeezed. For random brickwall circuits, we show that entanglement, as measured by the Rényi-2 entropy, grows at most diffusively as a function of the depth. In the other direction, for arbitrary circuit geometries we prove bounds on depths which ensure the average subsystem entanglement reaches within a constant factor of the maximum value in all subsystems, and bounds which ensure closeness of the random linear optical unitary to a Haar random unitary in $L^2$ Wasserstein distance. We also consider robust circuit complexity for random one-dimensional brickwall circuits, as measured by the minimum number of gates required in any circuit that approximately implements the linear optical unitary. Viewing this as a function of the number of modes and the circuit depth, we show the robust circuit complexity for random one-dimensional brickwall circuits scales at most diffusively in the depth with high probability. The corresponding Gaussian unitary $\tilde{\mathcal U}$ for the approximate implementation retains high output fidelity $|\langleψ|\mathcal U^\dagger \tilde{\mathcal U}|ψ\rangle|^2$ for pure states $|ψ\rangle$ with constrained expected photon-number.

</details>


### [153] [Optimal Quantum Logarithmic Trace Inequality](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14617)
*Gilad Gour*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文建立了一个尖锐的对数迹不等式（logarithmic trace inequality），用更小的常数$G_s$取代了Cheng等人工作中的$c_s/s$，该常数通过Lambert $W$函数给出闭式表达式，并在量子信息论中改进了关键原语（primitives）的有限资源界限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在强化Cheng等人近期工作中建立的对数迹不等式，通过寻找更小的最优常数来改进相关界限。这种改进对于量子信息理论中的关键原语（包括解耦、凸分裂和覆盖引理）具有重要意义，能够获得更紧的有限资源界限。

Method: 本文引入了一种迭代分部积分（iterative integration-by-parts）方法，该方法能够将最优标量界限无损地提升到算子层面。通过这种方法，作者证明了$G_s$是最优的通用常数，其中$G_s$由标量不等式$\log(1+r)\le G_s r^s$定义，并可通过Lambert $W$函数给出闭式表达式。

Result: 研究结果表明，$G_s$是最优的通用常数，即不存在更小的常数能够对所有正算子（positive operators）满足该不等式。对于密度矩阵（density matrices），当$s\le \frac{1}{2\log(2)}$时该最优性仍然成立；超过此阈值时，交换情形（commuting case）存在严格更小的最优常数，而非交换情形（noncommuting case）仍为开放问题。在$s\to0$的极限下，本文结果将Cheng等人的前置因子$c_s/s$改进了$1/e$倍。

Conclusion: 本文建立的尖锐对数迹不等式通过引入更小的最优常数$G_s$，显著改进了现有界限。这些更尖锐的不等式增强了量子信息理论中的关键原语，包括解耦（decoupling）、凸分裂（convex-splitting）和覆盖引理（covering lemmas），从而获得了更紧的有限资源界限。

Abstract: We establish a sharp logarithmic trace inequality that strengthens recent bounds of Cheng et al.(arXiv:2507.07961) by replacing their prefactor $c_s/s$ with the strictly smaller constant $G_s$. The constant $G_s$ is defined via the scalar inequality $\log(1+r)\le G_s r^s$ and admits a closed-form expression in terms of the Lambert $W$ function. Our approach introduces an iterative integration-by-parts procedure that lifts optimal scalar bounds to the operator level without loss. We prove that $G_s$ is the optimal universal constant, in the sense that no smaller constant satisfies the inequality for all positive operators. For density matrices, this optimality persists up to $s\le \frac{1}{2\log(2)}$, while beyond this threshold the commuting case exhibits a strictly smaller optimal constant and the noncommuting case remains open. In the regime $s\to0$, our result improves the prefactor $c_s/s$ of Cheng et al. by a factor of $1/e$. These sharper inequalities enhance key primitives in quantum information theory, including decoupling, convex-splitting, and covering lemmas, leading to tighter finite-resource bounds.

</details>


### [154] [Integrable, Mixed, and Chaotic Dynamics in a Single All-to-All Ising Spin Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14798)
*David Amaro-Alcalá,Carlos Pineda*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文证明了全连接伊辛模型（Ising all-to-all model）在不同对称性区块中展现出从可积到混沌的动力学行为范围，包括混合行为，为量子混沌研究提供了新平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 虽然已有研究通过改变参数探索全连接系统的动力学，但本文旨在分析固定参数下不同对称性区块内的动力学行为，并研究系统对噪声的鲁棒性。

Method: 通过将系统的每个对称性区块映射到受击陀螺（kicked top, KT），并观察每个区块的KT参数如何依赖于其维度，从而分析系统的动力学特性。

Result: 研究发现全连接伊辛模型在不同对称性区块中展现出从可积到混沌的动力学范围，包括混合行为；当代表噪声的哈密顿量范数接近1时，系统对噪声保持鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 该系统类似于经典混沌中的布尼莫维奇台球（Bunimovich billiard），为研究由对称性区块决定的动力学提供了新平台，推动了量子混沌研究的发展。

Abstract: We demonstrate that the Ising all-to-all (ATA) model exhibits a range of dynamics, from integrable to chaotic, including mixed behaviour across symmetry blocks within a single system. While other works have explored the dynamics of all-to-all systems by varying parameters, we analyse a fixed set of parameters and examine the dynamics within different blocks. In addition to investigating the dynamical properties, we show that the system remains resilient to noise when the norm of the Hamiltonian representing the noise is close to 1. Our results are presented by mapping each symmetry sector of the system to a kicked top (KT) and observing that KT parameters for each sector depend on its dimension. This system, similar to the Bunimovich billiard for classical chaos, provides a new platform for studying dynamics determined by the symmetry sector, advancing quantum chaos research.

</details>


### [155] [Time-Dependent Logarithmic Perturbation Theory for Quantum Dynamics: Formulation and Applications](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14812)
*Juan Carlos del Valle,Paul Bergold,Karolina Kropielnicka*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于对数微扰理论（logarithmic perturbation theory）的时间依赖扩展方法，用于处理含时薛定谔方程（Schrödinger equation）支配的非相对论量子动力学，通过波函数对数的耦合常数展开获得封闭积分形式的微扰修正。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有时间无关的对数微扰理论需要扩展到时间依赖情形，以研究含时量子系统。该方法旨在为含时多光子过程（time-dependent multi-photon processes）的解析研究提供一种有前景的替代方案。

Method: 将波函数的对数在耦合常数（coupling constant）的幂次上展开，构建由未扰动系统的规范旋转哈密顿量（gauge-rotated Hamiltonian）支配的微扰修正方程层次结构。基于Duhamel公式获得含时修正的封闭积分表达式（closed-integral expressions）。

Result: 该方法保持了时间无关对数微扰理论的封闭积分结构，提供了瞬时能量移动（instantaneous energy shift）的可计算表达式。动态能量移动以赝势（pseudopotentials）的时间平均期望值形式自然出现，可关联到AC斯塔克移动（AC Stark shifts）和电极化率（electric polarizabilities）。在谐振子和氢原子受含时激光场驱动的应用中，前者恢复了精确解，后者展示了原子系统的适用性。

Conclusion: 数值模拟支持该方法能以高精度获取相关物理可观测量。该含时对数微扰理论扩展为微扰区域内的含时多光子过程解析研究提供了有前景的替代方法。

Abstract: We present a time-dependent extension of logarithmic perturbation theory for nonrelativistic quantum dynamics governed by the Schrödinger equation, in which the logarithm of the wave function is expanded in powers of a coupling constant. The resulting hierarchy of equations defining the perturbative corrections is governed by a gauge-rotated Hamiltonian of the unperturbed system and leads to closed-integral expressions for the time-dependent corrections based on Duhamel's formula. This closed-integral structure of corrections is a hallmark of time-independent logarithmic perturbation theory and is preserved in the present extension. This structure, in particular, provides a computable expression for the instantaneous energy shift. Furthermore, dynamic energy shifts arise naturally within this framework in the form of time-averaged expectation values of pseudopotentials and can be related, for example, to AC Stark shifts and electric polarizabilities. As an illustration, we apply the method to the harmonic oscillator and the hydrogen atom, both driven by a time-dependent laser field. The harmonic oscillator provides a proof of principle for which the exact solution is recovered, while the hydrogen atom illustrates the method applied to atomic systems. Supported by numerical simulations, we demonstrate the applicability to obtain relevant physical observables with high accuracy. The present approach offers a promising alternative for analytical studies of time-dependent multi-photon processes in the perturbative regime.

</details>


### [156] [Computing the free energy of quantum Coulomb gases and molecules via quantum Gibbs sampling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15263)
*Simon Becker,Cambyse Rouzé,Robert Salzmann*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文开发了一种量子算法，用于估计有限温度下相互作用量子库仑气体（Coulomb gas）和分子系统的自由能（free energy）及总吉布斯态（Gibbs state）。该算法通过有限秩低能截断（finite-rank low-energy truncation）和量子吉布斯采样（quantum Gibbs sampling）方案，为具有奇异相互作用（singular interactions）和无限维希尔伯特空间（infinite-dimensional Hilbert space）的系统提供了首个严格的混合时间保证（mixing-time guarantee）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法无法处理具有奇异相互作用和无限维希尔伯特空间结构的相互作用量子库仑气体和分子系统。这些系统在有限温度下的自由能和吉布斯态估计面临理论挑战，需要开发新的量子算法来超越经典近似方法（如玻恩-奥本海默近似（Born-Oppenheimer reduction））的限制。

Method: 首先，通过有限秩低能截断将全多体哈密顿量（full many-body Hamiltonian）的自由能近似问题转化为受控的有限秩微扰问题（finite-rank perturbation problem）。其次，针对截断系统设计了一种基于量子马尔可夫半群（quantum Markov semigroups）的量子吉布斯采样方案，并证明了其生成元（generator）具有严格正谱隙（strictly positive spectral gap）。最后，给出了动力学的显式量子电路实现（quantum circuit implementation）。

Result: 主要分析结果表明，对于每个截断，相关生成元都具有严格正谱隙，这意味着向目标吉布斯态的指数收敛（exponential convergence）。这为库仑相互作用的连续变量量子系统中的吉布斯采样提供了首个严格的混合时间保证。同时，推导了近似自由能和吉布斯态本身的端到端复杂度界限（end-to-end complexity bound）。

Conclusion: 该研究为相互作用量子系统中的自由能估计提供了一条数学上严格的量子算法路径，无需依赖玻恩-奥本海默近似等经典近似方法。所提出的方法能够处理现有方法无法触及的奇异相互作用系统，为量子库仑气体和分子系统的模拟开辟了新途径。

Abstract: We develop a quantum algorithm for estimating the free energy as well as the total Gibbs state of interacting quantum Coulomb gases and molecular systems in dimensions $d \in \{2,3\}$ at finite temperature. These systems lie beyond the reach of existing methods due to their singular interactions and infinite-dimensional Hilbert space structure. First, we show that the free energy of the full many-body Hamiltonian can be approximated by that of the same Hamiltonian with a finite-rank low-energy truncation of the interaction, with an explicit error bound polynomial in the particle number. This reduces the problem to a controlled finite-rank perturbation problem. Second, we introduce a quantum Gibbs sampling scheme tailored to this truncated system, based on a class of quantum Markov semigroups. Our main analytical result establishes that the associated generator has a strictly positive spectral gap for every truncation, implying exponential convergence to the target Gibbs state. This provides, to our knowledge, the first rigorous mixing-time guarantee for Gibbs sampling in a Coulomb interacting continuous-variable quantum system. Finally, we give an explicit quantum circuit implementation of the dynamics and derive an end-to-end complexity bound for approximating the free energy and the Gibbs state itself. Our results provide a mathematically rigorous route to quantum algorithms for free energy estimation in interacting quantum systems, without relying on classical approximations such as the Born-Oppenheimer reduction.

</details>


### [157] [Ensembles of random quantum states tunable from volume law to area law](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15300)
*Héloïse Albot,Sebastian Paeckel*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了σ-ensemble（σ-ensemble）——一种仅含单个控制参数的新型随机量子态族，能够通过调节参数在体积律（volume-law）和面积律（area-law）纠缠行为之间切换，从而克服了传统Haar随机态在经典模拟中的计算困难。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统基于Haar测度（Haar measure）采样的随机纯量子态存在纠缠特性上的根本限制，其体积律纠缠行为使得经典模拟变得不可行，且无法准确反映典型哈密顿量基态的特性。

Method: 通过在对连续子系统的本征值上施加概率分布来构建σ-ensemble的代表态，随后利用矩阵乘积态（matrix product state, MPS）形式重构出相容的全局量子态。

Result: 所提出的σ-ensemble能够通过单个控制参数在体积律和面积律纠缠行为之间进行调节，其面积律纠缠特性避免了Haar随机纯态在经典模拟中的计算不可行性。

Conclusion: σ-ensemble提供了一种更适用于量子系统经典模拟的随机态生成方法，相比传统Haar随机态更能代表典型哈密顿量基态的特性，解决了体积律纠缠带来的计算困难。

Abstract: A standard approach to generate random pure quantum states relies on sampling from the Haar measure. However, the entanglement properties of such states present a fundamental challenge for their general applicability. Here, we introduce the $σ$-ensembles $\unicode{x2013}$ a family of random quantum states with only a single control parameter. Crucially, these states are designed such that they can be tuned between volume-law and area-law behavior, which has been a major obstacle thus far. We construct representatives of this ensemble by imposing a probability distribution on the eigenvalues of the successive subsystems, and subsequently reconstructing a compatible global state using the matrix product state (MPS) formalism. Due to their area-law entanglement, our approach circumvents the intractability of Haar-random pure states in classical simulations of quantum systems and is more representative of typical Hamiltonian ground states.

Result: 积分扩散复杂度（integrated spread complexity）能够在不同遍历性区域提供精细分辨率，表明该方法能够从早期到晚期时间稳健地诊断量子混沌。

Conclusion: 提出的时间积分复杂度度量为诊断量子遍历性提供了一种稳健方法，能够跨越不同时间尺度有效识别量子混沌特征。

Abstract: A time-integrated measure of complexity is proposed for diagnosing the degree of quantum ergodicity. The scrambling dynamics of maximally entangled states within the ensemble of unitary evolutions are quantified by applying numerical bootstrapped realizations of an ensemble of Hamiltonians, probing different unitary paths. Using Rosenzweig-Porter ensembles, we show that the integrated spread complexity provides a fine-grained resolution across different ergodic regimes. This approach offers a robust method for diagnosing quantum chaos from early to late times.

### [159] [Operator Space Transport and the Emergence of Boundary Time Crystals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14291)
*Dominik Nemeth,Ahsan Nazir,Robert-Jan Slager,Alessandro Principi*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该研究开发了一个完全量子兼容的框架来分类集体自旋动力学，揭示了边界时间晶体（BTC）行为源于Liouvillian算符缺乏非平凡弱对称性，并通过算符空间中的不可约张量表示将Lindbladian动力学映射到非厄米跳跃问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 边界时间晶体（boundary time crystals, BTCs）是Lindbladian演化下集体自旋系统中连续时间晶体的重要范例，但迄今为止的分析主要依赖于半经典和数值方法，缺乏完全量子兼容的理论框架。

Method: 研究引入了算符空间的不可约张量表示（irreducible tensor representation），在该表示中Lindbladian动力学被映射到非厄米跳跃问题（non-Hermitian hopping problem），从而将动力学描述为算符权重在不同张量扇区间的输运。

Result: 该框架能够识别不同的动力学区域，包括集体进动（collective precession）、纯弛豫（pure relaxation）和BTC相，并揭示BTCs源于算符空间中的非互易输运（non-reciprocal transport），这种输运使Liouvillian本征模式在多个张量扇区中离域化。

Conclusion: 研究建立了算符空间输运作为理解耗散多体动力学的新视角，强调了与非厄米现象的联系，并为BTC振荡对初始条件不敏感性提供了微观机制解释。

Abstract: Boundary time crystals (BTCs) are prominent examples of continuous time crystals in collective spin systems governed by Lindbladian evolution. To date, their analysis has mostly relied on semiclassical and numerical approaches. Here, we develop a fully quantum-compatible framework to classify collective spin dynamics and show that BTC behavior emerges from the absence of non-trivial weak symmetries of the Liouvillian. To this end, we introduce an irreducible tensor representation of operator space, in which the Lindbladian dynamics maps onto a non-Hermitian hopping problem. Within this picture, the dynamics corresponds to the transport of operator weight across tensor sectors. This mapping allows an identification of distinct dynamical regimes, including collective precession, pure relaxation, and the BTC phase, within a single unified framework. We show that BTCs arise from non-reciprocal transport in operator space, which delocalizes Liouvillian eigenmodes across multiple tensor sectors. This non-reciprocal transport provides a microscopic mechanism for the insensitivity to initial conditions of BTC oscillations. More broadly, our results establish operator space transport as a perspective for understanding dissipative many-body dynamics and highlights connections to non-Hermitian phenomena.

### [160] [Revealing the physical structure of the general quantum master equation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14382)
*Eugenia Pyurbeeva,Ronnie Kosloff*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该研究在不附加任何假设条件下探索Lindblad主方程的结构，提出量子动力学可分解为自由演化、广义电荷交换和纯退相干三个基本物理过程，为量子主方程提供了新的物理视角。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统研究通常对开放量子系统中的Lindblad主方程施加弱耦合或能量守恒等额外条件，本研究旨在探索无任何假设条件下该方程的基本结构，从而获得更普适的理解。

Method: 通过分析Lindblad主方程的数学结构，将一般量子动力学表达为三个基本物理过程的组合：自由演化、系统与热浴间的广义电荷交换（这些电荷不一定与哈密顿量对易）以及纯退相干。

Result: 研究证明强耦合、粒子交换和非阿贝尔效应具有相同的物理起源。此外，发现这三种情况下的广义吉布斯态都包含一个先前未被考虑的非对易项。

Conclusion: 该研究为量子主方程提供了基于物理过程分解的新视角，揭示了不同量子效应间的统一物理本质，并指出了广义吉布斯态中非对易项的重要性。

Abstract: The Lindblad (GKLS) master equation, which represents the mathematical form for the general evolution of a density matrix, is a versatile and widely-used tool in open quantum systems. In contrast with the typical approach of imposing additional conditions on the system, such as weak coupling or energy conservation, we explore the structure of the equation with no assumptions. We demonstrate that general quantum dynamics can be expressed through a combination of free evolution, exchanges of some physical quantities (generalised charges), not necessarily commuting with the Hamiltonian, between the system and the bath, and pure dephasing. This result comprises a novel perspective on quantum master equations, employing physical processes as elemental parts. We use it to explore the dynamics and stationary states of a two-level system and show that strong coupling, particle exchange, and non-Abelian effects all share the same physical origin. Moreover, we demonstrate that the generalised Gibbs state for all three cases contains a non-commutation term, which has not been previously considered.

### [161] [Spectroscopic measurement of the Casimir-Polder force in the intermediate regime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14721)
*K. Ton,G. Kestler,D. A. Steck,J. T. Barreiro*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该研究首次直接测量了锶原子与介电表面在中间距离区域（约189纳米）的卡西米尔-波尔德力，通过原子能级位移的光谱探测，验证了量子电动力学理论计算，排除了短程和长程近似。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 卡西米尔-波尔德效应（Casimir-Polder effect）作为量子真空涨落的直接体现，在中间距离区域（原子-表面间距与原子主导跃迁波长相当）的实验观测一直依赖间接方法。本研究旨在通过直接测量原子能级位移来揭示这一关键区域的CP力。

Method: 采用光谱探测方法，测量超冷锶原子在魔幻波长（magic-wavelength）光学晶格中，距离介电表面189(2)纳米时的kHz频率位移。该距离尺度与原子主导的461纳米跃迁波长相当，属于中间距离区域。

Result: 测量结果显示kHz量级的CP诱导频率位移，与量子电动力学（QED）理论计算高度吻合，同时排除了短程近似（z⁻³标度）和长程近似（z⁻⁴标度）的预测。实验数据明确支持中间距离区域的精确理论描述。

Conclusion: 该研究首次实现了中间距离区域CP力的直接测量，为研究不同表面性质和几何构型下的CP效应奠定了基础，同时为探索原子-表面势的张量性质提供了途径，这对开发混合原子光学-磁量子器件具有重要意义。

Abstract: The Casimir-Polder (CP) effect -- the force between a neutral atom and an uncharged conducting plate in empty space -- is an intriguing consequence of quantum vacuum fluctuations. The typically attractive CP potential crosses over from a scaling of $z^{-3}$ at short separations to $z^{-4}$ at long distances, where retardation effects due to the finite speed of light become important. At intermediate distances, where the atom--surface separation is of the order of the wavelength of the dominant atomic transition, experiments have so far relied on indirect methods, such as diffraction or quantum reflection, to observe the CP effect. Here, we directly reveal the CP force between strontium atoms and a dielectric surface via the induced shifts in the atomic energy levels in the intermediate regime. We spectroscopically probe the CP-induced kHz-frequency shift of ultracold atoms confined by a magic-wavelength optical lattice at 189(2)~nm from the surface -- on the scale of the dominant 461-nm transition. Our measurements agree well with QED calculations and differ from the short-range approximation, while excluding the long-distance one. This paves the way for studying the CP effect across various surface properties and geometries, as well as exploring the tensor nature of the atom-surface potential -- all important for the development of hybrid atomic optical-magnetic quantum devices.

</details>

Method: 本文发展了基于量子准概率动力学（quantum quasiprobability dynamics）的实时瞬子方法（real-time instanton approach），该方法能够在大自旋极限下捕捉系统的稳态行为，并描述弛豫速率的渐近标度。

Conclusion: 本文发展的实时瞬子方法为集体自旋系统的相变和弛豫动力学提供了更准确的理论描述，揭示了传统半经典方法的局限性，特别强调了非高斯涨落在系统动力学中的关键作用。

Abstract: Collective spin systems -- spin ensembles coupled to a common reservoir and effectively described by a single macrospin -- play an important role in both atomic and solid-state physics. Their intrinsic nonlinearity gives rise to multiple long-lived metastable states that ultimately relax to a unique most probable state. This dominant state can change with a control parameter, leading to first-order phase transitions. We develop a real-time instanton approach based on quantum quasiprobability dynamics that captures the stationary state in the large-spin limit and the asymptotic scaling of relaxation rates. We further show that these features are not accurately described by the previously applied semiclassical Wigner approach due to its neglect of non-Gaussian fluctuations.

### [164] [Assembling Extensive Quantum Fisher Information in Stabilizer Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15268)
*Arnau Lira-Solanilla,Sreemayee Aditya,Xhek Turkeshi,Silvia Pappalardi*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种系统框架，用于在稳定子码（stabilizer codes）中构建具有扩展量子费舍尔信息（quantum Fisher information）密度的非局域可观测量。通过将稳定子生成元映射到对偶伊辛自旋（dual Ising spins），将隐藏的非局域序转化为可用于计量学的可观测量，并在监测簇码（monitored cluster codes）和环面码（toric code）中识别了量子费舍尔信息标度从扩展区到密集区的转变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究的动机在于开发一种系统方法，将稳定子码中隐藏的非局域序（hidden nonlocal order）转化为计量学上可访问的可观测量。这旨在揭示量子多体系统中非局域关联与计量学资源之间的深层联系。

Method: 方法的核心是构建一个系统框架，将稳定子生成元（stabilizer generators）映射到对偶伊辛自旋（dual Ising spins），使得这些自旋的关联函数等于弦序参量（string order parameters）。这种映射将隐藏的非局域序转化为具有扩展量子费舍尔信息密度的可观测量。

Result: 将该框架应用于监测簇码（monitored cluster codes）和环面码（toric code）时，研究识别了量子费舍尔信息标度（QFI scaling）的转变：从长程弦序（long-range string order）占主导的扩展区（extensive regime），转变到由竞争性单点测量（competing single-site measurements）驱动的密集区（intensive one）。

Conclusion: 该研究成功建立了稳定子码中非局域序与计量学资源之间的系统联系，通过将隐藏的弦序参量转化为可测量的量子费舍尔信息，揭示了量子多体系统中计量学相变（metrological phase transitions）的新机制。

Abstract: We introduce a systematic framework to construct nonlocal observables with extensive quantum Fisher information (QFI) density in stabilizer codes. The construction maps stabilizer generators to dual Ising spins whose correlators equal string order parameters, converting hidden nonlocal order into a metrologically accessible observable. Applying this to monitored cluster codes and the toric code, we identify transitions in the QFI scaling from an extensive regime, where long-range string order prevails, to an intensive one driven by competing single-site measurements.

### [165] [Deeper analysis of Fermi-LAT unassociated 4FGL J2112.5-3043 for possible identification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14794)

Method: 研究对4FGL J2112.5-3043进行了详细的光谱和空间分析，使用亚指数截断幂律谱模型（subexponential cutoff power-law spectral model）描述其光子谱，并评估了其时间变异性（flux variability）和形态特征。

Abstract: In the 4FGL-DR4 point-source catalog of the Large Area Telescope (LAT) onboard NASA's Fermi Gamma-ray Observatory (Fermi-LAT), around a third of the sources are still unidentified (unIDs). In this work, we perform a detailed study of one of them, namely 4FGL J2112.5-3043. Only gamma-ray emission has been detected from this unidentified source, with no counterpart observed at any other wavelength as of today. Together with its high detection significance, this makes 4FGL J2112.5-3043 a particularly compelling target for further investigation. The results of our spectral and spatial analyses show that the source photon spectrum is better described with a subexponential cutoff power-law spectral model, with no significant flux variability over time, and a morphology consistent with being a point-like source. We investigate and discuss the characterized emission within the context of both conventional and exotic astrophysics, namely a pulsar origin or potential dark matter (DM) annihilations in a nearby Galactic subhalo. Although our results are inconclusive and neither confirm a DM origin nor firmly establish an astrophysical nature, we find a spectral preference for the $b\bar{b}$ and $c\bar{c}$ DM annihilation channels over a pulsar origin, thus making this unID a particularly intriguing candidate for next multiwavelength observations.

*Henrique Gieg,Ramon Jaeger,Maximiliano Ujevic,Tim Dietrich*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探究μ子和μ子弱反应对中子星并合过程可能产生的影响，特别是对核合成产物和电磁对应体的影响程度，以验证先前文献中可能高估的效应。

Method: 采用数值相对论模拟方法，结合两种基线重子物态方程（baryonic equations-of-state）。使用灰色（能量无关）截断矩方案（gray truncated moments scheme）和隐式-显式时间积分器（implicit-explicit time integrator）处理中微子。采用全运动学方法（full kinematics approach）计算相关反应的新中微子速率，并通过反应核计算不透明度来模拟对过程（pair-processes）。

Result: 研究发现物质与辐射之间的平衡通过新颖的双时间尺度方法（two timescales approach）成功捕获。μ子和非μ子模拟结果在遗迹演化、吸积盘和外流性质方面基本一致。平均电子分数（electron fractions）、渐近速度和温度差异小于约6%，而μ子的主要影响是使抛射物质量最多减少约17%。

Conclusion: 基于研究结果，考虑μ子和μ子弱反应的存在对核合成产物（nucleosynthetic yields）和电磁对应体（electromagnetic counterparts）的影响可能比先前文献报道的要轻微得多。

Abstract: We present a set of numerical-relativity binary neutron star merger simulations incorporating muons and muonic reactions for two baseline baryonic equations-of-state. In order to investigate the possible impact of muons and muonic weak reactions, we treat neutrinos with a gray (energy-independent) truncated moments scheme and an implicit-explicit time integrator. Newly computed neutrino rates are employed within the full kinematics approach for a set of relevant reactions, and pair-processes are modeled via opacities computed using reaction kernels, that allow a consistent treatment of neutrino interaction rates. We find that equilibration between matter and radiation is successfully captured by a novel two timescales approach. Of astrophysical interest is the general agreement between our muonic and non-muonic results regarding the remnant evolution, disk and outflow properties. Average electron fractions, asymptotic velocities and temperatures are different by less than $\sim 6\%$, while the main impact of muons is a reduction in ejecta masses by at most $\sim 17\%$. Therefore, based on our findings, accounting for the presence of muons and muonic reactions might result much less severe consequences regarding nucleosynthetic yields and electromagnetic counterparts than previously reported in the literature.

</details>


### [167] [The azimuthal structure of magnetically arrested disks during flux eruption events](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14313)
*Argyrios Loules,Antonios Nathanail,Ioannis Contopoulos*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 该研究通过分析三维广义相对论磁流体动力学（GRMHD）模拟数据，发现磁通量喷发事件期间黑洞附近吸积盘的非轴对称特征显著增强，主要由低方位角模数（m=1,2）主导，揭示了垂直磁通量束的形成和运动是决定黑洞附近吸积流形态的关键机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在通过分析三维广义相对论磁流体动力学（general-relativistic magnetohydrodynamics, GRMHD）模拟数据，详细探究吸积物质的方位角结构细节及其演化过程，特别是在磁通量喷发（flux eruption）事件期间黑洞附近吸积盘的非轴对称特征增强现象。

Method: 研究采用标准三维GRMHD模拟数据，聚焦于赤道切片（equatorial slices）进行分析，以详细考察吸积物质的方位角结构。通过分析赤道吸积盘的方位角结构，识别主导的方位角模数（azimuthal mode numbers）。

Result: 研究发现磁通量喷发事件期间，赤道内吸积盘的非轴对称特征显著增强，特别是在黑洞附近区域。黑洞视界附近的物质分布主要由低方位角模数主导，特别是m=2和m=1模，表明非轴对称性的增强源于赤道面上大角度尺度特征的出现。黑洞附近吸积流的形态主要由垂直磁通量束（vertical magnetic flux bundles）的形成和运动决定。

Conclusion: 研究提供了磁化吸积盘（MADs）形态及其在磁通量喷发期间演化的详细定量描述，并阐明了过剩磁通量从黑洞脱离、垂直重构和排出的物理过程。初始水平磁场在低密度高磁化区域重新连接形成垂直配置，产生的垂直磁通管（vertical flux tubes）通过磁浮力（magnetic buoyancy）向外输运。

Abstract: We analyze data from a standard 3D general-relativistic magnetohydrodynamics (GRMHD) simulation, focusing on equatorial slices in order to examine the details and the evolution of the azimuthal structure of the accreting matter. During flux eruption events, the non-axisymmetric features of the equatorial inner accretion disk are considerably enhanced, with this enhancement being more prominent close to the black hole. Our analysis of the azimuthal structure of the equatorial accretion disk finds that the matter distribution in the vicinity of the horizon is dominated by low azimuthal mode numbers, specifically by the $m = 2$, and $m = 1$ modes, indicating that the non-axisymmetry of the disk during flux eruption events is enhanced due to the emergence of features with a large angular size on the equatorial plane. Our results suggest that the morphology of the equatorial accretion flow close to the black hole is mainly determined by the formation and motion of vertical magnetic flux bundles. These bundles are formed when the initially horizontal magnetic field reconnects into a vertical configuration, effectively detaching from the black hole horizon. This reconnection occurs in a low-density, highly magnetized region on the equatorial plane that expands over time as more field lines undergo vertical reconfiguration. The resulting vertical flux tubes, filled with low-density plasma, are then transported outwards due to magnetic buoyancy. Our results present a detailed quantitative description of the morphology of MADs and of its evolution during flux eruptions, complemented by a description of the physical process by which excess magnetic flux is detached from the black hole, vertically reconfigured, and expelled.

</details>

### [168] [On the existence of toric ALE and ALF gravitational instantons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15159)
*Hari K. Kunduri,James Lucietti*

Main category: math.DG

TL;DR: 该论文证明了渐近局部欧几里得（ALE）和渐近局部平坦（ALF）引力瞬子的存在性与唯一性，特别建立了每个容许杆结构对应唯一Ricci平坦的环面ALE/ALF引力瞬子，并给出了环面自对偶瞬子必为多Eguchi-Hanson或多Taub-NUT解的基本证明。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于建立渐近局部欧几里得（asymptotically locally Euclidean, ALE）和渐近局部平坦（asymptotically locally flat, ALF）引力瞬子的严格数学理论，特别是针对环面对称性的情形，以完善这类特殊几何结构的分类与存在性理论。

Method: 研究方法采用数学分析工具，通过建立存在性与唯一性定理，并针对每个容许杆结构（admissible rod structure）构造相应的解。同时，论文提供了环面ALE或ALF自对偶瞬子（self-dual instanton）分类的基本证明方法。

Result: 主要结果包括：1）证明了每个容许杆结构对应存在唯一Ricci平坦的环面ALE和ALF引力瞬子，除可能的锥形奇点外光滑；2）给出了基本证明，表明任何环面ALE或ALF自对偶瞬子必为多Eguchi-Hanson或多Taub-NUT解。

Conclusion: 论文结论确立了ALE和ALF引力瞬子理论的严格数学基础，完成了环面对称情形下这类几何结构的完全分类，并揭示了自对偶瞬子与已知经典解（Eguchi-Hanson和Taub-NUT）之间的本质联系。

Abstract: We establish existence and uniqueness results for asymptotically locally Euclidean (ALE) and asymptotically locally flat (ALF) gravitational instantons. In particular, we prove the existence of a unique, Ricci-flat, toric ALE and ALF gravitational instanton, for every admissible rod structure, that is smooth up to possible conical singularites. We also give an elementary proof that any toric ALE or ALF self-dual instanton is a multi-Eguchi-Hanson or multi-Taub-NUT solution.

### [169] [Complete noncompact G2-manifolds with ALC asymptotics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14704)
*Lorenzo Foscolo,Mark Haskins,Johannes Nordström*

Main category: math.DG

TL;DR: 本文证明了7维G2-全纯（G2-holonomy）度量在ALC（渐近局部锥形）渐近条件下的存在性、唯一性和结构结果，建立了G2-几何中与4维超Kähler几何中ALF引力瞬子（gravitational instantons）的类比，并发展了适用于一般ALC空间的Fredholm理论。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于建立7维G2-全纯（G2-holonomy）度量与4维超Kähler（hyperkähler）几何中ALF引力瞬子（gravitational instantons）的类比关系。具体目标是证明具有ALC（asymptotically locally conical）渐近条件的非紧致7维G2-全纯度量的存在性、唯一性和结构性质。

Method: 核心方法是发展适用于ALC空间的稳健Fredholm理论，用于处理自然几何线性椭圆算子（elliptic operators）。该方法不依赖于任何全纯约化（holonomy reduction）或曲率条件，适用于任意具有ALC渐近条件的黎曼流形（Riemannian manifolds）。

Result: 主要结果包括：证明了G2-几何中Atiyah-Hitchin度量的类比存在性；建立了ALC G2-全纯度量的良好模理论（moduli theory）；获得了基于渐近模型对称性的ALC G2-度量的刚性结果（rigidity results）。同时，该Fredholm理论还应用于证明一般ALC空间上的Hodge理论结果。

Conclusion: 本文成功建立了7维G2-全纯度量与4维超Kähler几何中ALF引力瞬子的完整类比框架，发展了适用于一般ALC空间的Fredholm分析工具，为特殊全纯度量（special holonomy metrics）的研究提供了新的理论基础和分析方法。

Abstract: We prove existence, uniqueness and structure results for complete noncompact 7-dimensional G2-holonomy metrics with ALC (asymptotically locally conical) asymptotics. We regard such spaces as G2-analogues of ALF gravitational instantons in 4-dimensional hyperkähler geometry. Our main results include the existence of a G2-analogue of the Atiyah-Hitchin metric in 4-dimensional hyperkähler geometry, the existence of a good moduli theory for ALC G2-holonomy metrics and rigidity results for ALC G2-metrics in terms of the symmetries of their asymptotic model.
  The analytic toolkit needed to prove all these results is a robust Fredholm theory for the natural geometric linear elliptic operators on ALC spaces. We provide a self-contained derivation of this Fredholm theory for arbitrary Riemannian manifolds with ALC asymptotics. Since our ALC Fredholm theory does not rely on imposing any holonomy reduction or curvature conditions it may also be of utility beyond the setting of ALC special holonomy metrics. As one such application of our general Fredholm theory we prove some Hodge-theoretic results on general ALC spaces.

Method: 建立具有均匀进动磁化的弹道N/F/S和S/F/S结理论框架，推导安德烈夫束缚态的非平衡分布，分析电流-相位关系，并分别处理部分极化和完全极化铁磁体的情况。

Conclusion: 均匀进动磁化能有效调控弹道超导结的输运特性，特别是在完全极化铁磁体中实现开关效应，为基于磁化动力学的超导器件设计提供了理论依据。

Abstract: We present a theory of ballistic N/F/S and S/F/S junctions with a uniformly precessing magnetization, which generates long-range equal-spin superconducting correlations [Takahashi et al., Phys. Rev. Lett. 99, 057003 (2007), Houzet, Phys. Rev. Lett. 101, 057009 (2008)]. The non-equilibrium distribution of Andreev bound states leads to a strongly non-sinusoidal current-phase relationship for large precession angles. We derive detailed results for ballistic junctions involving partially and fully polarized ferromagnets. In the fully polarized half-metal limit, the magnetization precession switches the junction from an "off" state with vanishing subgap current to an "on" state with finite Andreev conductance and finite Josephson current.

### [171] [Josephson phase shift and diode effect due to the inverse spin Hall effect](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14521)
*Gen Tatara,Yositake Takane,Aurelien Manchon*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该理论研究在空间反演对称性不变的超导体-正常金属-超导体结中，由自旋轨道相互作用引起的直接和逆自旋霍尔效应。发现超电流能诱导自旋霍尔效应产生边缘自旋积累，而空间不均匀静磁场通过反常相移导致二极管效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究在保持空间反演对称性的超导结构中自旋轨道相互作用对自旋霍尔效应的影响，探索不同于Rashba系统的物理机制，该机制不需要破坏结构反演对称性。

Method: 采用理论分析方法研究超导体-正常金属-超导体结（superconductor-normal metal-superconductor junction），考虑空间反演不变的（invariant under spatial inversion）自旋轨道相互作用，分析直接自旋霍尔效应和逆自旋霍尔效应。

Result: 超电流（supercurrent）诱导产生直接自旋霍尔效应，导致两个边缘出现相反极化的静态自旋积累（static spin accumulation）。对于逆效应，空间不均匀静态磁场（spatially inhomogeneous static magnetic field）诱导反常相移（anomalous phase shift），在高次谐波存在时产生二极管效应（diode effect）。

Conclusion: 该研究揭示了在空间反演对称性不变的自旋轨道相互作用系统中，超导结构能够产生自旋霍尔效应和二极管效应，这一机制与需要破坏结构反演对称性的Rashba系统有本质区别。

Abstract: We theoretically study the direct and inverse spin Hall effects in a superconductor-normal metal-superconductor junction induced by a spin-orbit interaction that is invariant under spatial inversion. We show that a supercurrent induces a spin Hall effect, leading to a static spin accumulation with opposite polarizations at the two edges, analogous to that in normal conductors. For the inverse effect, we consider a spatially inhomogeneous static magnetic field and show that it induces an anomalous phase shift, which, in the presence of higher harmonics, results in a diode effect. Unlike Rashba systems, the present mechanism does not require broken structural inversion symmetry.

</details>


### [172] [Effect of Rashba spin-orbit coupling on Faraday rotation in an extended Haldane model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14665)
*Yuan Fang,Yixiang Wang,Xiaopu Zhang*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究系统探讨了Rashba自旋轨道耦合（SOC）对扩展Haldane模型中法拉第旋转（FR）光谱的影响，发现Rashba SOC可显著增强FR效应并调控其光谱特性，为基于拓扑材料的磁光器件设计提供了新思路。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 利用拓扑材料的法拉第旋转（Faraday rotation, FR）特性为新型磁光器件开发提供了有前景的途径。研究旨在系统探索Rashba自旋轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling, SOC）对FR光谱的影响，以优化磁光器件性能。

Method: 采用扩展Haldane模型，将Rashba SOC和交换劈裂（exchange splitting）整合到原始无自旋Haldane框架中。基于Kubo形式（Kubo formalism）计算了FR光谱，并推导了展开至二次项的低能有效哈密顿量（low-energy effective Hamiltonian），与紧束缚模型（tight-binding model）计算结果进行了对比验证。

Result: 在陈数（Chern number）C=2区域，无交换劈裂时FR角可超过4°，且峰值位置可通过Rashba SOC调控。加入交换劈裂后，在宽频率范围内出现近乎平坦的FR谱线，FR峰值随Rashba SOC强度单调增加。Rashba SOC开启了额外的跃迁通道，其净贡献对FR峰值产生建设性增强。低能有效哈密顿量计算结果与紧束缚模型吻合良好。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明，通过Rashba SOC工程可以设计和优化磁光器件特性。Rashba SOC不仅增强了FR效应，还提供了调控FR光谱特性的有效手段，为拓扑材料在磁光器件中的应用提供了理论指导。

Abstract: Utilization of Faraday rotation (FR) properties of topological materials offers a promising route toward novel magneto-optical devices. We systematically investigated the effect of Rashba spin-orbit coupling (SOC) on FR spectra in an extended Haldane model, which incorporates Rashba SOC and exchange splitting into the original spinless Haldane framework. Using the Kubo formalism, we calculated the FR spectra across the model's rich topological phase diagram. We found that in the Chern number C=2 region, in the absence of exchange splitting, the FR angle can exceed 4$^\circ$ and its peak position is tunable by the Rashba SOC. In contrast, with the inclusion of exchange splitting, a nearly flat FR profile emerges over a broad frequency range, and the FR peak values increase monotonically with the Rashba SOC strength. The Rashba SOC opens additional transition channels, whose net contribution constructively enhances the FR peak. Furthermore, we derived a low-energy effective Hamiltonian expanded up to quadratic terms, the results of which are in good agreement with tight-binding model calculations, thereby validating our numerical results. Our findings suggest that magneto-optical device characteristics can be designed and optimized through Rashba SOC engineering.

</details>


### [173] [Orbitals of Artificial Atoms in a Gapped Two-Dimensional Vacuum](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14737)
*Mong-Wen Gu,Aizhan Sabitova,Taner Esat,Christian Wagner,F. Stefan Tautz,Aleksandr Rodin,Ruslan Temirov*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究利用扫描隧道显微镜（scanning tunnelling microscopy）可视化二维分子薄膜中纳米结构的束缚态，发现人工原子（artificial atoms）不仅模拟自然原子的s和p轨道行为，还能产生由二维带隙真空环境塑造的新型准一维局域态，扩展了化学的轨道词汇。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 纳米技术进步使得能够创建模拟真实原子电子态的人工原子（artificial atoms），理解这些人工原子的相互作用和成键机制对于设计具有定制电子特性的新材料至关重要。

Method: 研究采用扫描隧道显微镜（scanning tunnelling microscopy）可视化在具有抛物线能带和多个部分能隙的二维分子薄膜中图案化纳米结构的束缚态。

Result: 最低能态从能带底部分离，类似于自然原子的s和p轨道，并以相同方式成键；更重要的是，人工原子所处的带隙二维真空环境产生了在真实原子中不存在对应物的全新轨道，这些准一维局域态丰富了化学的轨道词汇。

Conclusion: 人工原子不仅能够模拟自然原子的轨道行为，其所在的二维带隙真空环境还能产生全新类别的轨道，这些主要由周围电子真空塑造的准一维局域态为化学提供了新的轨道类型。

Abstract: Advances in nanotechnology now allow the creation of artificial atoms - engineered structures whose electronic states closely mimic those of real atoms. Understanding how these artificial atoms interact and bond is key to designing new materials with tailored electronic properties. Here, we use scanning tunnelling microscopy to visualise the bound states of nanostructures patterned in a two-dimensional molecular film featuring a parabolic band with multiple partial energy gaps. The lowest-energy states split off from the bottom of the band and resemble the familiar $s$ and $p$ orbitals of natural atoms, even bonding in the same way. Yet, artificial atoms go beyond this analogy: the gapped two-dimensional vacuum in which they reside gives rise to entirely new orbitals with no counterparts in real atoms. These quasi-one-dimensional localised states enrich the orbital vocabulary of chemistry, adding a new class of orbitals that are predominantly shaped by the surrounding electronic vacuum.

### [174] [Thermal conductivity tuning of scalable nanopatterned silicon membranes measured with a three-probe method](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14770)

TL;DR: 本研究展示了纳米图案化硅膜中热导率的显著可控降低，采用嵌段共聚物自组装方法制备了63纳米间距、35纳米孔径的纳米孔硅膜，并开发了改进的三探针技术进行热导率测量，实现了室温下热导率五倍降低至7.3 W/m.K。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 声子硅结构（phononic silicon structures）作为可集成、可扩展的纳米系统在调控热输运方面具有潜力，但其广泛应用受限于复杂的制备工艺。同时，悬浮纳米结构薄膜的热学性质表征面临挑战，热接触电阻（thermal contact resistances）常影响测量精度。

Method: 采用嵌段共聚物自组装（block copolymer self-assembly）方法制备纳米孔硅膜，孔径35纳米，间距63纳米。开发了改进的三探针技术（three-probe technique），能够对复杂薄膜系统进行稳健、定量、空间分辨的热导率测量，并考虑热接触伪影（thermal contact artifacts）。

Result: 在30-350 K温度范围内对未图案化的40纳米厚硅薄膜进行测量验证，室温热导率为46.5 W/m.K。纳米孔的受控刻蚀（controlled etching）在整个研究温度范围内有效调控热输运，孔刻蚀深度控制成为声子硅中的有效参数。完全刻穿膜在室温下实现热导率五倍降低，达到7.3 W/m.K。

Conclusion: 纳米孔刻蚀深度控制是调控声子硅热输运的有效参数，结合嵌段共聚物自组装制备方法和改进的三探针测量技术，实现了热导率的显著可控降低，为热管理应用提供了有力工具。

Abstract: Phononic silicon structures have emerged as an integrable and scalable nanosystem for tailoring thermal transport. However, their widespread adoption has been limited by their complex fabrication pathways. Alongside, the reliable characterization of thermal properties in suspended nanostructured films remains challenging, as thermal contact resistances often hinder the accuracy of measurements.
  In this work, we demonstrate a clear and controllable reduction of thermal conductivity in nanopatterned silicon membranes. A block copolymer self-assembly approach is employed to fabricate nanoholed silicon films with a pitch of 63 nm and hole diameters of 35 nm. Additionally, we introduce an extension of the three-probe technique that enables robust, quantitative, and spatially resolved thermal conductivity measurements in complex thin-film systems, accounting for thermal contact artifacts.
  The method is validated through measurements on unpatterned 40 nm-thick silicon thin films between 30 and 350 K, yielding a room-temperature thermal conductivity of 46.5 W/m.K. Finally, we further show that controlled etching of the nanoholes provides a powerful means to tune thermal transport in the overall studied temperature range, establishing hole etch depth control as an effective parameter in phononic silicon. Specifically, a fivefold reduction in thermal conductivity is achieved, reaching 7.3 W/m.K for fully etched-through membranes at room temperature.

</details>

Method: 本研究形式化重构了泊松-玻尔兹曼理论（Poisson-Boltzmann theory），在参数空间中揭示了不同的电场双层（EDL）区域。基于区域分类，建立了一个可调谐纳米流体输运的形式化框架。

Result: 该框架重现了观察到的电导率-浓度标度行为，合理解释了具有可重构极性的离子晶体管，并预测了静电调制的两个基本热力学极限（60 mV/dec 和 120 mV/dec）。

Conclusion: 该框架具有准确性、普适性和可扩展性，能够解释受限空间中广泛的离子输运现象，为纳米流体器件的设计和优化提供了理论基础。

Abstract: Nanofluidic devices prompts unconventional ion transports appealing to energy and information technologies, thanks to the susceptibility of confined electric double layers (EDL) to various external physical fields. Although experimental studies advance rapidly, the rationalization of field-tunable nanofluidic transports has not reached a formalized and unified level. Here we formally reformulate the Poisson-Boltzmann theory and reveal distinct EDL regimes on the parameter space. Based on the regime classification, we establish a formal framework for the tunable nanofluidic transport, which reproduces the observed conductivity-concentration scaling behaviors, rationalizes the ionic transistors with reconfigurable polarities, and predicts two fundamental thermodynamic limits for electrostatic modulation (60 mV/dec and 120 mV/dec). Being accurate, generalizable and extensible, this framework can account for a wide range of ion transports in confined spaces.

Abstract: While significant advancements have been made in weak magnetic field detection, conventional high-sensitivity techniques are often limited by requirements for cryogenic operation or bulky setups. In this work, we develop a sensitive alternating magnetic field sensor based on a coupled system of an active microwave cavity and yttrium iron garnet (YIG), with the components implemented on printed circuit boards (PCBs). By introducing electrically tunable gain to compensate for cavity losses, we substantially improve both the quality factor and the signal intensity. Under the coupled system, Floquet modulation is induced by the alternating magnetic field, allowing for weak field detection by driving a specific hybrid mode and measuring the resulting Floquet sidebands. This miniaturized device operates at room temperature, achieving a detection limit of 121 pT/\sqrt{Hz}.

### [177] [Layer-dependent quantum transport in KV2Se2O-based altermagnetic tunnel junctions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14817)
*Yue Zhao,Bin Xiao,Jiawei Liu,Hui Zeng,Jun Zhao*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究基于新型反铁磁金属候选材料KV₂Se₂O设计了反铁磁隧道结（AMTJ），通过第一性原理计算揭示了界面层数奇偶性对量子输运的调控机制，预测了高达4.6×10⁷%的巨大隧穿磁阻效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统磁性隧道结（MTJ）的持续微型化受到杂散磁场的限制。反铁磁体（altermagnets）结合了铁磁体和反铁磁体的优势，为制造具有巨自旋分裂、高本征频率和无杂散场等奇异特性的多功能隧道结提供了有前景的替代方案。

Method: 基于近期报道的反铁磁金属候选材料KV₂Se₂O，设计了KV₂Se₂O/SrTiO₃/KV₂Se₂O结构的反铁磁隧道结（AMTJ）。采用密度泛函理论（density functional theory）结合非平衡格林函数（non-equilibrium Green's function）方法，研究了该器件的层数依赖量子输运特性和隧穿磁阻（tunneling magnetoresistance）。

Result: 计算结果表明，AMTJ器件的透射率随SrTiO₃半导体层数呈现显著振荡行为，这归因于层数奇偶性决定的界面构型。奇数层器件中，富电子的O-Se界面具有平滑的有效势能，允许横向动量（k||）输运通道，从而增强透射；而偶数层器件中，Ti-Se界面呈现更陡峭的有效势能，阻碍了横向动量通道的量子输运。预测使用4层SrTiO₃可实现高达4.6×10⁷%的巨大隧穿磁阻。

Conclusion: 该研究不仅提供了与AMTJ中量子输运相关的物理理解，还揭示了势垒界面工程是调控磁电性能的有效策略。反铁磁隧道结的设计为开发高性能自旋电子器件开辟了新途径。

Abstract: Magnetic tunnel junction (MTJ) is the key component to enable information access and increasing number of MTJs is integrated to develop high-density spintronic devices. However, continuous miniaturization of the conventional MTJs is hindered by stray magnetic fields. Altermagnets, combining the advantages of both ferromagnets and antiferromagnets, provide a promising alternative to fabricate versatile MTJs with exotic properties, such as giant spin splitting, high intrinsic frequency, and absence of stray fields. Inspired by the altermagnetic metal candidate KV2Se2O reported recently, we design an altermagnetic tunnel junction (AMTJ) based on KV2Se2O/SrTiO3/KV2Se2O. Using density functional theory combined with non-equilibrium Green's function, we investigate the layer-dependent quantum transport properties and the tunneling magnetoresistance (TMR) of such AMTJ device. Our calculated results reveal that the transmission of the AMTJ device exhibits a pronounced oscillation behavior dependent on the number of layers of the SrTiO3 semiconductor, which is attributed to the interface configuration determined by parity of the layer number. In odd-layer devices, the electron-rich O-Se interface exhibits a smooth effective potential and enables transverse momentum (k||) transport channels, leading to enhanced transmission. In contrast, in even-layer devices, the Ti-Se interface presents a steeper effective potential, impeding quantum transport through transverse momentum (k||) channels. A giant TMR of 4.6*10^7% is predicted to be realized by using a 4-layer SrTiO3. Our findings not only provide physical understanding relevant to the quantum transport in AMTJs, but also unveil that the barrier interface engineering is a strategy to tune the magnetoelectric performance.

### [178] [Poor man's Majorana bound states in quantum dot based Kitaev chain coupled to a photonic cavity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15036)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子点平台为实现Kitaev链哈密顿量及其马约拉纳束缚态提供了有前景的途径。然而，传统方法需要精细调节系统参数至"甜点"才能实现"穷人版马约拉纳束缚态"。本研究旨在探索光子腔环境如何影响这一过程，并利用量子光工程化马约拉纳束缚态。

Method: 基于先前工作[Phys. Rev. B 111, 155410 (2025)]，研究者构建了基于量子点并嵌入光子腔的Kitaev链微观模型。通过分析光子耦合对系统的影响，推导出有效哈密顿量，并研究不同光子态下粒子相互作用的屏蔽机制。

Result: 研究发现光子耦合在微观模型中产生有效哈密顿量，其中腔场影响配对项。即使在光子耦合存在的情况下，仍可通过筛选粒子相互作用达到实现"穷人版马约拉纳束缚态"的甜点条件。具体而言，当腔处于零光子态时可抵消吸引相互作用，而单光子态可屏蔽排斥相互作用。此外，腔中存在大量光子时会抑制跳跃振幅，导致简并谱。

Conclusion: 该研究证明了利用量子光工程化"穷人版马约拉纳束缚态"的可行性，特别是通过光子腔嵌入技术。不同光子态提供了调节粒子相互作用的有效手段，为实现马约拉纳束缚态提供了新的调控维度。

Abstract: Quantum dot based platforms offer a promising route towards realizing the Kitaev chain Hamiltonian hosting Majorana bound states (MBSs). Poor man's MBSs arise in a two-site Kitaev chain when the parameters of the system are fine-tuned to the sweet spot. Based on our previous work [Phys. Rev. B 111, 155410 (2025)], we consider a microscopic model for the Kitaev chain based on quantum dots with proximity effect embedded in a photonic cavity. We find that the photon coupling in the microscopic model yields an effective Hamiltonian where the cavity affects the pairing term. However, we demonstrate that even in this case, it is possible to screen particle interactions and reach the sweet spot condition for the emergence of the poor man's MBSs. In particular, we find that attractive particle interactions can be canceled for the cavity prepared in the zero-photon state, while repulsive ones can be screened with a cavity prepared in the one-photon state. Furthermore, in case of a large number of photons in the cavity, we find that the hopping amplitudes are suppressed resulting in a degenerate spectrum. This motivates the use of quantum light for engineering poor man's MBSs with cavity embedding.

### [179] [Heat flux deflection induced by hydrodynamic electron transport in a homogeneous Corbino disk under magnetic field](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15062)
*Chuang Zhang,Meng Lian,Hong Liang,Xiaokang Li,Zhaoli Guo,JingTao Lü*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究通过电子玻尔兹曼输运方程（eBTE）耦合泊松方程，分析了均匀二维Corbino圆盘几何中电子流体动力学输运的热行为，揭示了在径向电场或温度梯度下出现热流偏转现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 过去十年间，流体动力学电子输运（hydrodynamic electron transport）受到广泛关注，但先前研究主要集中于电学性质。本研究旨在探索电子流体动力学输运中的热行为特性。

Method: 采用电子玻尔兹曼输运方程（electron Boltzmann transport equation, eBTE）耦合泊松方程，在垂直于圆盘平面的磁场下，研究均匀二维Corbino圆盘几何中的电子流体动力学输运。

Result: 在电子流体动力学区域（electron hydrodynamic regime）中，径向电场或温度梯度会导致热流偏转现象（heat flux deflection phenomenon），即热流不再仅沿径向流动，而是在半径的切向也存在热流。动量弛豫散射过程（momentum-relaxing scattering process）抑制该现象，而动量守恒散射过程（momentum-conserving scattering process）促进该现象。

Conclusion: 当分别施加同方向的电势梯度或温度梯度时，在电子流体动力学区域中热流方向会发生反转。这表明电子流体动力学输运中的热行为具有独特的偏转特性，受不同类型散射过程的调控。

Abstract: Hydrodynamic electron transport, namely, the electric behaviors in solid materials at the macroscopic level are similar to the fluid hydrodynamics when the momentum-conserving electron-electron scattering plays the leading role, has got much attention in the past ten years. However, most of previous studies mainly focus on the electric properties. In this work, the thermal behaviors of hydrodynamic electron transport in a homogeneous 2D Corbino disk geometry is studied by the electron Boltzmann transport equation (eBTE) coupled with the Poisson equation under the magnetic field perpendicular to disk plane. Results show that in the electron hydrodynamic regime, the heat flux deflection phenomenon appears under the radial electric field or temperature gradient, namely, the heat flux no longer flows only along the radial direction and there is heat flux in the tangential direction of the radius. Heat flux deflection phenomenon is suppressed by momentum-relaxing scattering process and promoted by momentum-conserving scattering process. When an electric potential gradient or temperature gradient in the same direction is applied separately, the direction of heat flux is reversed in the electron hydrodynamic regime.

### [180] [Hanbury Brown-Twiss interferometry at the $ν=2/5$ fractional quantum Hall edge](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15133)
*Ryotaro Sano,Fumihiro Murabayashi,Daigo Ichikawa,Thibaut Jonckheere,Jérôme Rech,Thierry Martin,Masayuki Hashisaka,Takeo Kato*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种用于ν=2/5分数量子霍尔边缘系统的Hanbury Brown-Twiss干涉仪，该装置基于准粒子在共传播边缘模式间的隧穿，通过双粒子干涉而非单粒子干涉来探测任意子统计特性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究主要关注任意子Fabry-Pérot和Mach-Zehnder干涉仪，这些装置依赖于单粒子干涉。本文旨在开发一种基于双粒子干涉的Hanbury Brown-Twiss干涉仪，为探测分数量子霍尔边缘系统的任意子统计特性提供新方法。

Method: 在弱隧穿区域，采用玻色化边缘理论（bosonized edge theory）结合Keldysh微扰理论（Keldysh perturbation theory）计算隧穿电流的交叉关联。通过分析大器件极限下的通量依赖噪声，获得解析表达式。

Result: 在大器件极限下，通量依赖噪声的结构与电子HBT干涉仪相似，但电子电荷被分数量子电荷e*=e/3取代，并具有分数量子边缘模式的特征标度维度。此时显式任意子交换相位抵消，但当器件尺寸与热长度相当时，交叉关联可能恢复对任意子统计角的显式依赖。

Conclusion: 提出的Hanbury Brown-Twiss干涉仪为研究ν=2/5分数量子霍尔边缘系统的任意子统计提供了基于双粒子干涉的新平台。大器件极限下噪声特性由分数量子电荷主导，而有限尺寸效应可能揭示任意子统计角的更显式依赖关系。

Abstract: We propose a Hanbury Brown-Twiss interferometer for a $ν=2/5$ fractional quantum Hall edge system, in which quasiparticles tunnel between two co-propagating edge modes. In contrast to the previously studied anyonic Fabry-Pérot and Mach-Zehnder interferometers, the proposed setup relies purely on two-particle interference rather than single-particle interference. In the weak-tunneling regime, we employ a bosonized edge theory together with Keldysh perturbation theory to evaluate the cross-correlation of the tunneling currents. In the large-device limit, we obtain an analytic expression for the flux-dependent noise, whose structure closely resembles that of an electronic HBT interferometer, but with the electron charge replaced by the fractional charge $e^{\star}=e/3$ and with scaling dimensions characteristic of the fractional edge modes. In this limit, the explicit anyonic exchange phases cancel, whereas when the device size becomes comparable to the thermal length, the cross-correlation may recover a more explicit dependence on the anyonic statistical angle.

### [181] [New frontiers in quantum science and technology using van der Waals Josephson junctions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15276)
*Joydip Sarkar,Ayshi Mukherjee,Amit Basu,Ritajit Kundu,Arijit Kundu,Mandar M. Deshmukh*

TL;DR: 本文综述了基于范德华（van der Waals）材料的约瑟夫森器件在过去十年的快速发展，重点介绍了其在探索新型物理现象和实现量子技术应用方面的独特优势。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过利用范德华晶体材料对器件对称性的基本新控制，实现了二维系统特有的哈密顿量。二维异质结构中多种激发的长弛豫时间为创建精密的量子传感器提供了可能性，其中二维材料本身可作为将激发传输到活性传感元件的高效总线。

Result: 范德华基超导电子学的创造性爆发正在快速增长，该综述重点介绍了由此产生的器件和物理。范德华约瑟夫森结与扭曲电子学（twistronics）和拓扑学的结合，有可能重新定义超导量子技术，实现从量子计算到超灵敏混合传感器的应用。

Conclusion: 尽管范德华约瑟夫森结机会众多，但必须克服可扩展性的挑战才能转化为实际器件。该综述综合了当前发展，并为研究人员在这一新兴领域导航提供了路线图。

Abstract: Over the last decade, the development of Josephson devices based on van der Waals (vdW) materials has advanced rapidly, representing a paradigm shift driven by the advent of 2D materials. The diverse vdW materials library, combined with advanced fabrication techniques, enables the integration of materials with vastly disparate properties for scientific exploration. The vdW Josephson junctions (JJs) offer a unique route to explore novel functionalities and associated physics that remain inaccessible in conventional JJs, which have reached an industrial level in terms of fabrication. Beyond material diversity, vdW crystalline materials offer fundamental new control over device symmetries, enabling the realization of Hamiltonians unique to 2D systems. Furthermore, the long relaxation times of myriad excitations in 2D heterostructures open possibilities for creating exquisite quantum sensors, with the 2D material itself acting as an efficient bus for transmitting excitations to the active sensing element. This creative explosion in vdW-based superconducting electronics is rapidly growing, and our review highlights the resulting devices and physics. The confluence of vdW JJs with twistronics and topology has the potential to redefine superconducting quantum technology, enabling applications from quantum computation to ultra-sensitive hybrid sensors. While opportunities abound with vdW JJs, the challenge of scalability must be surmounted for translation into real-world devices. This review synthesizes current developments and offers a roadmap for researchers navigating this burgeoning field.
